Authors: Shaswat Garg, Matin Moezzi, Brandon Da Silva

The Observer Effect in World Models: Invasive Adaptation Corrupts Latent Physics

Abstract (English): Determining whether neural models internalize physical laws as world models, rather than exploiting statistical shortcuts, remains challenging, especially under out-of-distribution (OOD) shifts. Standard evaluations often test latent capability via downstream adaptation (e.g., fine-tuning or high-capacity probes), but such interventions can change the representations being measured and thus confound what was learned during self-supervised learning (SSL). We propose a non-invasive evaluation protocol, PhyIP. We test whether physical quantities are linearly decodable from frozen representations, motivated by the linear representation hypothesis. Across fluid dynamics and orbital mechanics, we find that when SSL achieves low error, latent structure becomes linearly accessible. PhyIP recovers internal energy and Newtonian inverse-square scaling on OOD tests (e.g., $ρ> 0.90$). In contrast, adaptation-based evaluations can collapse this structure ($ρ\approx 0.05$). These findings suggest that adaptation-based evaluation can obscure latent structures and that low-capacity probes offer a more accurate evaluation of physical world models.

摘要（中文）: 确定神经模型是否将物理定律内化为世界模型，而非利用统计捷径，仍然具有挑战性，尤其是在分布外（OOD）偏移下。标准评估通常通过下游适应（例如，微调或高容量探针）来测试潜在能力，但这种干预会改变所测量的表示形式，从而混淆自监督学习（SSL）期间所学到的内容。我们提出了一种非侵入式评估协议，PhyIP。我们基于线性表示假说，测试物理量是否可以从冻结的表示中线性解码。在流体动力学和轨道力学中，我们发现当SSL达到低误差时，潜在结构变得线性可访问。在OOD测试中，PhyIP恢复了内能和牛顿平方反比定律缩放（例如，$ρ> 0.90$）。相比之下，基于适应的评估可能会使这种结构崩溃（$ρ\approx 0.05$）。这些发现表明，基于适应的评估可能会掩盖潜在结构，而低容量探针可以更准确地评估物理世界模型。

TLDR: The paper introduces PhyIP, a non-invasive evaluation protocol, to assess whether neural models internalize physical laws, finding that adaptation-based evaluations can obscure latent physical structures in world models, while low-capacity probes offer a more accurate evaluation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种非侵入式评估协议PhyIP，用于评估神经模型是否内化了物理定律。研究发现，基于调整的评估可能会掩盖世界模型中潜在的物理结构，而低容量探针则提供了更准确的评估。

Authors: Christian Internò, Jumpei Yamaguchi, Loren Amdahl-Culleton, Markus Olhofer, David Klindt, Barbara Hammer

Gaia2: Benchmarking LLM Agents on Dynamic and Asynchronous Environments

Abstract (English): We introduce Gaia2, a benchmark for evaluating large language model agents in realistic, asynchronous environments. Unlike prior static or synchronous evaluations, Gaia2 introduces scenarios where environments evolve independently of agent actions, requiring agents to operate under temporal constraints, adapt to noisy and dynamic events, resolve ambiguity, and collaborate with other agents. Each scenario is paired with a write-action verifier, enabling fine-grained, action-level evaluation and making Gaia2 directly usable for reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards. Our evaluation of state-of-the-art proprietary and open-source models shows that no model dominates across capabilities: GPT-5 (high) reaches the strongest overall score of 42% pass@1 but fails on time-sensitive tasks, Claude-4 Sonnet trades accuracy and speed for cost, Kimi-K2 leads among open-source models with 21% pass@1. These results highlight fundamental trade-offs between reasoning, efficiency, robustness, and expose challenges in closing the "sim2real" gap. Gaia2 is built on a consumer environment with the open-source Agents Research Environments platform and designed to be easy to extend. By releasing Gaia2 alongside the foundational ARE framework, we aim to provide the community with a flexible infrastructure for developing, benchmarking, and training the next generation of practical agent systems.

摘要（中文）: 我们引入Gaia2，一个用于评估大型语言模型智能体在真实、异步环境中的基准。不同于以往的静态或同步评估，Gaia2引入了环境独立于智能体行为演进的场景，要求智能体在时间约束下运行，适应嘈杂和动态事件，解决歧义，并与其他智能体协作。每个场景都配有一个写入行为验证器，支持细粒度的行为级别评估，并使Gaia2可以直接用于从可验证奖励中进行的强化学习。我们对最先进的专有和开源模型的评估表明，没有一个模型在各项能力上占据主导地位：GPT-5（高）获得了42%的pass@1最高总体评分，但在时间敏感型任务上表现不佳，Claude-4 Sonnet牺牲了准确性和速度来换取成本效益，Kimi-K2在开源模型中处于领先地位，pass@1为21%。这些结果突出了推理、效率、鲁棒性之间的根本权衡，并暴露了缩小“sim2real”差距的挑战。Gaia2建立在具有开源智能体研究环境平台的消费者环境中，并且被设计成易于扩展。通过发布Gaia2以及基础性的ARE框架，我们旨在为社区提供一个灵活的基础设施，用于开发、基准测试和训练下一代实用智能体系统。

TLDR: The paper introduces Gaia2, a new benchmark for evaluating LLM agents in dynamic, asynchronous environments, highlighting performance trade-offs between different models and open-sourcing the evaluation platform and scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Gaia2，一个用于评估LLM Agent在动态、异步环境下的新基准，突出了不同模型之间的性能权衡，并开源了评估平台和场景。

Authors: Romain Froger, Pierre Andrews, Matteo Bettini, Amar Budhiraja, Ricardo Silveira Cabral, Virginie Do, Emilien Garreau, Jean-Baptiste Gaya, Hugo Laurençon, Maxime Lecanu, Kunal Malkan, Dheeraj Mekala, Pierre Ménard, Gerard Moreno-Torres Bertran, Ulyana Piterbarg, Mikhail Plekhanov, Mathieu Rita, Andrey Rusakov, Vladislav Vorotilov, Mengjue Wang, Ian Yu, Amine Benhalloum, Grégoire Mialon, Thomas Scialom

DynaHOI: Benchmarking Hand-Object Interaction for Dynamic Target

Abstract (English): Most existing hand motion generation benchmarks for hand-object interaction (HOI) focus on static objects, leaving dynamic scenarios with moving targets and time-critical coordination largely untested. To address this gap, we introduce the DynaHOI-Gym, a unified online closed-loop platform with parameterized motion generators and rollout-based metrics for dynamic capture evaluation. Built on DynaHOI-Gym, we release DynaHOI-10M, a large-scale benchmark with 10M frames and 180K hand capture trajectories, whose target motions are organized into 8 major categories and 22 fine-grained subcategories. We also provide a simple observe-before-act baseline (ObAct) that integrates short-term observations with the current frame via spatiotemporal attention to predict actions, achieving an 8.1% improvement in location success rate.

摘要（中文）: 现有的大多数针对手-物体交互（HOI）的手部动作生成基准测试，主要关注静态物体，而对于具有移动目标和时间敏感协调的动态场景，则缺乏充分的测试。为了弥补这一空白，我们引入了DynaHOI-Gym，一个统一的在线闭环平台，具有参数化的运动生成器和基于rollout的指标，用于动态捕捉评估。基于DynaHOI-Gym，我们发布了DynaHOI-10M，一个大规模基准测试，包含1000万帧和18万条手部捕捉轨迹，其目标动作被组织成8个主要类别和22个细粒度子类别。我们还提供了一个简单的观察-再行动（ObAct）基线方法，该方法通过时空注意力将短期观察与当前帧相结合来预测动作，从而在位置成功率方面实现了8.1%的提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces DynaHOI, a new benchmark (DynaHOI-Gym and DynaHOI-10M) for hand-object interaction with dynamic objects, addressing the limitations of existing benchmarks that focus on static objects. It also provides a baseline model for performance evaluation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DynaHOI，一个新的用于手部-物体交互的基准测试 (DynaHOI-Gym 和 DynaHOI-10M)，该基准测试针对动态对象，解决了现有基准测试侧重于静态对象的局限性。 它还提供了一个基线模型用于性能评估。

Authors: BoCheng Hu, Zhonghan Zhao, Kaiyue Zhou, Hongwei Wang, Gaoang Wang

Talk2DM: Enabling Natural Language Querying and Commonsense Reasoning for Vehicle-Road-Cloud Integrated Dynamic Maps with Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Dynamic maps (DM) serve as the fundamental information infrastructure for vehicle-road-cloud (VRC) cooperative autonomous driving in China and Japan. By providing comprehensive traffic scene representations, DM overcome the limitations of standalone autonomous driving systems (ADS), such as physical occlusions. Although DM-enhanced ADS have been successfully deployed in real-world applications in Japan, existing DM systems still lack a natural-language-supported (NLS) human interface, which could substantially enhance human-DM interaction. To address this gap, this paper introduces VRCsim, a VRC cooperative perception (CP) simulation framework designed to generate streaming VRC-CP data. Based on VRCsim, we construct a question-answering data set, VRC-QA, focused on spatial querying and reasoning in mixed-traffic scenes. Building upon VRCsim and VRC-QA, we further propose Talk2DM, a plug-and-play module that extends VRC-DM systems with NLS querying and commonsense reasoning capabilities. Talk2DM is built upon a novel chain-of-prompt (CoP) mechanism that progressively integrates human-defined rules with the commonsense knowledge of large language models (LLMs). Experiments on VRC-QA show that Talk2DM can seamlessly switch across different LLMs while maintaining high NLS query accuracy, demonstrating strong generalization capability. Although larger models tend to achieve higher accuracy, they incur significant efficiency degradation. Our results reveal that Talk2DM, powered by Qwen3:8B, Gemma3:27B, and GPT-oss models, achieves over 93\% NLS query accuracy with an average response time of only 2-5 seconds, indicating strong practical potential.

摘要（中文）: 动态地图 (DM) 作为中日车路云 (VRC) 协同自动驾驶的基础信息设施。通过提供全面的交通场景表示，DM 克服了诸如物理遮挡等单机自动驾驶系统 (ADS) 的局限性。尽管 DM 增强型 ADS 已在日本的实际应用中成功部署，但现有的 DM 系统仍然缺乏自然语言支持 (NLS) 的人机界面，这可以显著增强人与 DM 之间的交互。为了弥补这一差距，本文介绍了 VRCsim，一个旨在生成流式 VRC-CP 数据的 VRC 协同感知 (CP) 仿真框架。基于 VRCsim，我们构建了一个问题回答数据集 VRC-QA，专注于混合交通场景中的空间查询和推理。在 VRCsim 和 VRC-QA 的基础上，我们进一步提出了 Talk2DM，一个即插即用的模块，它通过 NLS 查询和常识推理能力扩展了 VRC-DM 系统。Talk2DM 构建于一种新型的链式提示 (CoP) 机制之上，该机制逐步将人定义的规则与大型语言模型 (LLM) 的常识知识相结合。在 VRC-QA 上的实验表明，Talk2DM 可以在不同的 LLM 之间无缝切换，同时保持较高的 NLS 查询准确率，展现出强大的泛化能力。虽然更大的模型往往能获得更高的准确率，但它们会造成显著的效率下降。我们的结果表明，由 Qwen3:8B、Gemma3:27B 和 GPT-oss 模型驱动的 Talk2DM 可以实现超过 93% 的 NLS 查询准确率，平均响应时间仅为 2-5 秒，表明其具有强大的实际应用潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces Talk2DM, a plug-and-play module that empowers vehicle-road-cloud dynamic maps with natural language querying and commonsense reasoning capabilities using large language models and a chain-of-prompt mechanism, achieving high accuracy and reasonable response times on a new spatial reasoning dataset, VRC-QA, built upon a new simulator, VRCsim.

Authors: Lu Tao, Jinxuan Luo, Yousuke Watanabe, Zhengshu Zhou, Yuhuan Lu, Shen Ying, Pan Zhang, Fei Zhao, Hiroaki Takada

Zooming without Zooming: Region-to-Image Distillation for Fine-Grained Multimodal Perception

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) excel at broad visual understanding but still struggle with fine-grained perception, where decisive evidence is small and easily overwhelmed by global context. Recent "Thinking-with-Images" methods alleviate this by iteratively zooming in and out regions of interest during inference, but incur high latency due to repeated tool calls and visual re-encoding. To address this, we propose Region-to-Image Distillation, which transforms zooming from an inference-time tool into a training-time primitive, thereby internalizing the benefits of agentic zooming into a single forward pass of an MLLM. In particular, we first zoom in to micro-cropped regions to let strong teacher models generate high-quality VQA data, and then distill this region-grounded supervision back to the full image. After training on such data, the smaller student model improves "single-glance" fine-grained perception without tool use. To rigorously evaluate this capability, we further present ZoomBench, a hybrid-annotated benchmark of 845 VQA data spanning six fine-grained perceptual dimensions, together with a dual-view protocol that quantifies the global--regional "zooming gap". Experiments show that our models achieve leading performance across multiple fine-grained perception benchmarks, and also improve general multimodal cognition on benchmarks such as visual reasoning and GUI agents. We further discuss when "Thinking-with-Images" is necessary versus when its gains can be distilled into a single forward pass. Our code is available at https://github.com/inclusionAI/Zooming-without-Zooming.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)擅长广泛的视觉理解，但在细粒度感知方面仍存在不足，因为在这种场景下，决定性的证据很小，容易被全局上下文所淹没。 近期提出的“图像思考”方法通过在推理过程中迭代式地放大和缩小感兴趣区域来缓解这一问题，但由于重复的工具调用和视觉重编码，导致了高延迟。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了区域到图像的蒸馏方法，将放大操作从推理时工具转变为训练时原语，从而将代理式放大的优势内化到 MLLM 的单次前向传播中。 具体而言，我们首先放大到微裁剪区域，使强大的教师模型生成高质量的 VQA 数据，然后将这种以区域为基础的监督知识蒸馏回完整图像。 在使用此类数据进行训练后，较小的学生模型无需使用工具即可提高“单次浏览”的细粒度感知能力。 为了严格评估这种能力，我们进一步提出了 ZoomBench，这是一个混合标注的基准，包含 845 个 VQA 数据，涵盖六个细粒度感知维度，以及量化全局-区域“放大差距”的双视图协议。 实验表明，我们的模型在多个细粒度感知基准上取得了领先的性能，并且还在视觉推理和 GUI 代理等基准上提高了通用多模态认知能力。 我们进一步讨论了何时“图像思考”是必要的，以及何时可以将它的收益提炼成单次前向传播。 我们的代码可在 https://github.com/inclusionAI/Zooming-without-Zooming 上获取。

TLDR: This paper introduces Region-to-Image Distillation, a method to train MLLMs to perform fine-grained visual understanding in a single forward pass by distilling knowledge from zoomed-in regions, and introduces a new benchmark, ZoomBench, for evaluating this capability.

简要说明: 本文介绍了区域到图像蒸馏方法，通过从放大区域中提取知识，训练MLLM在单次前向传递中执行细粒度视觉理解，并引入了一个新的基准ZoomBench，用于评估这种能力。

Authors: Lai Wei, Liangbo He, Jun Lan, Lingzhong Dong, Yutong Cai, Siyuan Li, Huijia Zhu, Weiqiang Wang, Linghe Kong, Yue Wang, Zhuosheng Zhang, Weiran Huang

FlowMind: Execute-Summarize for Structured Workflow Generation from LLM Reasoning

Abstract (English): LLMs can solve complex tasks through reasoning and tool use, but accurately translating these solutions into structured workflows remains challenging. We model workflows as sequences of tool use and reformulate the problem as designing a mechanism that can both solve tasks and reliably construct workflows. Prior approaches that build workflows during execution often suffer from inaccuracies due to interference between the two processes. We propose an Execute-Summarize(ES) framework that decouples task execution from workflow construction: the model first completes the task using available tools, then independently reconstructs a structured workflow from execution traces. This separation improves workflow accuracy and robustness. We introduce FlowBench and show through extensive experiments that our approach outperforms existing methods, providing a reliable paradigm for grounding free-form LLM reasoning into structured workflows.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型可以通过推理和工具使用来解决复杂的任务，但将这些解决方案准确地转化为结构化的工作流仍然具有挑战性。我们将工作流建模为工具使用序列，并将问题重新定义为设计一种机制，该机制既能解决任务，又能可靠地构建工作流。以往在执行过程中构建工作流的方法通常会由于这两个过程之间的干扰而导致不准确。我们提出了一种执行-总结（ES）框架，该框架将任务执行与工作流构建解耦：模型首先使用可用工具完成任务，然后独立地从执行轨迹中重建结构化的工作流。这种分离提高了工作流的准确性和鲁棒性。我们引入了FlowBench，并通过大量的实验表明，我们的方法优于现有的方法，为将自由形式的大型语言模型推理转化为结构化的工作流提供了一种可靠的范例。

TLDR: The paper introduces FlowMind, an Execute-Summarize framework that decouples task execution and workflow construction for more accurate and robust workflow generation from LLM reasoning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FlowMind，一个“执行-总结”框架，它将任务执行和工作流程构建分离，从而从LLM推理中生成更准确、更健壮的工作流程。

Authors: Yihao Liu, Ziyun Zhang, Zile He, Huaqian Cai

AmbiBench: Benchmarking Mobile GUI Agents Beyond One-Shot Instructions in the Wild

Abstract (English): Benchmarks are paramount for gauging progress in the domain of Mobile GUI Agents. In practical scenarios, users frequently fail to articulate precise directives containing full task details at the onset, and their expressions are typically ambiguous. Consequently, agents are required to converge on the user's true intent via active clarification and interaction during execution. However, existing benchmarks predominantly operate under the idealized assumption that user-issued instructions are complete and unequivocal. This paradigm focuses exclusively on assessing single-turn execution while overlooking the alignment capability of the agent. To address this limitation, we introduce AmbiBench, the first benchmark incorporating a taxonomy of instruction clarity to shift evaluation from unidirectional instruction following to bidirectional intent alignment. Grounded in Cognitive Gap theory, we propose a taxonomy of four clarity levels: Detailed, Standard, Incomplete, and Ambiguous. We construct a rigorous dataset of 240 ecologically valid tasks across 25 applications, subject to strict review protocols. Furthermore, targeting evaluation in dynamic environments, we develop MUSE (Mobile User Satisfaction Evaluator), an automated framework utilizing an MLLM-as-a-judge multi-agent architecture. MUSE performs fine-grained auditing across three dimensions: Outcome Effectiveness, Execution Quality, and Interaction Quality. Empirical results on AmbiBench reveal the performance boundaries of SoTA agents across different clarity levels, quantify the gains derived from active interaction, and validate the strong correlation between MUSE and human judgment. This work redefines evaluation standards, laying the foundation for next-generation agents capable of truly understanding user intent.

摘要（中文）: 基准测试对于衡量移动 GUI 代理领域的进展至关重要。在实际场景中，用户通常无法在开始时清晰地表达包含完整任务细节的精确指令，并且他们的表达通常是含糊不清的。因此，代理需要通过执行过程中的主动澄清和交互来收敛到用户的真实意图。然而，现有的基准测试主要在用户发布的指令完整明确的理想假设下运作。这种范式只关注评估单轮执行，而忽略了代理的对齐能力。为了解决这个局限性，我们引入了 AmbiBench，这是第一个包含指令清晰度分类法的基准测试，旨在将评估从单向指令跟随转变为双向意图对齐。基于认知差距理论，我们提出了一个包含四个清晰度级别的分类法：详细、标准、不完整和模糊。我们构建了一个严格的数据集，包含 25 个应用程序中 240 个生态有效的任务，并经过严格的审查协议。此外，针对动态环境中的评估，我们开发了 MUSE (移动用户满意度评估器)，这是一个利用 MLLM 即评判的多代理架构的自动化框架。MUSE 在三个维度上执行细粒度的审计：结果有效性、执行质量和交互质量。在 AmbiBench 上的经验结果揭示了 SoTA 代理在不同清晰度级别下的性能边界，量化了从主动交互中获得的收益，并验证了 MUSE 和人类判断之间的高度相关性。这项工作重新定义了评估标准，为能够真正理解用户意图的下一代代理奠定了基础。

TLDR: The paper introduces AmbiBench, a new benchmark for mobile GUI agents that focuses on evaluating their ability to handle ambiguous user instructions and engage in interactive clarification, along with MUSE, an automated evaluation framework.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AmbiBench，一个新的移动GUI代理的基准测试，专注于评估它们处理模糊用户指令并进行交互式澄清的能力，以及MUSE，一个自动评估框架。

Authors: Jiazheng Sun, Mingxuan Li, Yingying Zhang, Jiayang Niu, Yachen Wu, Ruihan Jin, Shuyu Lei, Pengrongrui Tan, Zongyu Zhang, Ruoyi Wang, Jiachen Yang, Boyu Yang, Jiacheng Liu, Xin Peng

AIR: Improving Agent Safety through Incident Response

Abstract (English): Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly deployed in practice across a wide range of autonomous applications. Yet current safety mechanisms for LLM agents focus almost exclusively on preventing failures in advance, providing limited capabilities for responding to, containing, or recovering from incidents after they inevitably arise. In this work, we introduce AIR, the first incident response framework for LLM agent systems. AIR defines a domain-specific language for managing the incident response lifecycle autonomously in LLM agent systems, and integrates it into the agent's execution loop to (1) detect incidents via semantic checks grounded in the current environment state and recent context, (2) guide the agent to execute containment and recovery actions via its tools, and (3) synthesize guardrail rules during eradication to block similar incidents in future executions. We evaluate AIR on three representative agent types. Results show that AIR achieves detection, remediation, and eradication success rates all exceeding 90%. Extensive experiments further confirm the necessity of AIR's key design components, show the timeliness and moderate overhead of AIR, and demonstrate that LLM-generated rules can approach the effectiveness of developer-authored rules across domains. These results show that incident response is both feasible and essential as a first-class mechanism for improving agent safety.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）智能体正日益广泛地应用于各种自主应用领域。然而，目前针对LLM智能体的安全机制几乎完全侧重于提前预防故障，对于在事故不可避免地发生后进行响应、遏制或恢复的能力有限。在这项工作中，我们提出了AIR，这是首个用于LLM智能体系统的事件响应框架。AIR定义了一种特定领域的语言，用于在LLM智能体系统中自主管理事件响应生命周期，并将其集成到智能体的执行循环中，以（1）通过基于当前环境状态和近期上下文的语义检查来检测事件，（2）指导智能体通过其工具执行遏制和恢复行动，以及（3）在根除阶段合成防护规则，以阻止未来执行中发生类似事件。我们在三种具有代表性的智能体类型上评估了AIR。结果表明，AIR在检测、补救和根除方面的成功率均超过90%。广泛的实验进一步证实了AIR关键设计组件的必要性，展示了AIR的及时性和适度开销，并表明LLM生成的规则可以接近开发者编写的规则在各个领域的效果。这些结果表明，事件响应作为一种一流机制对于提高智能体安全性是可行的，而且至关重要。

TLDR: The paper introduces AIR, a framework for incident response in LLM agents, enabling detection, containment, recovery, and eradication of failures after they occur, with high success rates demonstrated across various agent types.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AIR，一个用于LLM代理中事件响应的框架，能够检测、遏制、恢复和消除故障发生后发生的错误，并在各种代理类型中展现出高成功率。

Authors: Zibo Xiao, Jun Sun, Junjie Chen

Beyond Pixels: Vector-to-Graph Transformation for Reliable Schematic Auditing

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown remarkable progress in visual understanding, yet they suffer from a critical limitation: structural blindness. Even state-of-the-art models fail to capture topology and symbolic logic in engineering schematics, as their pixel-driven paradigm discards the explicit vector-defined relations needed for reasoning. To overcome this, we propose a Vector-to-Graph (V2G) pipeline that converts CAD diagrams into property graphs where nodes represent components and edges encode connectivity, making structural dependencies explicit and machine-auditable. On a diagnostic benchmark of electrical compliance checks, V2G yields large accuracy gains across all error categories, while leading MLLMs remain near chance level. These results highlight the systemic inadequacy of pixel-based methods and demonstrate that structure-aware representations provide a reliable path toward practical deployment of multimodal AI in engineering domains. To facilitate further research, we release our benchmark and implementation at https://github.com/gm-embodied/V2G-Audit.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）在视觉理解方面取得了显著进展，但它们存在一个关键的局限：结构盲视。即使是最先进的模型也无法捕获工程原理图中的拓扑结构和符号逻辑，因为它们以像素驱动的范式抛弃了推理所需的明确的矢量定义关系。为了克服这一点，我们提出了一种矢量到图（V2G）的管道，该管道将CAD图转换为属性图，其中节点表示组件，边编码连接性，从而使结构依赖关系显式化且机器可审计。在一个电气合规性检查的诊断基准上，V2G在所有错误类别中都获得了显著的精度提升，而领先的MLLM仍然接近随机水平。这些结果突出了基于像素的方法的系统性不足，并表明结构感知表示法为多模态人工智能在工程领域的实际部署提供了一条可靠的途径。为了促进进一步的研究，我们发布了我们的基准和实现，网址为https://github.com/gm-embodied/V2G-Audit。

TLDR: The paper introduces a Vector-to-Graph (V2G) pipeline to address the structural blindness of MLLMs in understanding engineering schematics, demonstrating significant accuracy gains in electrical compliance checks by converting CAD diagrams into property graphs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种向量到图 (V2G) 管道，旨在解决多模态大型语言模型 (MLLM) 在理解工程示意图方面的结构盲点，通过将 CAD 图转换为属性图，在电气合规性检查中实现了显著的准确性提升。

Authors: Chengwei Ma, Zhen Tian, Zhou Zhou, Zhixian Xu, Xiaowei Zhu, Xia Hua, Si Shi, F. Richard Yu

ScalSelect: Scalable Training-Free Multimodal Data Selection for Efficient Visual Instruction Tuning

Abstract (English): Large-scale Visual Instruction Tuning (VIT) has become a key paradigm for advancing the performance of vision-language models (VLMs) across various multimodal tasks. However, training on the large-scale datasets is computationally expensive and inefficient due to redundancy in the data, which motivates the need for multimodal data selection to improve training efficiency. Existing data selection methods for VIT either require costly training or gradient computation. Training-free alternatives often depend on proxy models or datasets, instruction-agnostic representations, and pairwise similarity with quadratic complexity, limiting scalability and representation fidelity. In this work, we propose ScalSelect, a scalable training-free multimodal data selection method with linear-time complexity with respect to the number of samples, eliminating the need for external models or auxiliary datasets. ScalSelect first constructs sample representations by extracting visual features most attended by instruction tokens in the target VLM, capturing instruction-relevant information. It then identifies samples whose representations best approximate the dominant subspace of the full dataset representations, enabling scalable importance scoring without pairwise comparisons. Extensive experiments across multiple VLMs, datasets, and selection budgets demonstrate that ScalSelect achieves over 97.5% of the performance of training on the full dataset using only 16% of the data, and even outperforms full-data training in some settings. The code is available at \href{https://github.com/ChangtiWu/ScalSelect}{ScalSelect}.

摘要（中文）: 大规模视觉指令调优（VIT）已成为提升视觉-语言模型（VLM）在各种多模态任务中性能的关键范式。然而，由于数据的冗余性，在大规模数据集上进行训练的计算成本高昂且效率低下，这推动了对多模态数据选择的需求，以提高训练效率。现有的VIT数据选择方法要么需要昂贵的训练，要么需要梯度计算。无需训练的替代方案通常依赖于代理模型或数据集、与指令无关的表示以及具有二次复杂度的成对相似性，从而限制了可扩展性和表示保真度。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种可扩展的无需训练的多模态数据选择方法ScalSelect，它具有关于样本数量的线性时间复杂度，消除了对外部模型或辅助数据集的需求。ScalSelect首先通过提取目标VLM中指令令牌最关注的视觉特征来构建样本表示，从而捕获与指令相关的信息。然后，它识别出其表示最接近完整数据集表示的优势子空间的样本，从而实现可扩展的重要性评分，而无需进行成对比较。在多个VLM、数据集和选择预算上的大量实验表明，ScalSelect仅使用16%的数据即可达到使用完整数据集训练性能的97.5%以上，甚至在某些情况下优于完整数据训练。 代码可在\href{https://github.com/ChangtiWu/ScalSelect}{ScalSelect}获得。

TLDR: The paper introduces ScalSelect, a scalable and training-free method for multimodal data selection in Visual Instruction Tuning (VIT). It efficiently selects crucial data subsets achieving comparable or better performance than training on the full dataset.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为ScalSelect的可扩展且无需训练的多模态数据选择方法，用于视觉指令调优（VIT）。它能够高效地选择关键数据子集，达到与在完整数据集上训练相当甚至更好的性能。

Authors: Changti Wu, Jiahuai Mao, Yuzhuo Miao, Shijie Lian, Bin Yu, Xiaopeng Lin, Cong Huang, Lei Zhang, Kai Chen

When Agents Disagree With Themselves: Measuring Behavioral Consistency in LLM-Based Agents

Abstract (English): Run the same LLM agent on the same task twice: do you get the same behavior? We find the answer is often no. In a study of 3,000 agent runs across three models (Llama 3.1 70B, GPT-4o, and Claude Sonnet 4.5) on HotpotQA, we observe that ReAct-style agents produce 2.0--4.2 distinct action sequences per 10 runs on average, even with identical inputs. More importantly, this variance predicts failure: tasks with consistent behavior ($\leq$2 unique paths) achieve 80--92% accuracy, while highly inconsistent tasks ($\geq$6 unique paths) achieve only 25--60%, a 32--55 percentage point gap depending on model. We trace variance to early decisions: 69% of divergence occurs at step 2, the first search query. Our results suggest that monitoring behavioral consistency during execution could enable early error detection and improve agent reliability.

摘要（中文）: 在同一任务上运行同一个 LLM 智能体两次：你会得到相同的行为吗？我们的研究发现答案通常是否定的。在一项对 HotpotQA 上三个模型（Llama 3.1 70B、GPT-4o 和 Claude Sonnet 4.5）进行的 3000 次智能体运行的实验中，我们观察到，即使输入完全相同，ReAct 风格的智能体平均每次运行 10 次也会产生 2.0-4.2 个不同的行动序列。更重要的是，这种差异预示着失败：行为一致的任务（≤2 条唯一路径）的准确率达到 80-92%，而高度不一致的任务（≥6 条唯一路径）的准确率仅为 25-60%，具体取决于模型，差距为 32-55 个百分点。我们追溯差异的来源，发现差异主要来自早期决策：69% 的差异发生在第二步，即第一次搜索查询。我们的结果表明，在执行期间监控行为一致性可以尽早发现错误并提高智能体的可靠性。

TLDR: This paper investigates the behavioral consistency of LLM agents on a task and finds that inconsistency in action sequences is a strong predictor of task failure, suggesting a method for early error detection.

简要说明: 本文研究了LLM智能体在任务中的行为一致性，发现动作序列的不一致性是任务失败的强预测指标，为早期错误检测提供了一种方法。

Authors: Aman Mehta

MAPLE: Modality-Aware Post-training and Learning Ecosystem

Abstract (English): Multimodal language models now integrate text, audio, and video for unified reasoning. Yet existing RL post-training pipelines treat all input signals as equally relevant, ignoring which modalities each task actually requires. This modality-blind training inflates policy-gradient variance, slows convergence, and degrades robustness to real-world distribution shifts where signals may be missing, added, or reweighted. We introduce MAPLE, a complete modality-aware post-training and learning ecosystem comprising: (1) MAPLE-bench, the first benchmark explicitly annotating minimal signal combinations required per task; (2) MAPO, a modality-aware policy optimization framework that stratifies batches by modality requirement to reduce gradient variance from heterogeneous group advantages; (3) Adaptive weighting and curriculum scheduling that balances and prioritizes harder signal combinations. Systematic analysis across loss aggregation, clipping, sampling, and curriculum design establishes MAPO's optimal training strategy. Adaptive weighting and curriculum focused learning further boost performance across signal combinations. MAPLE narrows uni/multi-modal accuracy gaps by 30.24%, converges 3.18x faster, and maintains stability across all modality combinations under realistic reduced signal access. MAPLE constitutes a complete recipe for deployment-ready multimodal RL post-training.

摘要（中文）: 多模态语言模型目前集成了文本、音频和视频，以实现统一的推理。然而，现有的强化学习后训练流程将所有输入信号视为同等重要，忽略了每个任务实际所需的模态。这种模态盲训练会增大策略梯度方差，减缓收敛速度，并降低对真实世界分布偏移的鲁棒性，在真实世界中，信号可能缺失、添加或重新加权。我们引入了MAPLE，一个完整的模态感知后训练和学习生态系统，包括：（1）MAPLE-bench，这是第一个明确标注每个任务所需最小信号组合的基准；（2）MAPO，一个模态感知策略优化框架，通过模态需求对批次进行分层，以减少来自异构组收益的梯度方差；（3）自适应权重和课程调度，平衡并优先处理更难的信号组合。对损失聚合、裁剪、采样和课程设计的系统分析确立了MAPO的最佳训练策略。自适应权重和聚焦于学习的课程进一步提升了跨信号组合的性能。MAPLE将单/多模态准确率差距缩小了30.24%，收敛速度提高了3.18倍，并在现实中减少信号访问的情况下，保持了跨所有模态组合的稳定性。MAPLE构成了一个完整的可部署多模态强化学习后训练方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces MAPLE, a modality-aware RL post-training ecosystem that includes a benchmark, a policy optimization framework (MAPO), and adaptive weighting/curriculum scheduling, demonstrating improved performance and robustness in multimodal RL tasks with varying signal availability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MAPLE，一个模态感知的强化学习后训练生态系统，包括一个基准测试、一个策略优化框架（MAPO）和自适应权重/课程安排，展示了在具有不同信号可用性的多模态强化学习任务中改进的性能和鲁棒性。

Authors: Nikhil Verma, Minjung Kim, JooYoung Yoo, Kyung-Min Jin, Manasa Bharadwaj, Kevin Ferreira, Ko Keun Kim, Youngjoon Kim

The Five Ws of Multi-Agent Communication: Who Talks to Whom, When, What, and Why -- A Survey from MARL to Emergent Language and LLMs

Abstract (English): Multi-agent sequential decision-making powers many real-world systems, from autonomous vehicles and robotics to collaborative AI assistants. In dynamic, partially observable environments, communication is often what reduces uncertainty and makes collaboration possible. This survey reviews multi-agent communication (MA-Comm) through the Five Ws: who communicates with whom, what is communicated, when communication occurs, and why communication is beneficial. This framing offers a clean way to connect ideas across otherwise separate research threads. We trace how communication approaches have evolved across three major paradigms. In Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL), early methods used hand-designed or implicit protocols, followed by end-to-end learned communication optimized for reward and control. While successful, these protocols are frequently task-specific and hard to interpret, motivating work on Emergent Language (EL), where agents can develop more structured or symbolic communication through interaction. EL methods, however, still struggle with grounding, generalization, and scalability, which has fueled recent interest in large language models (LLMs) that bring natural language priors for reasoning, planning, and collaboration in more open-ended settings. Across MARL, EL, and LLM-based systems, we highlight how different choices shape communication design, where the main trade-offs lie, and what remains unsolved. We distill practical design patterns and open challenges to support future hybrid systems that combine learning, language, and control for scalable and interpretable multi-agent collaboration.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体序列决策驱动着许多现实世界的系统，从自动驾驶汽车和机器人技术到协作式AI助手。在动态、部分可观察的环境中，通信通常是减少不确定性并使协作成为可能的关键。本综述通过五个“W”来回顾多智能体通信（MA-Comm）：谁与谁通信(Who)、通信的内容(What)、通信发生的时间(When)以及为什么通信是有益的(Why)。这种框架提供了一种清晰的方式，可以将各个独立的研究思路联系起来。我们追溯了通信方法在三个主要范式中的演变历程。 在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，早期方法使用手工设计或隐式协议，随后是为奖励和控制而优化的端到端学习得到的通信。 虽然这些方法取得了成功，但这些协议通常是特定于任务的并且难以解释，这促使了涌现语言（EL）的研究，在该领域中，智能体可以通过交互来发展更结构化或符号化的通信。 然而，EL方法仍然在语义扎根、泛化和可扩展性方面存在困难，这推动了最近对大型语言模型（LLMs）的兴趣，这些模型将自然语言先验知识带入更开放环境中的推理、规划和协作中。 在MARL、EL和基于LLM的系统中，我们强调了不同的选择如何塑造通信设计、主要的权衡取舍以及仍然未解决的问题。 我们提炼出实用的设计模式和开放的挑战，以支持未来的混合系统，这些系统将学习、语言和控制相结合，以实现可扩展和可解释的多智能体协作。

TLDR: This survey paper reviews multi-agent communication through the lens of the 'Five Ws' (Who, What, When, Why), tracing its evolution across MARL, Emergent Language, and LLM-based systems, and highlighting design trade-offs and open challenges.

简要说明: 这篇综述论文从“五个W”（谁、什么、何时、为什么）的角度回顾了多智能体通信，追溯了它在MARL、Emergent Language和基于LLM的系统中的演变，并强调了设计权衡和未解决的挑战。

Authors: Jingdi Chen, Hanqing Yang, Zongjun Liu, Carlee Joe-Wong

Budget-Constrained Agentic Large Language Models: Intention-Based Planning for Costly Tool Use

Abstract (English): We study budget-constrained tool-augmented agents, where a large language model must solve multi-step tasks by invoking external tools under a strict monetary budget. We formalize this setting as sequential decision making in context space with priced and stochastic tool executions, making direct planning intractable due to massive state-action spaces, high variance of outcomes and prohibitive exploration cost. To address these challenges, we propose INTENT, an inference-time planning framework that leverages an intention-aware hierarchical world model to anticipate future tool usage, risk-calibrated cost, and guide decisions online. Across cost-augmented StableToolBench, INTENT strictly enforces hard budget feasibility while substantially improving task success over baselines, and remains robust under dynamic market shifts such as tool price changes and varying budgets.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了预算约束的工具增强型智能体，其中大型语言模型必须通过在严格的资金预算下调用外部工具来解决多步骤任务。我们将此设定形式化为上下文空间中的序列决策，其中工具执行的价格是确定的且具有随机性，这使得直接规划由于巨大的状态-动作空间、结果的高度方差和过高的探索成本而变得难以处理。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出 INTENT，一种推理时规划框架，它利用具有意图感知的分层世界模型来预测未来的工具使用、经过风险校准的成本，并在线指导决策。在成本增强的 StableToolBench 上，INTENT 严格执行硬预算可行性，同时大幅提高了任务成功率，并且在工具价格变化和预算变化等动态市场变化下保持稳健性。

TLDR: The paper introduces INTENT, a planning framework for budget-constrained LLM agents that use external tools by employing a hierarchical world model to anticipate costs and guide decisions, demonstrating improved task success and robustness.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为INTENT的规划框架，用于在预算约束下使用外部工具的LLM智能体。该框架通过使用分层世界模型来预测成本并指导决策，从而提高了任务成功率和鲁棒性。

Authors: Hanbing Liu, Chunhao Tian, Nan An, Ziyuan Wang, Pinyan Lu, Changyuan Yu, Qi Qi

Adaptive Milestone Reward for GUI Agents

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a mainstream paradigm for training Mobile GUI Agents, yet it struggles with the temporal credit assignment problem inherent in long-horizon tasks. A primary challenge lies in the trade-off between reward fidelity and density: outcome reward offers high fidelity but suffers from signal sparsity, while process reward provides dense supervision but remains prone to bias and reward hacking. To resolve this conflict, we propose the Adaptive Milestone Reward (ADMIRE) mechanism. ADMIRE constructs a verifiable, adaptive reward system by anchoring trajectory to milestones, which are dynamically distilled from successful explorations. Crucially, ADMIRE integrates an asymmetric credit assignment strategy that denoises successful trajectories and scaffolds failed trajectories. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ADMIRE consistently yields over 10% absolute improvement in success rate across different base models on AndroidWorld. Moreover, the method exhibits robust generalizability, achieving strong performance across diverse RL algorithms and heterogeneous environments such as web navigation and embodied tasks.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）已经成为训练移动GUI Agent的主流范式，但它在长时程任务中难以处理固有的时间信用分配问题。一个主要的挑战在于奖励忠实度和密度之间的权衡：结果奖励提供高忠实度，但存在信号稀疏问题，而过程奖励提供密集监督，但仍然容易产生偏差和奖励操纵。为了解决这一冲突，我们提出了自适应里程碑奖励（ADMIRE）机制。ADMIRE通过将轨迹锚定到里程碑来构建可验证的自适应奖励系统，这些里程碑是从成功的探索中动态提炼出来的。至关重要的是，ADMIRE集成了一种非对称信用分配策略，该策略对成功的轨迹进行去噪，并为失败的轨迹提供支架。大量实验表明，ADMIRE在AndroidWorld上的不同基准模型上，成功率始终能带来超过10%的绝对提升。此外，该方法表现出强大的泛化能力，在不同的RL算法和异构环境中（例如Web导航和具身任务）都取得了良好的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Adaptive Milestone Reward (ADMIRE), a novel reinforcement learning method that uses dynamically distilled milestones and asymmetric credit assignment to improve long-horizon GUI agent performance, showing significant gains in AndroidWorld and generalization to other environments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为自适应里程碑奖励（ADMIRE）的新型强化学习方法，该方法利用动态提取的里程碑和不对称的信用分配来提高长时程GUI代理的性能，并在AndroidWorld中显示出显著的改进，并推广到其他环境。

Authors: Congmin Zheng, Xiaoyun Mo, Xinbei Ma, Qiqiang Lin, Yin Zhao, Jiachen Zhu, Xingyu Lou, Jun Wang, Zhaoxiang Wang, Weiwen Liu, Zhuosheng Zhang, Yong Yu, Weinan Zhang

Credit Where It is Due: Cross-Modality Connectivity Drives Precise Reinforcement Learning for MLLM Reasoning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), yet how visual evidence is integrated during reasoning remains poorly understood. We explore multimodal RLVR through the lens of cross-modal attention connectivity and find that only a small fraction of tokens (approximately 15%) exhibit strong visual-textual coupling. These high-connectivity tokens act as anchors that ground reasoning in the image, while the majority follow linguistic patterns. During RLVR training, credit assignment naturally concentrates on these anchors, sharpening their visual grounding over time. Building on this insight, we propose Anchor-Token Reinforcement Learning (AT-RL), a lightweight framework that selectively reinforces high-connectivity tokens via graph-based clustering of attention topology. Evaluated across the series (3B-32B), AT-RL introduces only 1.2% overhead yet enables the 32B model to surpass the 72B-Instruct baseline on MathVista (80.2), with consistent gains observed across STEM, video and general tasks. Conversely, training solely on low-connectivity tokens causes severe degradation, confirming that effective multimodal RL hinges on precise credit assignment to visual anchors. Our work reveals that reasoning quality is governed not by token quantity but by the fidelity of cross-modal anchoring.

摘要（中文）: 具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）的推理能力，然而，视觉证据如何在推理过程中整合仍不甚明了。我们通过跨模态注意力连通性的视角探索多模态RLVR，发现只有一小部分token（约15%）表现出强烈的视觉-文本耦合。这些高连通性的token充当锚点，将推理锚定在图像中，而大多数token遵循语言模式。在RLVR训练期间，信用分配自然集中在这些锚点上，随着时间的推移，增强了它们的视觉基础。基于这一洞察，我们提出了锚定Token强化学习（AT-RL），这是一个轻量级框架，通过基于图的注意力拓扑聚类选择性地强化高连通性token。经过对一系列模型（3B-32B）的评估，AT-RL仅引入1.2%的开销，却使得32B模型在MathVista上超越了72B-Instruct基线（80.2），并在STEM、视频和通用任务中观察到一致的收益。相反，仅对低连通性token进行训练会导致严重的性能下降，证实了有效的多模态强化学习依赖于对视觉锚点的精确信用分配。我们的工作表明，推理质量并非由token数量决定，而是由跨模态锚定的保真度决定。

TLDR: This paper identifies and leverages high cross-modal connectivity tokens in MLLMs for more efficient and effective reinforcement learning, achieving significant performance gains with minimal overhead.

简要说明: 该论文发现并利用MLLM中高跨模态连接的tokens，以实现更高效和有效的强化学习，并以最小的开销实现了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Zhengbo Jiao, Shaobo Wang, Zifan Zhang, Wei Wang, Bing Zhao, Hu Wei, Linfeng Zhang

Causal-JEPA: Learning World Models through Object-Level Latent Interventions

Abstract (English): World models require robust relational understanding to support prediction, reasoning, and control. While object-centric representations provide a useful abstraction, they are not sufficient to capture interaction-dependent dynamics. We therefore propose C-JEPA, a simple and flexible object-centric world model that extends masked joint embedding prediction from image patches to object-centric representations. By applying object-level masking that requires an object's state to be inferred from other objects, C-JEPA induces latent interventions with counterfactual-like effects and prevents shortcut solutions, making interaction reasoning essential. Empirically, C-JEPA leads to consistent gains in visual question answering, with an absolute improvement of about 20\% in counterfactual reasoning compared to the same architecture without object-level masking. On agent control tasks, C-JEPA enables substantially more efficient planning by using only 1\% of the total latent input features required by patch-based world models, while achieving comparable performance. Finally, we provide a formal analysis demonstrating that object-level masking induces a causal inductive bias via latent interventions. Our code is available at https://github.com/galilai-group/cjepa.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型需要稳健的关系理解来支持预测、推理和控制。虽然以对象为中心的表征提供了一种有用的抽象，但它们不足以捕捉依赖于交互的动态。因此，我们提出了C-JEPA，一种简单而灵活的以对象为中心的世界模型，它将掩码联合嵌入预测从图像块扩展到以对象为中心的表征。通过应用对象级别的掩码，要求从其他对象推断一个对象的状态，C-JEPA诱导具有反事实效应的潜在干预，并防止捷径解决方案，使得交互推理至关重要。在经验上，C-JEPA在视觉问答中带来了持续的收益，与没有对象级别掩码的相同架构相比，在反事实推理方面取得了大约20%的绝对改进。在智能体控制任务中，C-JEPA通过仅使用基于图像块的世界模型所需总潜在输入特征的1%来实现更高效的规划，同时获得可比较的性能。最后，我们提供了一个正式的分析，证明了对象级别的掩码通过潜在干预诱导了一种因果归纳偏置。我们的代码可在https://github.com/galilai-group/cjepa 上找到。

TLDR: C-JEPA, a new object-centric world model, uses object-level masking to encourage interaction reasoning, leading to improvements in visual question answering and agent control with better efficiency.

简要说明: C-JEPA是一种新的以对象为中心的世界模型，它利用对象级别的掩蔽来促进交互推理, 从而在视觉问答和智能体控制方面获得了改进，并提高了效率。

Authors: Heejeong Nam, Quentin Le Lidec, Lucas Maes, Yann LeCun, Randall Balestriero

Pushing Forward Pareto Frontiers of Proactive Agents with Behavioral Agentic Optimization

Abstract (English): Proactive large language model (LLM) agents aim to actively plan, query, and interact over multiple turns, enabling efficient task completion beyond passive instruction following and making them essential for real-world, user-centric applications. Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) has recently emerged as a promising solution for training such agents in multi-turn settings, allowing interaction strategies to be learned from feedback. However, existing pipelines face a critical challenge in balancing task performance with user engagement, as passive agents can not efficiently adapt to users' intentions while overuse of human feedback reduces their satisfaction. To address this trade-off, we propose BAO, an agentic RL framework that combines behavior enhancement to enrich proactive reasoning and information-gathering capabilities with behavior regularization to suppress inefficient or redundant interactions and align agent behavior with user expectations. We evaluate BAO on multiple tasks from the UserRL benchmark suite, and demonstrate that it substantially outperforms proactive agentic RL baselines while achieving comparable or even superior performance to commercial LLM agents, highlighting its effectiveness for training proactive, user-aligned LLM agents in complex multi-turn scenarios. Our website: https://proactive-agentic-rl.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 主动大型语言模型 (LLM) 智能体旨在主动规划、查询和进行多轮交互，从而实现超越被动指令执行的高效任务完成，使其对以用户为中心的实际应用至关重要。智能体强化学习 (RL) 近期已成为一种有前景的解决方案，用于在多轮环境中训练此类智能体，从而允许交互策略从反馈中学习。然而，现有的流程面临着在任务性能和用户参与度之间取得平衡的关键挑战，因为被动智能体无法有效地适应用户的意图，而过度使用人工反馈会降低他们的满意度。为了解决这种权衡，我们提出了一种智能体 RL 框架 BAO，该框架结合了行为增强以丰富主动推理和信息收集能力，以及行为正则化以抑制低效或冗余的交互并使智能体的行为与用户的期望保持一致。我们在 UserRL 基准测试套件中的多个任务上评估了 BAO，并证明它大幅优于主动智能体 RL 基线，同时实现了与商业 LLM 智能体相当甚至更优越的性能，突显了其在复杂多轮场景中训练主动、用户对齐 LLM 智能体的有效性。我们的网站：https://proactive-agentic-rl.github.io/。

TLDR: This paper introduces BAO, an agentic RL framework that balances task performance and user engagement for proactive LLM agents by combining behavior enhancement and regularization. It shows improved performance compared to other RL and commercial LLM agent baselines.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为BAO的智能体强化学习框架，该框架通过结合行为增强和正则化，平衡了主动LLM智能体的任务性能和用户参与度。结果表明，相较于其他RL和商业LLM智能体基线，其性能有所提高。

Authors: Yihang Yao, Zhepeng Cen, Haohong Lin, Shiqi Liu, Zuxin Liu, Jiacheng Zhu, Zhang-Wei Hong, Laixi Shi, Ding Zhao

AgentNoiseBench: Benchmarking Robustness of Tool-Using LLM Agents Under Noisy Condition

Abstract (English): Recent advances in large language models have enabled LLM-based agents to achieve strong performance on a variety of benchmarks. However, their performance in real-world deployments often that observed on benchmark settings, especially in complex and imperfect environments. This discrepancy largely arises because prevailing training and evaluation paradigms are typically built on idealized assumptions, overlooking the inherent stochasticity and noise present in real-world interactions. To bridge this gap, we introduce AgentNoiseBench, a framework for systematically evaluating the robustness of agentic models under noisy environments. We first conduct an in-depth analysis of biases and uncertainties in real-world scenarios and categorize environmental noise into two primary types: user-noise and tool-noise. Building on this analysis, we develop an automated pipeline that injects controllable noise into existing agent-centric benchmarks while preserving task solvability. Leveraging this pipeline, we perform extensive evaluations across a wide range of models with diverse architectures and parameter scales. Our results reveal consistent performance variations under different noise conditions, highlighting the sensitivity of current agentic models to realistic environmental perturbations.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型近期的进展使得基于大语言模型的智能体在各种基准测试中取得了优异的表现。然而，它们在现实世界部署中的表现通常低于在基准测试环境中所观察到的水平，尤其是在复杂和不完善的环境中。这种差异很大程度上源于当前主流的训练和评估范例通常基于理想化的假设，忽略了现实世界交互中固有的随机性和噪声。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了AgentNoiseBench，这是一个系统性地评估智能体模型在噪声环境下鲁棒性的框架。我们首先对现实场景中的偏差和不确定性进行了深入分析，并将环境噪声分为两种主要类型：用户噪声和工具噪声。基于这一分析，我们开发了一个自动化的管道，可以将可控噪声注入到现有的以智能体为中心的基准测试中，同时保持任务的可解性。利用该管道，我们对各种架构和参数规模的模型进行了广泛的评估。我们的结果表明，在不同的噪声条件下，性能存在持续的变化，突显了当前智能体模型对现实环境扰动的敏感性。

TLDR: The paper introduces AgentNoiseBench, a framework to benchmark the robustness of tool-using LLM agents under noisy conditions by injecting controllable noise into existing benchmarks. The results show current agents are sensitive to realistic environmental perturbations.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AgentNoiseBench，一个用于评估工具型LLM智能体在噪声条件下鲁棒性的框架，通过向现有基准测试注入可控噪声。结果表明，当前的智能体对现实环境中的扰动非常敏感。

Authors: Ruipeng Wang, Yuxin Chen, Yukai Wang, Chang Wu, Junfeng Fang, Xiaodong Cai, Qi Gu, Hui Su, An Zhang, Xiang Wang, Xunliang Cai, Tat-Seng Chua

Beyond VLM-Based Rewards: Diffusion-Native Latent Reward Modeling

Abstract (English): Preference optimization for diffusion and flow-matching models relies on reward functions that are both discriminatively robust and computationally efficient. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have emerged as the primary reward provider, leveraging their rich multimodal priors to guide alignment. However, their computation and memory cost can be substantial, and optimizing a latent diffusion generator through a pixel-space reward introduces a domain mismatch that complicates alignment. In this paper, we propose DiNa-LRM, a diffusion-native latent reward model that formulates preference learning directly on noisy diffusion states. Our method introduces a noise-calibrated Thurstone likelihood with diffusion-noise-dependent uncertainty. DiNa-LRM leverages a pretrained latent diffusion backbone with a timestep-conditioned reward head, and supports inference-time noise ensembling, providing a diffusion-native mechanism for test-time scaling and robust rewarding. Across image alignment benchmarks, DiNa-LRM substantially outperforms existing diffusion-based reward baselines and achieves performance competitive with state-of-the-art VLMs at a fraction of the computational cost. In preference optimization, we demonstrate that DiNa-LRM improves preference optimization dynamics, enabling faster and more resource-efficient model alignment.

摘要（中文）: 扩散模型和流匹配模型的偏好优化依赖于具有判别鲁棒性和计算效率的奖励函数。视觉-语言模型（VLMs）已成为主要的奖励提供者，利用其丰富的多模态先验来指导对齐。然而，它们的计算和内存成本可能相当高昂，并且通过像素空间的奖励优化一个潜在扩散生成器引入了域不匹配，这使得对齐变得复杂。在本文中，我们提出了 DiNa-LRM，一种扩散原生潜在奖励模型，它直接在噪声扩散状态上制定偏好学习。我们的方法引入了一种噪声校准的 Thurstone 似然，其中包含扩散噪声相关的置信度。DiNa-LRM 利用预训练的潜在扩散主干网络和一个时间步条件奖励头，并支持推理时噪声集成，从而为测试时缩放和稳健奖励提供了一种扩散原生机制。在图像对齐基准测试中，DiNa-LRM 显著优于现有的基于扩散的奖励基线，并且以极低的计算成本实现了与最先进的 VLM 相当的性能。在偏好优化方面，我们证明 DiNa-LRM 改善了偏好优化动态，从而实现了更快、资源效率更高的模型对齐。

TLDR: The paper introduces DiNa-LRM, a diffusion-native reward model that operates in the latent space of diffusion models, improving efficiency and performance compared to VLM-based rewards in preference optimization for image alignment.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为DiNa-LRM的扩散原生奖励模型，该模型在扩散模型的潜在空间中运行，与基于VLM的奖励相比，提高了图像对齐偏好优化中的效率和性能。

Authors: Gongye Liu, Bo Yang, Yida Zhi, Zhizhou Zhong, Lei Ke, Didan Deng, Han Gao, Yongxiang Huang, Kaihao Zhang, Hongbo Fu, Wenhan Luo

FormalJudge: A Neuro-Symbolic Paradigm for Agentic Oversight

Abstract (English): As LLM-based agents increasingly operate in high-stakes domains with real-world consequences, ensuring their behavioral safety becomes paramount. The dominant oversight paradigm, LLM-as-a-Judge, faces a fundamental dilemma: how can probabilistic systems reliably supervise other probabilistic systems without inheriting their failure modes? We argue that formal verification offers a principled escape from this dilemma, yet its adoption has been hindered by a critical bottleneck: the translation from natural language requirements to formal specifications. This paper bridges this gap by proposing , a neuro-symbolic framework that employs a bidirectional Formal-of-Thought architecture: LLMs serve as specification compilers that top-down decompose high-level human intent into atomic, verifiable constraints, then bottom-up prove compliance using Dafny specifications and Z3 Satisfiability modulo theories solving, which produces mathematical guarantees rather than probabilistic scores. We validate across three benchmarks spanning behavioral safety, multi-domain constraint adherence, and agentic upward deception detection. Experiments on 7 agent models demonstrate that achieves an average improvement of 16.6% over LLM-as-a-Judge baselines, enables weak-to-strong generalization where a 7B judge achieves over 90% accuracy detecting deception from 72B agents, and provides near-linear safety improvement through iterative refinement.

摘要（中文）: 随着基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体越来越多地在高风险、具有现实世界后果的领域中运行，确保其行为安全性变得至关重要。目前主流的监督范式，即“LLM-即-法官”，面临一个根本性的困境：概率系统如何在不继承其自身失效模式的情况下，可靠地监督其他概率系统？我们认为，形式化验证提供了一种摆脱这种困境的原则性方法，但其应用受到一个关键瓶颈的阻碍：从自然语言需求到形式化规范的转换。本文通过提出，一个神经符号框架，来弥合这一差距。采用双向思维链架构：LLM充当规范编译器，自上而下地将高层人类意图分解为原子性的、可验证的约束，然后自下而上地使用Dafny规范和Z3可满足性模理论（SMT）求解来证明合规性，从而产生数学保证而非概率分数。我们在涵盖行为安全、多域约束遵守以及智能体向上欺骗检测的三个基准测试中进行了验证。针对7个智能体模型的实验表明，相比“LLM-即-法官”基线，平均提高了16.6%，实现了弱到强的泛化，即一个7B的法官能够以超过90%的准确率检测来自72B智能体的欺骗行为，并通过迭代精化实现了近乎线性的安全提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces FormalJudge, a neuro-symbolic framework that uses formal verification (Dafny, Z3) to improve the behavioral safety and reliability of LLM-based agents, achieving better performance than LLM-as-a-Judge baselines.

简要说明: 本文介绍FormalJudge，一个神经符号框架，使用形式化验证（Dafny, Z3）来提高基于LLM的代理的行为安全性和可靠性，并实现了比LLM-as-a-Judge基线更好的性能。

Authors: Jiayi Zhou, Yang Sheng, Hantao Lou, Yaodong Yang, Jie Fu

Learning to Compose for Cross-domain Agentic Workflow Generation

Abstract (English): Automatically generating agentic workflows -- executable operator graphs or codes that orchestrate reasoning, verification, and repair -- has become a practical way to solve complex tasks beyond what single-pass LLM generation can reliably handle. Yet what constitutes a good workflow depends heavily on the task distribution and the available operators. Under domain shift, current systems typically rely on iterative workflow refinement to discover a feasible workflow from a large workflow space, incurring high iteration costs and yielding unstable, domain-specific behavior. In response, we internalize a decompose-recompose-decide mechanism into an open-source LLM for cross-domain workflow generation. To decompose, we learn a compact set of reusable workflow capabilities across diverse domains. To recompose, we map each input task to a sparse composition over these bases to generate a task-specific workflow in a single pass. To decide, we attribute the success or failure of workflow generation to counterfactual contributions from learned capabilities, thereby capturing which capabilities actually drive success by their marginal effects. Across stringent multi-domain, cross-domain, and unseen-domain evaluations, our 1-pass generator surpasses SOTA refinement baselines that consume 20 iterations, while substantially reducing generation latency and cost.

摘要（中文）: 自动生成具有自主行动性的工作流（即编排推理、验证和修复的可执行算子图或代码）已经成为解决复杂任务的实用方法，这些任务超出了单次LLM生成能够可靠处理的范围。然而，什么构成一个好的工作流在很大程度上取决于任务分布和可用的算子。在领域迁移下，目前的系统通常依赖于迭代式工作流优化，以从庞大的工作流空间中发现一个可行的工作流，这导致了高迭代成本，并产生不稳定的、特定领域的行为。为了解决这个问题，我们将分解-重组-决策机制内置到一个开源LLM中，用于跨领域工作流生成。为了分解，我们学习了一组紧凑且可重用的、跨越不同领域的工作流能力。为了重组，我们将每个输入任务映射到这些基础能力的稀疏组合，从而单次生成一个特定于任务的工作流。为了决策，我们将工作流生成成功或失败归因于学习到的能力的逆事实贡献，从而通过它们的边际效应来捕获哪些能力实际上驱动了成功。在严格的多领域、跨领域和未见领域评估中，我们的单次生成器超越了消耗20次迭代的SOTA优化基线，同时显著降低了生成延迟和成本。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method for generating agentic workflows that can generalize across different domains, using a decompose-recompose-decide mechanism to improve efficiency and reduce iteration costs compared to current state-of-the-art refinement-based approaches.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种生成代理工作流的方法，该方法可以通过分解-重组-决策机制跨不同领域泛化，与当前最先进的基于改进的方法相比，提高了效率并降低了迭代成本。

Authors: Jialiang Wang, Shengxiang Xu, Hanmo Liu, Jiachuan Wang, Yuyu Luo, Shimin Di, Min-Ling Zhang, Lei Chen

Can Local Vision-Language Models improve Activity Recognition over Vision Transformers? -- Case Study on Newborn Resuscitation

Abstract (English): Accurate documentation of newborn resuscitation is essential for quality improvement and adherence to clinical guidelines, yet remains underutilized in practice. Previous work using 3D-CNNs and Vision Transformers (ViT) has shown promising results in detecting key activities from newborn resuscitation videos, but also highlighted the challenges in recognizing such fine-grained activities. This work investigates the potential of generative AI (GenAI) methods to improve activity recognition from such videos. Specifically, we explore the use of local vision-language models (VLMs), combined with large language models (LLMs), and compare them to a supervised TimeSFormer baseline. Using a simulated dataset comprising 13.26 hours of newborn resuscitation videos, we evaluate several zero-shot VLM-based strategies and fine-tuned VLMs with classification heads, including Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA). Our results suggest that small (local) VLMs struggle with hallucinations, but when fine-tuned with LoRA, the results reach F1 score at 0.91, surpassing the TimeSformer results of 0.70.

摘要（中文）: 新生儿复苏过程的准确记录对于质量改进和临床指南的遵循至关重要，但在实践中仍然未得到充分利用。先前使用3D-CNN和视觉Transformer（ViT）的工作在检测新生儿复苏视频中的关键活动方面已显示出前景，但也突出了识别此类细粒度活动的挑战。本研究探讨了生成式人工智能（GenAI）方法在提高此类视频活动识别方面的潜力。具体而言，我们探索了局部视觉-语言模型（VLM）与大型语言模型（LLM）的结合使用，并将它们与监督学习的TimeSFormer基线进行比较。我们使用包含13.26小时新生儿复苏视频的模拟数据集，评估了几种基于零样本VLM的策略以及带有分类头的微调VLM，包括低秩自适应（LoRA）。我们的结果表明，小型（局部）VLM存在幻觉问题，但当使用LoRA进行微调时，结果的F1分数达到0.91，超过了TimeSformer的结果0.70。

TLDR: This paper explores the use of local vision-language models (VLMs) for newborn resuscitation activity recognition, finding that fine-tuned VLMs outperform TimeSformer baselines on a simulated dataset.

简要说明: 本文探索了局部视觉-语言模型（VLM）在新生儿复苏活动识别中的应用，发现经过微调的VLM在模拟数据集上的表现优于TimeSformer基线。

Authors: Enrico Guerriero, Kjersti Engan, Øyvind Meinich-Bache

Code2Worlds: Empowering Coding LLMs for 4D World Generation

Abstract (English): Achieving spatial intelligence requires moving beyond visual plausibility to build world simulators grounded in physical laws. While coding LLMs have advanced static 3D scene generation, extending this paradigm to 4D dynamics remains a critical frontier. This task presents two fundamental challenges: multi-scale context entanglement, where monolithic generation fails to balance local object structures with global environmental layouts; and a semantic-physical execution gap, where open-loop code generation leads to physical hallucinations lacking dynamic fidelity. We introduce Code2Worlds, a framework that formulates 4D generation as language-to-simulation code generation. First, we propose a dual-stream architecture that disentangles retrieval-augmented object generation from hierarchical environmental orchestration. Second, to ensure dynamic fidelity, we establish a physics-aware closed-loop mechanism in which a PostProcess Agent scripts dynamics, coupled with a VLM-Motion Critic that performs self-reflection to iteratively refine simulation code. Evaluations on the Code4D benchmark show Code2Worlds outperforms baselines with a 41% SGS gain and 49% higher Richness, while uniquely generating physics-aware dynamics absent in prior static methods. Code: https://github.com/AIGeeksGroup/Code2Worlds. Website: https://aigeeksgroup.github.io/Code2Worlds.

摘要（中文）: 实现空间智能需要超越视觉合理性，构建基于物理定律的世界模拟器。尽管编码大语言模型在静态3D场景生成方面取得了进展，但将这种范式扩展到4D动态仍然是一个关键前沿。这项任务提出了两个根本性挑战：多尺度上下文纠缠，其中单体生成无法平衡局部对象结构与全局环境布局；以及语义-物理执行鸿沟，其中开环代码生成导致缺乏动态保真度的物理幻觉。我们引入了Code2Worlds，一个将4D生成形式化为语言到模拟代码生成的框架。首先，我们提出了一种双流架构，将检索增强的对象生成与分层环境编排分离。其次，为了确保动态保真度，我们建立了一个物理感知闭环机制，其中一个后处理代理编写动力学脚本，并结合一个VLM-运动评论家执行自我反思以迭代地细化模拟代码。在Code4D基准上的评估表明，Code2Worlds优于基线，SGS增益高达41%，丰富度提高了49%，同时独特地生成了现有静态方法中不存在的物理感知动态。代码：https://github.com/AIGeeksGroup/Code2Worlds。网站：https://aigeeksgroup.github.io/Code2Worlds。

What if Agents Could Imagine? Reinforcing Open-Vocabulary HOI Comprehension through Generation

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models have shown promising capabilities in bridging visual and textual reasoning, yet their reasoning capabilities in Open-Vocabulary Human-Object Interaction (OV-HOI) are limited by cross-modal hallucinations and occlusion-induced ambiguity. To address this, we propose \textbf{ImagineAgent}, an agentic framework that harmonizes cognitive reasoning with generative imagination for robust visual understanding. Specifically, our method innovatively constructs cognitive maps that explicitly model plausible relationships between detected entities and candidate actions. Subsequently, it dynamically invokes tools including retrieval augmentation, image cropping, and diffusion models to gather domain-specific knowledge and enriched visual evidence, thereby achieving cross-modal alignment in ambiguous scenarios. Moreover, we propose a composite reward that balances prediction accuracy and tool efficiency. Evaluations on SWIG-HOI and HICO-DET datasets demonstrate our SOTA performance, requiring approximately 20\% of training data compared to existing methods, validating our robustness and efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型在桥接视觉和文本推理方面展现出令人鼓舞的能力，但它们在开放词汇人类-物体交互(OV-HOI)中的推理能力受到跨模态幻觉和遮挡引起的歧义性的限制。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 \textbf{ImagineAgent}，一个代理框架，它协调认知推理和生成想象，以实现稳健的视觉理解。具体而言，我们的方法创新性地构建了认知地图，该地图显式地建模了检测到的实体与候选动作之间可能的关系。随后，它动态地调用包括检索增强、图像裁剪和扩散模型在内的工具，以收集特定领域的知识和丰富的视觉证据，从而在模糊场景中实现跨模态对齐。此外，我们提出了一种复合奖励，以平衡预测准确性和工具效率。 在SWIG-HOI和HICO-DET数据集上的评估表明我们实现了SOTA性能，与现有方法相比，只需要约20\%的训练数据，验证了我们的鲁棒性和效率。

PhyCritic: Multimodal Critic Models for Physical AI

Abstract (English): With the rapid development of large multimodal models, reliable judge and critic models have become essential for open-ended evaluation and preference alignment, providing pairwise preferences, numerical scores, and explanatory justifications for assessing model-generated responses. However, existing critics are primarily trained in general visual domains such as captioning or image question answering, leaving physical AI tasks involving perception, causal reasoning, and planning largely underexplored. We introduce PhyCritic, a multimodal critic model optimized for physical AI through a two-stage RLVR pipeline: a physical skill warmup stage that enhances physically oriented perception and reasoning, followed by self-referential critic finetuning, where the critic generates its own prediction as an internal reference before judging candidate responses, improving judgment stability and physical correctness. Across both physical and general-purpose multimodal judge benchmarks, PhyCritic achieves strong performance gains over open-source baselines and, when applied as a policy model, further improves perception and reasoning in physically grounded tasks.

摘要（中文）: 随着大型多模态模型的飞速发展，可靠的评判模型和评论模型对于开放式评估和偏好对齐变得至关重要，它们为评估模型生成的回应提供成对偏好、数值评分和解释性理由。然而，现有的评论模型主要在一般的视觉领域进行训练，例如图像描述或图像问答，使得涉及感知、因果推理和规划的物理人工智能任务在很大程度上未被探索。我们引入了PhyCritic，一种针对物理人工智能优化的多模态评论模型，通过两阶段的RLVR流程实现：一个物理技能预热阶段，增强面向物理的感知和推理能力；随后是自指式的评论微调，评论模型在评判候选回应之前，首先生成其自身的预测作为内部参考，从而提高评判的稳定性和物理正确性。在物理和通用多模态评判基准测试中，PhyCritic相较于开源基线取得了显著的性能提升，并且当应用于策略模型时，进一步提升了物理具身任务中的感知和推理能力。

TLDR: PhyCritic is a multimodal critic model tailored for physical AI tasks, trained using a two-stage RLVR pipeline, demonstrating performance gains in both physical and general domains.

Authors: Tianyi Xiong, Shihao Wang, Guilin Liu, Yi Dong, Ming Li, Heng Huang, Jan Kautz, Zhiding Yu

Geometry of Uncertainty: Learning Metric Spaces for Multimodal State Estimation in RL

Abstract (English): Estimating the state of an environment from high-dimensional, multimodal, and noisy observations is a fundamental challenge in reinforcement learning (RL). Traditional approaches rely on probabilistic models to account for the uncertainty, but often require explicit noise assumptions, in turn limiting generalization. In this work, we contribute a novel method to learn a structured latent representation, in which distances between states directly correlate with the minimum number of actions required to transition between them. The proposed metric space formulation provides a geometric interpretation of uncertainty without the need for explicit probabilistic modeling. To achieve this, we introduce a multimodal latent transition model and a sensor fusion mechanism based on inverse distance weighting, allowing for the adaptive integration of multiple sensor modalities without prior knowledge of noise distributions. We empirically validate the approach on a range of multimodal RL tasks, demonstrating improved robustness to sensor noise and superior state estimation compared to baseline methods. Our experiments show enhanced performance of an RL agent via the learned representation, eliminating the need of explicit noise augmentation. The presented results suggest that leveraging transition-aware metric spaces provides a principled and scalable solution for robust state estimation in sequential decision-making.

摘要（中文）: 从高维、多模态和噪声观测中估计环境状态是强化学习（RL）中的一个根本挑战。传统方法依赖概率模型来处理不确定性，但通常需要显式的噪声假设，反过来限制了泛化能力。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新的方法来学习结构化的潜在表示，其中状态之间的距离直接与状态间转换所需的最少动作次数相关。所提出的度量空间公式提供了不确定性的几何解释，而无需显式的概率建模。为了实现这一点，我们引入了一种多模态潜在转换模型和一个基于反距离加权的传感器融合机制，允许自适应地整合多种传感器模态，而无需预先了解噪声分布。我们在一系列多模态RL任务上进行了实证验证，证明了该方法在传感器噪声方面的改进的鲁棒性，并且与基准方法相比具有更优越的状态估计能力。我们的实验表明，通过学习到的表示，强化学习智能体的性能得到了提升，消除了对显式噪声增强的需求。提出的结果表明，利用转换感知度量空间为顺序决策中的鲁棒状态估计提供了一种有原则且可扩展的解决方案。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel method for learning a metric space representation for state estimation in RL, where state distances correlate with transition costs, improving robustness to sensor noise and eliminating the need for explicit noise augmentation.

Authors: Alfredo Reichlin, Adriano Pacciarelli, Danica Kragic, Miguel Vasco

From Path Signatures to Sequential Modeling: Incremental Signature Contributions for Offline RL

Abstract (English): Path signatures embed trajectories into tensor algebra and constitute a universal, non-parametric representation of paths; however, in the standard form, they collapse temporal structure into a single global object, which limits their suitability for decision-making problems that require step-wise reactivity. We propose the Incremental Signature Contribution (ISC) method, which decomposes truncated path signatures into a temporally ordered sequence of elements in the tensor-algebra space, corresponding to incremental contributions induced by last path increments. This reconstruction preserves the algebraic structure and expressivity of signatures, while making their internal temporal evolution explicit, enabling processing signature-based representations via sequential modeling approaches. In contrast to full signatures, ISC is inherently sensitive to instantaneous trajectory updates, which is critical for sensitive and stability-requiring control dynamics. Building on this representation, we introduce ISC-Transformer (ISCT), an offline reinforcement learning model that integrates ISC into a standard Transformer architecture without further architectural modification. We evaluate ISCT on HalfCheetah, Walker2d, Hopper, and Maze2d, including settings with delayed rewards and downgraded datasets. The results demonstrate that ISC method provides a theoretically grounded and practically effective alternative to path processing for temporally sensitive control tasks.

摘要（中文）: 路径签名将轨迹嵌入到张量代数中，构成了一种通用的非参数路径表示；然而，在标准形式下，它们将时间结构折叠成单个全局对象，这限制了它们在需要逐步反应的决策问题中的适用性。我们提出增量签名贡献（ISC）方法，该方法将截断的路径签名分解为张量代数空间中按时间排序的元素序列，对应于由最后路径增量引起的增量贡献。这种重构保留了签名的代数结构和表达能力，同时使其内部时间演化显式化，从而能够通过序列建模方法处理基于签名的表示。与完整签名相比，ISC本质上对瞬时轨迹更新敏感，这对于敏感和需要稳定性的控制动力学至关重要。在此表示的基础上，我们引入了ISC-Transformer（ISCT），这是一种离线强化学习模型，它将ISC集成到标准的Transformer架构中，而无需进一步的架构修改。我们在HalfCheetah、Walker2d、Hopper和Maze2d上评估了ISCT，包括具有延迟奖励和降级数据集的设置。结果表明，ISC方法为时间敏感的控制任务提供了一种理论上有根据且实践中有效的路径处理替代方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces Incremental Signature Contribution (ISC), a method to decompose path signatures into a temporally ordered sequence, and applies it to offline reinforcement learning with an ISC-Transformer (ISCT) model, showing improved performance on temporally sensitive control tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了增量签名贡献(ISC)方法，将路径签名分解为时间排序的序列，并将其应用于离线强化学习中，通过ISC-Transformer (ISCT)模型在时间敏感的控制任务上展现了性能提升。

Authors: Ziyi Zhao, Qingchuan Li, Yuxuan Xu

Temperature as a Meta-Policy: Adaptive Temperature in LLM Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Temperature is a crucial hyperparameter in large language models (LLMs), controlling the trade-off between exploration and exploitation during text generation. High temperatures encourage diverse but noisy outputs, while low temperatures produce focused outputs but may cause premature convergence. Yet static or heuristic temperature schedules fail to adapt to the dynamic demands of reinforcement learning (RL) throughout training, often limiting policy improvement. We propose Temperature Adaptive Meta Policy Optimization (TAMPO), a new framework that recasts temperature control as a learnable meta-policy. TAMPO operates through a hierarchical two-loop process. In the inner loop, the LLM policy is updated (e.g., using GRPO) with trajectories sampled at the temperature selected by the meta-policy. In the outer loop, meta-policy updates the distribution over candidate temperatures by rewarding those that maximize the likelihood of high-advantage trajectories. This trajectory-guided, reward-driven mechanism enables online adaptation without additional rollouts, directly aligning exploration with policy improvement. On five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, TAMPO outperforms baselines using fixed or heuristic temperatures, establishing temperature as an effective learnable meta-policy for adaptive exploration in LLM reinforcement learning. Accepted at ICLR 2026.

摘要（中文）: 温度是大型语言模型 (LLM) 中的一个关键超参数，它控制文本生成过程中探索与利用之间的权衡。高温鼓励生成多样但嘈杂的输出，而低温产生聚焦的输出，但可能导致过早收敛。然而，静态或启发式温度调整策略无法适应强化学习 (RL) 在整个训练过程中的动态需求，通常会限制策略改进。我们提出了温度自适应元策略优化 (TAMPO)，这是一个新的框架，将温度控制重新定义为一个可学习的元策略。TAMPO 通过一个分层的双循环过程运行。在内循环中，LLM 策略（例如，使用 GRPO）会根据由元策略选择的温度采样的轨迹进行更新。在外循环中，元策略通过奖励那些最大化高优势轨迹可能性的温度来更新候选温度的分布。这种轨迹引导的、奖励驱动的机制能够实现在线自适应，而无需额外的 rollout，从而直接将探索与策略改进对齐。在五个数学推理基准测试中，TAMPO 优于使用固定或启发式温度的基线，确立了温度作为 LLM 强化学习中自适应探索的有效可学习元策略的地位。文章已被 ICLR 2026 接收。

TLDR: The paper introduces Temperature Adaptive Meta Policy Optimization (TAMPO), a framework that learns to dynamically adjust the temperature hyperparameter in LLM reinforcement learning via a meta-policy, outperforming fixed or heuristic temperature baselines on mathematical reasoning tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为温度自适应元策略优化 (TAMPO) 的框架，该框架通过元策略学习动态调整 LLM 强化学习中的温度超参数，在数学推理任务中优于固定或启发式温度基线。

Authors: Haoran Dang, Cuiling Lan, Hai Wan, Xibin Zhao, Yan Lu

SkillRater: Untangling Capabilities in Multimodal Data

Abstract (English): Data curation methods typically assign samples a single quality score. We argue this scalar framing is fundamentally limited: when training requires multiple distinct capabilities, a monolithic scorer cannot maximize useful signals for all of them simultaneously. Quality is better understood as multidimensional, with each dimension corresponding to a capability the model must acquire. We introduce SkillRater, a framework that decomposes data filtering into specialized raters - one per capability, each trained via meta-learning on a disjoint validation objective - and composes their scores through a progressive selection rule: at each training stage, a sample is retained if any rater ranks it above a threshold that tightens over time, preserving diversity early while concentrating on high-value samples late. We validate this approach on vision language models, decomposing quality into three capability dimensions: visual understanding, OCR, and STEM reasoning. At 2B parameters, SkillRater improves over unfiltered baselines by 5.63% on visual understanding, 2.00% on OCR, and 3.53% on STEM on held out benchmarks. The learned rater signals are near orthogonal, confirming that the decomposition captures genuinely independent quality dimensions and explaining why it outperforms both unfiltered training and monolithic learned filtering.

摘要（中文）: 数据整理方法通常为样本分配一个单一的质量评分。我们认为这种标量框架具有根本性的局限性：当训练需要多种不同的能力时，一个单一的评分器无法同时最大化所有这些能力的有用信号。质量最好被理解为多维的，其中每个维度对应于模型必须获得的一种能力。我们引入了SkillRater，一个将数据过滤分解为专门的评分器的框架——每个能力对应一个评分器，每个评分器通过元学习在不相交的验证目标上进行训练——并通过逐步选择规则组合它们的得分：在每个训练阶段，如果任何评分器将样本的排名置于随着时间推移而收紧的阈值之上，则保留该样本，从而在早期保持多样性，同时在后期集中于高价值的样本。我们在视觉语言模型上验证了这种方法，将质量分解为三个能力维度：视觉理解、光学字符识别(OCR)和科学、技术、工程和数学(STEM)推理。在20亿参数规模下，SkillRater在保留的基准测试集上，相比于未过滤的基线，在视觉理解方面提升了5.63%，在OCR方面提升了2.00%，在STEM方面提升了3.53%。学习到的评分器信号近乎正交，证实了这种分解捕捉到了真正独立的质量维度，并解释了为什么它优于未过滤的训练和单体的学习型过滤。

TLDR: The paper introduces SkillRater, a meta-learning framework for data filtering in multimodal contexts that decomposes quality into capability-specific raters and progressively selects data based on these ratings, demonstrating improved performance on vision-language tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍 SkillRater，一个用于多模态数据过滤的元学习框架，它将数据质量分解为特定于能力的评分器，并根据这些评分逐步选择数据，从而在视觉语言任务中表现出改进的性能。

Authors: Naveen Sahi, Jeremy Dohmann, Armen Aghajanyan, Akshat Shrivastava

Unifying Stable Optimization and Reference Regularization in RLHF

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) has advanced alignment capabilities significantly but remains hindered by two core challenges: \textbf{reward hacking} and \textbf{stable optimization}. Current solutions independently address these issues through separate regularization strategies, specifically a KL-divergence penalty against a supervised fine-tuned model ($π_0$) to mitigate reward hacking, and policy ratio clipping towards the current policy ($π_t$) to promote stable alignment. However, the implicit trade-off arising from simultaneously regularizing towards both $π_0$ and $π_t$ remains under-explored. In this paper, we introduce a unified regularization approach that explicitly balances the objectives of preventing reward hacking and maintaining stable policy updates. Our simple yet principled alignment objective yields a weighted supervised fine-tuning loss with a superior trade-off, which demonstrably improves both alignment results and implementation complexity. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks validate that our method consistently outperforms RLHF and online preference learning methods, achieving enhanced alignment performance and stability.

摘要（中文）: 基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）显著提升了对齐能力，但仍然受到两个核心挑战的制约：\textbf{奖励入侵}和\textbf{稳定优化}。目前的解决方案通过独立的正则化策略分别解决这些问题，具体来说，使用相对于监督式微调模型（$π_0$）的KL散度惩罚来缓解奖励入侵，并使用相对于当前策略（$π_t$）的策略比例裁剪来促进稳定的对齐。然而，同时向$π_0$和$π_t$正则化所产生的隐式权衡仍未得到充分探讨。在本文中，我们提出了一种统一的正则化方法，该方法明确地平衡了防止奖励入侵和维持稳定策略更新的目标。我们简单而有原则的对齐目标产生了一种具有更优权衡的加权监督式微调损失，这明显改善了对齐结果和实现复杂性。跨多个基准的大量实验验证了我们的方法始终优于RLHF和在线偏好学习方法，实现了增强的对齐性能和稳定性。

TLDR: This paper proposes a unified regularization approach for RLHF that balances reward hacking prevention and stable policy updates, outperforming existing methods in alignment performance and stability.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于RLHF的统一正则化方法，该方法平衡了防止奖励黑客行为和稳定策略更新，在对齐性能和稳定性方面优于现有方法。

Authors: Li He, Qiang Qu, He Zhao, Stephen Wan, Dadong Wang, Lina Yao, Tongliang Liu

Asymmetric Prompt Weighting for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has driven recent advances in LLM post-training, in particular for reasoning. Policy optimization algorithms generate a number of responses for a given prompt and then effectively weight the corresponding gradients depending on the rewards. The most popular algorithms including GRPO, DAPO, and RLOO focus on ambiguous prompts, i.e., prompts with intermediate success probability, while downgrading gradients with very easy and very hard prompts. In this paper, we consider asymmetric prompt weightings that assign higher weights to prompts with low, or even zero, empirical success probability. We find that asymmetric weighting particularly benefits from-scratch RL (as in R1-Zero), where training traverses a wide accuracy range, and less so in post-SFT RL where the model already starts at high accuracy. We also provide theory that characterizes prompt weights which minimize the time needed to raise success probability from an initial level to a target accuracy under a fixed update budget. In low-success regimes, where informative responses are rare and response cost dominates, these optimal weights become asymmetric, upweighting low success probabilities and thereby accelerating effective-time convergence.

摘要（中文）: 使用可验证奖励的强化学习推动了LLM后训练的最新进展，尤其是在推理方面。策略优化算法为给定的提示生成多个回复，然后根据奖励有效地加权相应的梯度。包括GRPO、DAPO和RLOO在内的最流行的算法专注于具有中间成功概率的模糊提示，同时降低非常容易和非常困难的提示的梯度。在本文中，我们考虑了不对称的提示加权，该加权方式为具有较低甚至零经验成功概率的提示分配更高的权重。我们发现不对称加权特别有利于从头开始的强化学习（如R1-Zero），其中训练遍历了广泛的准确率范围，而在后SFT强化学习中，由于模型已经从高准确率开始，效果较小。我们还提供了理论，用于表征在固定更新预算下，将成功概率从初始水平提高到目标精度所需时间最小化的提示权重。在低成功率的情况下，信息丰富的回复很少且回复成本占主导地位，这些最优权重变为不对称，提高低成功概率的权重，从而加速有效时间的收敛。

TLDR: This paper explores asymmetric prompt weighting in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, showing performance improvements, especially in from-scratch RL settings where initial success rates are low, and providing theory to justify their approach.

简要说明: 本文探讨了在带有可验证奖励的强化学习中采用非对称提示权重，结果表明此方法，特别是在初始成功率较低的从零开始强化学习设置中，能提高性能，并提供了理论依据来支持他们的方法。

Authors: Reinhard Heckel, Mahdi Soltanolkotabi, Christos Thramboulidis

Pack it in: Packing into Partially Filled Containers Through Contact

Abstract (English): The automation of warehouse operations is crucial for improving productivity and reducing human exposure to hazardous environments. One operation frequently performed in warehouses is bin-packing where items need to be placed into containers, either for delivery to a customer, or for temporary storage in the warehouse. Whilst prior bin-packing works have largely been focused on packing items into empty containers and have adopted collision-free strategies, it is often the case that containers will already be partially filled with items, often in suboptimal arrangements due to transportation about a warehouse. This paper presents a contact-aware packing approach that exploits purposeful interactions with previously placed objects to create free space and enable successful placement of new items. This is achieved by using a contact-based multi-object trajectory optimizer within a model predictive controller, integrated with a physics-aware perception system that estimates object poses even during inevitable occlusions, and a method that suggests physically-feasible locations to place the object inside the container.

摘要（中文）: 仓库运营的自动化对于提高生产效率和减少人员在危险环境中的暴露至关重要。装箱是仓库中经常执行的一项操作，需要将物品放入容器中，以便交付给客户，或在仓库中进行临时存储。 虽然先前的装箱工作主要集中在将物品装入空容器，并采用无碰撞策略，但实际情况往往是容器已经部分装填了物品，而且由于在仓库中运输，这些物品通常以次优方式排列。本文提出了一种接触感知的装箱方法，该方法利用与先前放置的物体进行有目的的交互来创造自由空间，从而能够成功放置新的物品。 这是通过在模型预测控制器中，采用一个基于接触的多目标轨迹优化器实现的，该控制器与一个具备物理感知能力的感知系统集成，该系统即使在不可避免的遮挡情况下也能估计物体姿态，并且采用一种方法来建议在容器内部放置物体的物理可行位置。

TLDR: This paper presents a contact-aware bin-packing approach for partially filled containers using a multi-object trajectory optimizer and physics-aware perception, addressing a common problem in warehouse automation.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于部分填充容器的接触感知式装箱方法，该方法使用多目标轨迹优化器和具有物理感知能力的感知系统，解决了仓库自动化中的一个常见问题。

Authors: David Russell, Zisong Xu, Maximo A. Roa, Mehmet Dogar

RF-Modulated Adaptive Communication Improves Multi-Agent Robotic Exploration

Abstract (English): Reliable coordination and efficient communication are critical challenges for multi-agent robotic exploration of environments where communication is limited. This work introduces Adaptive-RF Transmission (ART), a novel communication-aware planning algorithm that dynamically modulates transmission location based on signal strength and data payload size, enabling heterogeneous robot teams to share information efficiently without unnecessary backtracking. We further explore an extension to this approach called ART-SST, which enforces signal strength thresholds for high-fidelity data delivery. Through over 480 simulations across three cave-inspired environments, ART consistently outperforms existing strategies, including full rendezvous and minimum-signal heuristic approaches, achieving up to a 58% reduction in distance traveled and up to 52% faster exploration times compared to baseline methods. These results demonstrate that adaptive, payload-aware communication significantly improves coverage efficiency and mission speed in complex, communication-constrained environments, offering a promising foundation for future planetary exploration and search-and-rescue missions.

摘要（中文）: 以下是在环境受限的通信条件下，多智能体机器人探索中可靠的协调和高效的通信所面临的关键挑战。本文介绍了一种名为自适应射频传输(ART)的新型通信感知规划算法，该算法基于信号强度和数据负载大小动态地调节传输位置，使异构机器人团队能够高效地共享信息，而无需不必要的回溯。我们进一步探索了这种方法的扩展版本ART-SST，它对高保真数据传输强制执行信号强度阈值。通过在三个受洞穴启发的环境中进行的480多次模拟，ART始终优于现有的策略，包括完全汇合和最小信号启发式方法，与基线方法相比，行程距离最多减少58%，探索时间最多缩短52%。这些结果表明，自适应的、负载感知的通信显著提高了复杂、通信受限环境中的覆盖效率和任务速度，为未来的行星探索和搜索救援任务提供了一个有希望的基础。

TLDR: The paper introduces Adaptive-RF Transmission (ART), a communication-aware planning algorithm that dynamically modulates transmission for multi-agent robotic exploration in communication-limited environments, achieving significant improvements in exploration efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种自适应射频传输（ART）算法，该算法是一种通信感知规划算法，可动态调节多智能体机器人在通信受限环境中进行探索的传输，从而显著提高探索效率。

Authors: Lorin Achey, Breanne Crockett, Christoffer Heckman, Bradley Hayes

Where Bits Matter in World Model Planning: A Paired Mixed-Bit Study for Efficient Spatial Reasoning

Abstract (English): Efficient spatial reasoning requires world models that remain reliable under tight precision budgets. We study whether low-bit planning behavior is determined mostly by total bitwidth or by where bits are allocated across modules. Using DINO-WM on the Wall planning task, we run a paired-goal mixed-bit evaluation across uniform, mixed, asymmetric, and layerwise variants under two planner budgets. We observe a consistent three-regime pattern: 8-bit and 6-bit settings remain close to FP16, 3-bit settings collapse, and 4-bit settings are allocation-sensitive. In that transition region, preserving encoder precision improves planning relative to uniform quantization, and near-size asymmetric variants show the same encoder-side direction. In a later strict 22-cell replication with smaller per-cell episode count, the mixed-versus-uniform INT4 sign becomes budget-conditioned, which further highlights the sensitivity of this transition regime. These findings motivate module-aware, budget-aware quantization policies as a broader research direction for efficient spatial reasoning. Code and run artifacts are available at https://github.com/suraj-ranganath/DINO-MBQuant.

摘要（中文）: 高效的空间推理需要能在严格的精度预算下保持可靠性的世界模型。我们研究了低比特规划行为主要由总比特宽度决定，还是由比特在模块之间的分配方式决定。在使用DINO-WM进行Wall规划任务时，我们在两种规划器预算下，对均匀、混合、不对称和逐层变体进行了配对目标混合比特评估。我们观察到了一致的三种模式：8比特和6比特设置与FP16保持接近，3比特设置崩溃，而4比特设置对分配敏感。在那个过渡区域中，与均匀量化相比，保留编码器精度可以改善规划，并且近似大小的不对称变体显示出相同的编码器侧方向。在之后一个更严格的、每个单元格episode计数更少的22单元格复制实验中，混合与均匀INT4的符号变得受预算限制，这进一步突出了该过渡区域的敏感性。这些发现激发了模块感知、预算感知的量化策略作为高效空间推理更广泛的研究方向。代码和运行结果已在https://github.com/suraj-ranganath/DINO-MBQuant 提供。

TLDR: This paper investigates the impact of bit allocation strategies on the performance of world model-based planning, finding that encoder precision is crucial in low-bit regimes and highlighting the need for budget-aware quantization policies.
