Authors: Suraj Ranganath, Anish Patnaik, Vaishak Menon

DiffPlace: Street View Generation via Place-Controllable Diffusion Model Enhancing Place Recognition

Abstract (English): Generative models have advanced significantly in realistic image synthesis, with diffusion models excelling in quality and stability. Recent multi-view diffusion models improve 3D-aware street view generation, but they struggle to produce place-aware and background-consistent urban scenes from text, BEV maps, and object bounding boxes. This limits their effectiveness in generating realistic samples for place recognition tasks. To address these challenges, we propose DiffPlace, a novel framework that introduces a place-ID controller to enable place-controllable multi-view image generation. The place-ID controller employs linear projection, perceiver transformer, and contrastive learning to map place-ID embeddings into a fixed CLIP space, allowing the model to synthesize images with consistent background buildings while flexibly modifying foreground objects and weather conditions. Extensive experiments, including quantitative comparisons and augmented training evaluations, demonstrate that DiffPlace outperforms existing methods in both generation quality and training support for visual place recognition. Our results highlight the potential of generative models in enhancing scene-level and place-aware synthesis, providing a valuable approach for improving place recognition in autonomous driving

摘要（中文）: 生成模型在逼真图像合成方面取得了显著进展，其中扩散模型在质量和稳定性方面表现出色。近期的多视角扩散模型改进了3D感知的街景生成，但它们难以从文本、鸟瞰图（BEV）和物体边界框生成具有场所感知和背景一致的城市场景。这限制了它们在为场所识别任务生成逼真样本方面的有效性。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出DiffPlace，一种新颖的框架，引入了一个场所ID控制器，以实现场所可控的多视角图像生成。场所ID控制器采用线性投影、感知器Transformer和对比学习，将场所ID嵌入映射到固定的CLIP空间中，从而使模型能够合成具有一致背景建筑物的图像，同时灵活地修改前景物体和天气条件。包括定量比较和增强训练评估在内的大量实验表明，DiffPlace在生成质量和视觉场所识别的训练支持方面均优于现有方法。我们的结果突显了生成模型在增强场景级别和场所感知合成方面的潜力，为改进自动驾驶中的场所识别提供了一种有价值的方法。

TLDR: DiffPlace introduces a place-ID controller for diffusion models to generate place-aware street view images, improving both generation quality and place recognition performance.

Authors: Ji Li, Zhiwei Li, Shihao Li, Zhenjiang Yu, Boyang Wang, Haiou Liu

AC-MASAC: An Attentive Curriculum Learning Framework for Heterogeneous UAV Swarm Coordination

Abstract (English): Cooperative path planning for heterogeneous UAV swarms poses significant challenges for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL), particularly in handling asymmetric inter-agent dependencies and addressing the risks of sparse rewards and catastrophic forgetting during training. To address these issues, this paper proposes an attentive curriculum learning framework (AC-MASAC). The framework introduces a role-aware heterogeneous attention mechanism to explicitly model asymmetric dependencies. Moreover, a structured curriculum strategy is designed, integrating hierarchical knowledge transfer and stage-proportional experience replay to address the issues of sparse rewards and catastrophic forgetting. The proposed framework is validated on a custom multi-agent simulation platform, and the results show that our method has significant advantages over other advanced methods in terms of Success Rate, Formation Keeping Rate, and Success-weighted Mission Time. The code is available at \textcolor{red}{https://github.com/Wanhao-Liu/AC-MASAC}.

摘要（中文）: 异构无人机集群的协同路径规划对多智能体强化学习(MARL)提出了重大挑战，尤其是在处理非对称智能体间依赖关系以及解决训练过程中稀疏奖励和灾难性遗忘的风险方面。为了解决这些问题，本文提出了一种基于注意力机制的课程学习框架(AC-MASAC)。该框架引入了一种角色感知的异构注意力机制来显式地建模非对称依赖关系。此外，设计了一种结构化的课程策略，集成了分层知识迁移和阶段比例经验回放，以解决稀疏奖励和灾难性遗忘的问题。所提出的框架在一个定制的多智能体仿真平台上得到了验证，结果表明，在成功率、队形保持率和成功加权任务时间方面，我们的方法优于其他先进方法。代码可在\textcolor{red}{https://github.com/Wanhao-Liu/AC-MASAC}获取。

Authors: Wanhao Liu, Junhong Dai, Yixuan Zhang, Shengyun Yin, Panshuo Li

Human-Like Gaze Behavior in Social Robots: A Deep Learning Approach Integrating Human and Non-Human Stimuli

Abstract (English): Nonverbal behaviors, particularly gaze direction, play a crucial role in enhancing effective communication in social interactions. As social robots increasingly participate in these interactions, they must adapt their gaze based on human activities and remain receptive to all cues, whether human-generated or not, to ensure seamless and effective communication. This study aims to increase the similarity between robot and human gaze behavior across various social situations, including both human and non-human stimuli (e.g., conversations, pointing, door openings, and object drops). A key innovation in this study, is the investigation of gaze responses to non-human stimuli, a critical yet underexplored area in prior research. These scenarios, were simulated in the Unity software as a 3D animation and a 360-degree real-world video. Data on gaze directions from 41 participants were collected via virtual reality (VR) glasses. Preprocessed data, trained two neural networks-LSTM and Transformer-to build predictive models based on individuals' gaze patterns. In the animated scenario, the LSTM and Transformer models achieved prediction accuracies of 67.6% and 70.4%, respectively; In the real-world scenario, the LSTM and Transformer models achieved accuracies of 72% and 71.6%, respectively. Despite the gaze pattern differences among individuals, our models outperform existing approaches in accuracy while uniquely considering non-human stimuli, offering a significant advantage over previous literature. Furthermore, deployed on the NAO robot, the system was evaluated by 275 participants via a comprehensive questionnaire, with results demonstrating high satisfaction during interactions. This work advances social robotics by enabling robots to dynamically mimic human gaze behavior in complex social contexts.

摘要（中文）: 非语言行为，尤其是视线方向，在增强社交互动中的有效沟通方面起着至关重要的作用。随着社交机器人越来越多地参与这些互动，它们必须根据人类活动调整视线，并对所有人为和非人为的线索保持敏感，以确保无缝和有效的沟通。本研究旨在提高机器人在各种社交情境中与人类视线行为的相似度，这些情境包括人与非人的刺激（例如，对话、指点、开门和掉落物体）。本研究的一个关键创新是调查对非人类刺激的视线反应，这是先前研究中一个关键但未被充分探索的领域。这些场景在Unity软件中模拟成3D动画和360度真实世界视频。通过虚拟现实（VR）眼镜收集了41名参与者的视线方向数据。预处理后的数据用于训练两个神经网络——LSTM和Transformer——以基于个体视线模式构建预测模型。在动画场景中，LSTM和Transformer模型的预测准确率分别为67.6%和70.4%；在真实世界场景中，LSTM和Transformer模型的准确率分别为72%和71.6%。尽管个体之间的视线模式存在差异，但我们的模型在准确性方面优于现有方法，同时独特地考虑了非人类刺激，从而提供了优于先前文献的显著优势。 此外，该系统部署在NAO机器人上，并通过一份全面的问卷由275名参与者进行评估，结果表明在互动过程中满意度很高。这项工作通过使机器人能够在复杂的社交环境中动态地模仿人类的视线行为，从而推进了社交机器人技术的发展。

TLDR: This paper presents a deep learning approach (LSTM & Transformer) for mimicking human-like gaze behavior in social robots, especially focusing on responses to both human and non-human stimuli in VR and real-world scenarios, and demonstrates improved accuracy and user satisfaction compared to existing methods.

Authors: Faezeh Vahedi, Morteza Memari, Ramtin Tabatabaei, Alireza Taheri

EasyMimic: A Low-Cost Framework for Robot Imitation Learning from Human Videos

Abstract (English): Robot imitation learning is often hindered by the high cost of collecting large-scale, real-world data. This challenge is especially significant for low-cost robots designed for home use, as they must be both user-friendly and affordable. To address this, we propose the EasyMimic framework, a low-cost and replicable solution that enables robots to quickly learn manipulation policies from human video demonstrations captured with standard RGB cameras. Our method first extracts 3D hand trajectories from the videos. An action alignment module then maps these trajectories to the gripper control space of a low-cost robot. To bridge the human-to-robot domain gap, we introduce a simple and user-friendly hand visual augmentation strategy. We then use a co-training method, fine-tuning a model on both the processed human data and a small amount of robot data, enabling rapid adaptation to new tasks. Experiments on the low-cost LeRobot platform demonstrate that EasyMimic achieves high performance across various manipulation tasks. It significantly reduces the reliance on expensive robot data collection, offering a practical path for bringing intelligent robots into homes. Project website: https://zt375356.github.io/EasyMimic-Project/.

摘要（中文）: 机器人模仿学习常常受限于收集大规模真实世界数据的巨大成本。对于为家庭使用而设计的低成本机器人而言，这一挑战尤为显著，因为它们必须兼具用户友好性和经济性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了EasyMimic框架，一种低成本且可复现的解决方案，使机器人能够通过标准RGB摄像头捕获的人类视频演示快速学习操作策略。我们的方法首先从视频中提取3D手部轨迹。然后，一个动作对齐模块将这些轨迹映射到低成本机器人的夹爪控制空间。为了弥合人与机器人的领域差距，我们引入了一个简单且用户友好的手部视觉增强策略。接着，我们使用一种协同训练方法，在一个经过处理的人类数据和一个少量机器人数据上微调模型，从而实现对新任务的快速适应。在低成本LeRobot平台上的实验表明，EasyMimic在各种操作任务中都实现了高性能。它显著降低了对昂贵的机器人数据收集的依赖，为将智能机器人引入家庭提供了一条切实可行的途径。项目网站：https://zt375356.github.io/EasyMimic-Project/.

TLDR: The paper introduces EasyMimic, a low-cost framework for imitation learning on low-cost robots, leveraging human video demonstrations enhanced with 3D hand tracking and co-training to reduce the need for extensive robot data collection.

Authors: Tao Zhang, Song Xia, Ye Wang, Qin Jin

Human Preference Modeling Using Visual Motion Prediction Improves Robot Skill Learning from Egocentric Human Video

Abstract (English): We present an approach to robot learning from egocentric human videos by modeling human preferences in a reward function and optimizing robot behavior to maximize this reward. Prior work on reward learning from human videos attempts to measure the long-term value of a visual state as the temporal distance between it and the terminal state in a demonstration video. These approaches make assumptions that limit performance when learning from video. They must also transfer the learned value function across the embodiment and environment gap. Our method models human preferences by learning to predict the motion of tracked points between subsequent images and defines a reward function as the agreement between predicted and observed object motion in a robot's behavior at each step. We then use a modified Soft Actor Critic (SAC) algorithm initialized with 10 on-robot demonstrations to estimate a value function from this reward and optimize a policy that maximizes this value function, all on the robot. Our approach is capable of learning on a real robot, and we show that policies learned with our reward model match or outperform prior work across multiple tasks in both simulation and on the real robot.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种从以人为中心的视频中进行机器人学习的方法，该方法通过在奖励函数中建模人类偏好并优化机器人行为以最大化该奖励来实现。先前基于人类视频的奖励学习工作试图衡量视觉状态的长期价值，将其作为演示视频中该状态与终止状态之间的时间距离。这些方法做出的假设限制了从视频中学习的性能。它们还必须跨越具身性和环境的差距来迁移学习到的价值函数。我们的方法通过学习预测后续图像之间跟踪点的运动来建模人类偏好，并将奖励函数定义为机器人行为在每个步骤中预测的和观察到的对象运动之间的一致性。然后，我们使用一种改进的软演员-评论家 (SAC) 算法，并用10个机器人演示数据初始化，来估计来自该奖励的价值函数，并优化最大化该价值函数的策略，所有操作均在机器人上进行。我们的方法能够在真实机器人上进行学习，并且我们表明，使用我们的奖励模型学习到的策略在模拟和真实机器人上的多个任务中，都与先前的工作相匹配或超过了它们。

TLDR: This paper presents a method for robot learning from egocentric human videos by modeling human preferences as visual motion predictions. The learned reward function, based on motion agreement, is used to train a robot policy, outperforming prior methods in simulation and real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种通过将人类偏好建模为视觉运动预测，从以自我为中心的人类视频中进行机器人学习的方法。学习到的奖励函数基于运动一致性，用于训练机器人策略，在模拟和真实世界实验中优于先前的方法。

Authors: Mrinal Verghese, Christopher G. Atkeson

ExtremControl: Low-Latency Humanoid Teleoperation with Direct Extremity Control

Abstract (English): Building a low-latency humanoid teleoperation system is essential for collecting diverse reactive and dynamic demonstrations. However, existing approaches rely on heavily pre-processed human-to-humanoid motion retargeting and position-only PD control, resulting in substantial latency that severely limits responsiveness and prevents tasks requiring rapid feedback and fast reactions. To address this problem, we propose ExtremControl, a low latency whole-body control framework that: (1) operates directly on SE(3) poses of selected rigid links, primarily humanoid extremities, to avoid full-body retargeting; (2) utilizes a Cartesian-space mapping to directly convert human motion to humanoid link targets; and (3) incorporates velocity feedforward control at low level to support highly responsive behavior under rapidly changing control interfaces. We further provide a unified theoretical formulation of ExtremControl and systematically validate its effectiveness through experiments in both simulation and real-world environments. Building on ExtremControl, we implement a low-latency humanoid teleoperation system that supports both optical motion capture and VR-based motion tracking, achieving end-to-end latency as low as 50ms and enabling highly responsive behaviors such as ping-pong ball balancing, juggling, and real-time return, thereby substantially surpassing the 200ms latency limit observed in prior work.

摘要（中文）: 构建低延迟人形机器人遥操作系统对于收集多样化的反应式和动态演示至关重要。然而，现有方法依赖于大量预处理的人-机器人运动重定向和仅基于位置的PD控制，导致显著的延迟，严重限制了响应性，并阻碍了需要快速反馈和快速反应的任务。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了ExtremControl，一种低延迟全身控制框架，该框架：（1）直接操作选定刚性连杆（主要为人形机器人四肢）的SE(3)姿态，以避免全身重定向；（2）利用笛卡尔空间映射将人类运动直接转换为人形机器人连杆目标；（3）在低层次上融入速度前馈控制，以支持在快速变化的控制界面下实现高度响应的行为。我们进一步提供了ExtremControl的统一理论公式，并通过在模拟和现实环境中的实验系统地验证了其有效性。基于ExtremControl，我们实现了一个低延迟人形机器人遥操作系统，该系统支持光学运动捕捉和基于VR的运动跟踪，实现了低至50ms的端到端延迟，并实现了诸如乒乓球平衡、杂耍和实时回馈等高度响应的行为，从而大大超过了先前工作中观察到的200ms延迟限制。

TLDR: The paper introduces ExtremControl, a low-latency whole-body control framework for humanoid teleoperation that operates directly on extremity poses with velocity feedforward control, achieving significantly lower latency than prior methods and enabling more responsive behaviors.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ExtremControl，一种用于人形机器人遥操作的低延迟全身控制框架，该框架直接在肢体姿势上进行操作，并采用速度前馈控制，与之前的方法相比，显著降低了延迟，并实现了更灵敏的响应。

Authors: Ziyan Xiong, Lixing Fang, Junyun Huang, Kashu Yamazaki, Hao Zhang, Chuang Gan

YOR: Your Own Mobile Manipulator for Generalizable Robotics

Abstract (English): Recent advances in robot learning have generated significant interest in capable platforms that may eventually approach human-level competence. This interest, combined with the commoditization of actuators, has propelled growth in low-cost robotic platforms. However, the optimal form factor for mobile manipulation, especially on a budget, remains an open question. We introduce YOR, an open-source, low-cost mobile manipulator that integrates an omnidirectional base, a telescopic vertical lift, and two arms with grippers to achieve whole-body mobility and manipulation. Our design emphasizes modularity, ease of assembly using off-the-shelf components, and affordability, with a bill-of-materials cost under 10,000 USD. We demonstrate YOR's capability by completing tasks that require coordinated whole-body control, bimanual manipulation, and autonomous navigation. Overall, YOR offers competitive functionality for mobile manipulation research at a fraction of the cost of existing platforms. Project website: https://www.yourownrobot.ai/

摘要（中文）: 机器人学习领域的最新进展激发了人们对具有较高能力的平台（最终可能达到人类水平）的浓厚兴趣。这种兴趣，加上执行器商品化趋势，推动了低成本机器人平台的增长。然而，移动操作的最佳外形尺寸，尤其是在预算有限的情况下，仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。我们推出了YOR，一个开源、低成本的移动操作平台，它集成了全向底座、伸缩式垂直升降机构以及两个带有夹爪的机械臂，以实现全身移动和操作。我们的设计强调模块化、易于使用现成组件进行组装以及经济性，材料清单成本低于10,000美元。我们通过完成需要协调全身控制、双臂操作和自主导航的任务来展示YOR的能力。总而言之，YOR以现有平台一小部分的成本为移动操作研究提供了具有竞争力的功能。项目网站：https://www.yourownrobot.ai/

APEX: Learning Adaptive High-Platform Traversal for Humanoid Robots

Abstract (English): Humanoid locomotion has advanced rapidly with deep reinforcement learning (DRL), enabling robust feet-based traversal over uneven terrain. Yet platforms beyond leg length remain largely out of reach because current RL training paradigms often converge to jumping-like solutions that are high-impact, torque-limited, and unsafe for real-world deployment. To address this gap, we propose APEX, a system for perceptive, climbing-based high-platform traversal that composes terrain-conditioned behaviors: climb-up and climb-down at vertical edges, walking or crawling on the platform, and stand-up and lie-down for posture reconfiguration. Central to our approach is a generalized ratchet progress reward for learning contact-rich, goal-reaching maneuvers. It tracks the best-so-far task progress and penalizes non-improving steps, providing dense yet velocity-free supervision that enables efficient exploration under strong safety regularization. Based on this formulation, we train LiDAR-based full-body maneuver policies and reduce the sim-to-real perception gap through a dual strategy: modeling mapping artifacts during training and applying filtering and inpainting to elevation maps during deployment. Finally, we distill all six skills into a single policy that autonomously selects behaviors and transitions based on local geometry and commands. Experiments on a 29-DoF Unitree G1 humanoid demonstrate zero-shot sim-to-real traversal of 0.8 meter platforms (approximately 114% of leg length), with robust adaptation to platform height and initial pose, as well as smooth and stable multi-skill transitions.

摘要（中文）: 基于深度强化学习的人形机器人运动已经取得了快速进展，实现了在不平坦地形上基于足部的稳健穿越。然而，超出腿长范围的平台在很大程度上仍然无法到达，因为当前的强化学习训练范式通常收敛到跳跃式的解决方案，这些方案具有高冲击、扭矩受限的特点，并且不适用于现实世界的部署。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了APEX，一个用于感知的、基于攀爬的高平台穿越系统，该系统组合了地形条件下的行为：垂直边缘处的向上攀爬和向下攀爬、在平台上行走或爬行，以及用于姿态重构的站立和躺下。我们方法的核心是一种通用的棘轮式进度奖励，用于学习富含接触的、达到目标的动作。它跟踪到目前为止的最佳任务进度，并惩罚未改进的步骤，从而提供密集但无速度的监督，从而能够在强大的安全正则化下进行高效探索。基于此公式，我们训练了基于激光雷达的全身动作策略，并通过双重策略来减少模拟到现实的感知差距：在训练期间对地图伪像进行建模，并在部署期间对高程图应用滤波和修复。最后，我们将所有六个技能提炼成一个单一的策略，该策略根据局部几何形状和指令自主选择行为和执行转换。在一台29自由度的宇树G1人形机器人上的实验表明，实现了对0.8米平台（大约为腿长的114%）的零样本模拟到真实穿越，能够稳健地适应平台高度和初始姿势，并实现平滑和稳定的多技能转换。

TLDR: The paper introduces APEX, a DRL-based system for humanoid robots to traverse high platforms by composing various climbing-related skills, achieving zero-shot sim-to-real transfer on a Unitree G1 robot.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种基于深度强化学习（DRL）的系统APEX，用于人形机器人通过组合各种攀爬相关技能来穿越高平台，并在Unitree G1机器人上实现了零样本的模拟到真实世界的迁移。

Authors: Yikai Wang, Tingxuan Leng, Changyi Lin, Shiqi Liu, Shir Simon, Bingqing Chen, Jonathan Francis, Ding Zhao

A receding-horizon multi-contact motion planner for legged robots in challenging environments

Abstract (English): We present a novel receding-horizon multi-contact motion planner for legged robots in challenging scenarios, able to plan motions such as chimney climbing, navigating very narrow passages or crossing large gaps. Our approach adds new capabilities to the state of the art, including the ability to reactively re-plan in response to new information, and planning contact locations and whole-body trajectories simultaneously, simplifying the implementation and removing the need for post-processing or complex multi-stage approaches. Our method is more resistant to local minima problems than other potential field based approaches, and our quadratic-program-based posture generator returns nodes more quickly than those of existing algorithms. Rigorous statistical analysis shows that, with short planning horizons (e.g., one step ahead), our planner is faster than the state-of-the-art across all scenarios tested (between 45% and 98% faster on average, depending on the scenario), while planning less efficient motions (requiring 5% fewer to 700% more stance changes on average). In all but one scenario (Chimney Walking), longer planning horizons (e.g., four steps ahead) extended the average planning times (between 73% faster and 400% slower than the state-of-the-art) but resulted in higher quality motion plans (between 8% more and 47% fewer stance changes than the state-of-the-art).

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种新型的用于腿足机器人应对复杂环境的后退视界多接触运动规划器，该规划器能规划诸如烟囱攀爬、穿越狭窄通道或跨越大间隙等运动。我们的方法为现有技术增加了新的能力，包括对新信息作出反应性重规划的能力，以及同时规划接触位置和全身轨迹的能力，从而简化了实现过程，并消除了对后处理或复杂多阶段方法的需求。我们的方法比其他基于势场的方法更不容易陷入局部最小值问题，并且我们基于二次规划的姿态生成器返回节点的速度比现有算法更快。严格的统计分析表明，在较短规划视界（例如，提前一步）下，我们的规划器比所有测试情景下的最先进方法都快（平均快45%到98%，具体取决于情景），但规划的运动效率较低（平均需要多5%到700%的站姿切换）。除了一个情景（烟囱行走）外，更长的规划视界（例如，提前四步）延长了平均规划时间（比最先进方法快73%到慢400%），但产生了更高质量的运动规划（比最先进方法少8%到47%的站姿切换）。

TLDR: This paper presents a receding-horizon multi-contact motion planner for legged robots in complex environments, demonstrating improved speed and adaptability compared to existing methods, albeit with trade-offs in motion efficiency depending on the planning horizon.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了一种用于复杂环境中腿式机器人的后退水平多接触运动规划器，与现有方法相比，该规划器在速度和适应性方面有所提高，但运动效率有所权衡，具体取决于规划范围。

Authors: Daniel S. J. Derwent, Simon Watson, Bruno V. Adorno

On the Complexity of Offline Reinforcement Learning with $Q^\star$-Approximation and Partial Coverage

Abstract (English): We study offline reinforcement learning under $Q^\star$-approximation and partial coverage, a setting that motivates practical algorithms such as Conservative $Q$-Learning (CQL; Kumar et al., 2020) but has received limited theoretical attention. Our work is inspired by the following open question: "Are $Q^\star$-realizability and Bellman completeness sufficient for sample-efficient offline RL under partial coverage?" We answer in the negative by establishing an information-theoretic lower bound. Going substantially beyond this, we introduce a general framework that characterizes the intrinsic complexity of a given $Q^\star$ function class, inspired by model-free decision-estimation coefficients (DEC) for online RL (Foster et al., 2023b; Liu et al., 2025b). This complexity recovers and improves the quantities underlying the guarantees of Chen and Jiang (2022) and Uehara et al. (2023), and extends to broader settings. Our decision-estimation decomposition can be combined with a wide range of $Q^\star$ estimation procedures, modularizing and generalizing existing approaches. Beyond the general framework, we make further contributions: By developing a novel second-order performance difference lemma, we obtain the first $ε^{-2}$ sample complexity under partial coverage for soft $Q$-learning, improving the $ε^{-4}$ bound of Uehara et al. (2023). We remove Chen and Jiang's (2022) need for additional online interaction when the value gap of $Q^\star$ is unknown. We also give the first characterization of offline learnability for general low-Bellman-rank MDPs without Bellman completeness (Jiang et al., 2017; Du et al., 2021; Jin et al., 2021), a canonical setting in online RL that remains unexplored in offline RL except for special cases. Finally, we provide the first analysis for CQL under $Q^\star$-realizability and Bellman completeness beyond the tabular case.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了$Q^\star$近似和部分覆盖下的离线强化学习，这是一种激发了诸如保守Q学习（CQL; Kumar et al., 2020）等实用算法的设置，但其理论研究较少。我们的工作受到以下开放问题的启发：“在部分覆盖下，$Q^\star$可实现性和贝尔曼完备性是否足以支持样本高效的离线RL？” 我们建立了一个信息论下界，从而否定了这个问题。更重要的是，我们引入了一个通用框架，用于表征给定$Q^\star$函数类的内在复杂性，其灵感来源于在线RL的无模型决策估计系数（DEC）（Foster et al., 2023b; Liu et al., 2025b）。这种复杂性恢复并改进了Chen和Jiang（2022）以及Uehara等人（2023）的保证背后的数量，并扩展到更广泛的设置。我们的决策估计分解可以与各种$Q^\star$估计过程相结合，从而将现有方法模块化和泛化。 除了通用框架之外，我们还做出了进一步的贡献：通过开发一种新颖的二阶性能差异引理，我们获得了soft $Q$-learning在部分覆盖下的第一个$ε^{-2}$样本复杂度，改进了Uehara等人（2023）的$ε^{-4}$界。我们消除了Chen和Jiang（2022）在$Q^\star$的值差距未知时对额外在线交互的需求。我们还首次对一般低贝尔曼秩MDP的离线可学习性进行了表征，这些MDP没有贝尔曼完备性（Jiang et al., 2017; Du et al., 2021; Jin et al., 2021），这是在线RL中的一个典型设置，但在离线RL中除了特殊情况外仍未被探索。最后，我们提供了在表格情况之外的，$Q^\star$可实现性和贝尔曼完备性下对CQL的首次分析。

TLDR: This paper investigates the complexity of offline RL under Q*-approximation and partial coverage, providing a general framework for characterizing this complexity, improved sample complexity for soft Q-learning, and analysis of CQL and low-Bellman-rank MDPs in this setting.

简要说明: 本文研究了在Q*-近似和部分覆盖下的离线RL的复杂性，提供了一个表征这种复杂性的通用框架，改进了软Q学习的样本复杂度，并分析了在这种设置下的CQL和低Bellman秩MDP。

Authors: Haolin Liu, Braham Snyder, Chen-Yu Wei

Differentiable Modal Logic for Multi-Agent Diagnosis, Orchestration and Communication

Abstract (English): As multi-agent AI systems evolve from simple chatbots to autonomous swarms, debugging semantic failures requires reasoning about knowledge, belief, causality, and obligation, precisely what modal logic was designed to formalize. However, traditional modal logic requires manual specification of relationship structures that are unknown or dynamic in real systems. This tutorial demonstrates differentiable modal logic (DML), implemented via Modal Logical Neural Networks (MLNNs), enabling systems to learn trust networks, causal chains, and regulatory boundaries from behavioral data alone. We present a unified neurosymbolic debugging framework through four modalities: epistemic (who to trust), temporal (when events cause failures), deontic (what actions are permitted), and doxastic (how to interpret agent confidence). Each modality is demonstrated on concrete multi-agent scenarios, from discovering deceptive alliances in diplomacy games to detecting LLM hallucinations, with complete implementations showing how logical contradictions become learnable optimization objectives. Key contributions for the neurosymbolic community: (1) interpretable learned structures where trust and causality are explicit parameters, not opaque embeddings; (2) knowledge injection via differentiable axioms that guide learning with sparse data (3) compositional multi-modal reasoning that combines epistemic, temporal, and deontic constraints; and (4) practical deployment patterns for monitoring, active control and communication of multi-agent systems. All code provided as executable Jupyter notebooks.

摘要（中文）: 随着多智能体人工智能系统从简单的聊天机器人演变为自主集群，调试语义故障需要对知识、信念、因果关系和义务进行推理，而这些正是模态逻辑旨在形式化的内容。然而，传统的模态逻辑需要手动指定关系结构，而这些结构在实际系统中是未知的或动态的。本教程演示了可微分模态逻辑（DML），通过模态逻辑神经网络（MLNNs）实现，使系统能够仅从行为数据中学习信任网络、因果链和监管边界。 我们通过四种模态，提出了一个统一的神经符号调试框架：认知模态（信任谁）、时间模态（何时事件导致故障）、道义模态（允许采取什么行动）和信念模态（如何解释智能体的置信度）。每种模态都在具体的多智能体场景中进行演示，从发现外交游戏中的欺骗联盟到检测大型语言模型的幻觉，并提供完整的实现，展示了逻辑矛盾如何成为可学习的优化目标。 为神经符号社区的主要贡献包括：（1）可解释的学习结构，其中信任和因果关系是显式参数，而不是不透明的嵌入；（2）通过可微分公理注入知识，利用稀疏数据指导学习；（3）组合式的多模态推理，结合了认知、时间和道义约束；以及（4）用于监控、主动控制和多智能体系统通信的实际部署模式。所有代码均以可执行的Jupyter Notebook形式提供。

TLDR: This paper introduces Differentiable Modal Logic (DML) implemented via Modal Logical Neural Networks (MLNNs) for debugging multi-agent systems by learning trust networks, causal chains, and regulatory boundaries from behavioral data.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种通过模态逻辑神经网络 (MLNN) 实现的可微模态逻辑 (DML)，用于调试多智能体系统，通过从行为数据中学习信任网络、因果链和监管边界。

Authors: Antonin Sulc

AdaptEvolve: Improving Efficiency of Evolutionary AI Agents through Adaptive Model Selection

Abstract (English): Evolutionary agentic systems intensify the trade-off between computational efficiency and reasoning capability by repeatedly invoking large language models (LLMs) during inference. This setting raises a central question: how can an agent dynamically select an LLM that is sufficiently capable for the current generation step while remaining computationally efficient? While model cascades offer a practical mechanism for balancing this trade-off, existing routing strategies typically rely on static heuristics or external controllers and do not explicitly account for model uncertainty. We introduce AdaptEvolve: Adaptive LLM Selection for Multi-LLM Evolutionary Refinement within an evolutionary sequential refinement framework that leverages intrinsic generation confidence to estimate real-time solvability. Empirical results show that confidence-driven selection yields a favourable Pareto frontier, reducing total inference cost by an average of 37.9% across benchmarks while retaining 97.5% of the upper-bound accuracy of static large-model baselines. Our code is available at https://github.com/raypretam/adaptive_llm_selection.

摘要（中文）: 进化式智能体系统通过在推理过程中重复调用大型语言模型(LLM)，加剧了计算效率和推理能力之间的权衡。 这种设定引出了一个核心问题：智能体如何动态选择一个既足以胜任当前生成步骤，又能保持计算高效的LLM？ 虽然模型级联为平衡这种权衡提供了一种实用的机制，但现有的路由策略通常依赖于静态启发式方法或外部控制器，并且没有明确考虑模型的不确定性。 我们引入了AdaptEvolve：一种自适应LLM选择方法，用于进化式顺序改进框架中的多LLM进化式改进，该方法利用内在生成置信度来估计实时可解性。 实验结果表明，置信度驱动的选择产生了一个有利的帕累托前沿，在基准测试中平均降低了37.9% 的总推理成本，同时保留了静态大型模型基线97.5% 的上限精度。 我们的代码可在https://github.com/raypretam/adaptive_llm_selection获取。

TLDR: AdaptEvolve dynamically selects LLMs during evolutionary agent inference based on generation confidence, achieving a better trade-off between efficiency and accuracy compared to static or heuristic approaches. The method reduces inference costs by an average of 37.9% while maintaining high accuracy.

简要说明: AdaptEvolve 是一种基于生成置信度的动态 LLM 选择方法，用于进化代理推理，与静态或启发式方法相比，在效率和准确性之间实现了更好的权衡。该方法将推理成本平均降低了 37.9%，同时保持了较高的准确性。

Authors: Pretam Ray, Pratik Prabhanjan Brahma, Zicheng Liu, Emad Barsoum

Intelligent AI Delegation

Abstract (English): AI agents are able to tackle increasingly complex tasks. To achieve more ambitious goals, AI agents need to be able to meaningfully decompose problems into manageable sub-components, and safely delegate their completion across to other AI agents and humans alike. Yet, existing task decomposition and delegation methods rely on simple heuristics, and are not able to dynamically adapt to environmental changes and robustly handle unexpected failures. Here we propose an adaptive framework for intelligent AI delegation - a sequence of decisions involving task allocation, that also incorporates transfer of authority, responsibility, accountability, clear specifications regarding roles and boundaries, clarity of intent, and mechanisms for establishing trust between the two (or more) parties. The proposed framework is applicable to both human and AI delegators and delegatees in complex delegation networks, aiming to inform the development of protocols in the emerging agentic web.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能体能够处理日益复杂的任务。为了实现更宏伟的目标，人工智能体需要能够有意义地将问题分解为可管理的子组件，并将它们的完成安全地委托给其他人工智能体以及人类。然而，现有的任务分解和委托方法依赖于简单的启发式算法，并且无法动态地适应环境变化和稳健地处理意外故障。本文中，我们提出了一个用于智能人工智能委托的自适应框架——一个包含任务分配的决策序列，该序列还包括权力的转移、责任、可问责性、关于角色和界限的清晰规范、意图的清晰性以及在双方（或多方）之间建立信任的机制。所提出的框架适用于复杂委托网络中的人类和人工智能委托者及被委托者，旨在为新兴的主动代理网络中协议的开发提供信息。

TLDR: This paper introduces an adaptive framework for intelligent AI delegation, addressing task decomposition and delegation in complex AI and human agent networks with a focus on dynamic adaptation and robustness. It appears relevant to the broader field of agent collaboration and task distribution.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个智能AI委托的自适应框架，旨在解决复杂AI和人类代理网络中的任务分解和委托问题，重点关注动态适应性和鲁棒性。它与代理协作和任务分配的更广泛领域相关。

Authors: Nenad Tomašev, Matija Franklin, Simon Osindero

Cooperation Breakdown in LLM Agents Under Communication Delays

Abstract (English): LLM-based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS), in which autonomous AI agents cooperate to solve tasks, are gaining increasing attention. For such systems to be deployed in society, agents must be able to establish cooperation and coordination under real-world computational and communication constraints. We propose the FLCOA framework (Five Layers for Cooperation/Coordination among Autonomous Agents) to conceptualize how cooperation and coordination emerge in groups of autonomous agents, and highlight that the influence of lower-layer factors - especially computational and communication resources - has been largely overlooked. To examine the effect of communication delay, we introduce a Continuous Prisoner's Dilemma with Communication Delay and conduct simulations with LLM-based agents. As delay increases, agents begin to exploit slower responses even without explicit instructions. Interestingly, excessive delay reduces cycles of exploitation, yielding a U-shaped relationship between delay magnitude and mutual cooperation. These results suggest that fostering cooperation requires attention not only to high-level institutional design but also to lower-layer factors such as communication delay and resource allocation, pointing to new directions for MAS research.

摘要（中文）: 基于大型语言模型的多智能体系统（LLM-MAS）正受到越来越多的关注，在该系统中，自主AI智能体协作解决任务。为了使此类系统能够在社会中部署，智能体必须能够在真实的计算和通信约束下建立合作和协调。我们提出了FLCOA框架（自主智能体间合作/协调的五层模型），以概念化自主智能体群体中合作和协调是如何产生的，并强调了底层因素——特别是计算和通信资源——的影响在很大程度上被忽视了。为了检验通信延迟的影响，我们引入了带有通信延迟的连续囚徒困境，并对基于LLM的智能体进行了模拟。 随着延迟的增加，智能体开始利用较慢的响应，即使没有明确的指示。 有趣的是，过度的延迟会减少剥削周期，从而产生延迟幅度与相互合作之间的U型关系。 这些结果表明，促进合作不仅需要关注高层制度设计，还需要关注底层因素，例如通信延迟和资源分配，这为MAS研究指明了新的方向。

TLDR: This paper investigates the impact of communication delays on cooperation in multi-agent systems using LLM agents in a Continuous Prisoner's Dilemma, finding a U-shaped relationship between delay and cooperation.

简要说明: 本文研究了通信延迟对多智能体系统中LLM智能体合作的影响，通过连续囚徒困境，发现延迟与合作之间存在U型关系。

Authors: Keita Nishimoto, Kimitaka Asatani, Ichiro Sakata

Provable Offline Reinforcement Learning for Structured Cyclic MDPs

Abstract (English): We introduce a novel cyclic Markov decision process (MDP) framework for multi-step decision problems with heterogeneous stage-specific dynamics, transitions, and discount factors across the cycle. In this setting, offline learning is challenging: optimizing a policy at any stage shifts the state distributions of subsequent stages, propagating mismatch across the cycle. To address this, we propose a modular structural framework that decomposes the cyclic process into stage-wise sub-problems. While generally applicable, we instantiate this principle as CycleFQI, an extension of fitted Q-iteration enabling theoretical analysis and interpretation. It uses a vector of stage-specific Q-functions, tailored to each stage, to capture within-stage sequences and transitions between stages. This modular design enables partial control, allowing some stages to be optimized while others follow predefined policies. We establish finite-sample suboptimality error bounds and derive global convergence rates under Besov regularity, demonstrating that CycleFQI mitigates the curse of dimensionality compared to monolithic baselines. Additionally, we propose a sieve-based method for asymptotic inference of optimal policy values under a margin condition. Experiments on simulated and real-world Type 1 Diabetes data sets demonstrate CycleFQI's effectiveness.

摘要（中文）: 我们引入了一种新颖的循环马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架，用于解决具有异构阶段特定动力学、转移概率和跨循环折扣因子的多步决策问题。 在这种情况下，离线学习面临挑战：在任何阶段优化策略都会改变后续阶段的状态分布，并在整个循环中传播不匹配。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种模块化的结构框架，将循环过程分解为阶段性的子问题。 虽然该框架具有普遍适用性，但我们将此原则实例化为CycleFQI，它是拟合Q迭代（fitted Q-iteration）的扩展，可以进行理论分析和解释。 它使用一个阶段特定的Q函数向量，专为每个阶段定制，以捕获阶段内的序列以及阶段之间的转移。这种模块化设计实现了局部控制，允许优化某些阶段的策略，而其他阶段遵循预定义的策略。我们建立了有限样本的次优性误差界，并在Besov正则性下推导出全局收敛速率，证明了CycleFQI相比于单体基线可以缓解维度诅咒。 此外，我们提出了一种基于筛法的渐近推理方法，用于在边际条件下推断最优策略值。在模拟和真实世界的一型糖尿病数据集上的实验证明了CycleFQI的有效性。

TLDR: This paper introduces CycleFQI, a modular offline reinforcement learning algorithm designed for cyclic MDPs with stage-specific dynamics, and provides theoretical guarantees and empirical validation on diabetes management.

简要说明: 该论文提出了 CycleFQI，一种专为具有阶段特定动态的循环 MDP 设计的模块化离线强化学习算法，并提供了理论保证和糖尿病管理方面的实证验证。

Authors: Kyungbok Lee, Angelica Cristello Sarteau, Michael R. Kosorok

Human-Inspired Continuous Learning of Internal Reasoning Processes: Learning How to Think for Adaptive AI Systems

Abstract (English): Learning internal reasoning processes is crucial for developing AI systems capable of sustained adaptation in dynamic real-world environments. However, most existing approaches primarily emphasize learning task-specific outputs or static knowledge representations, while overlooking the continuous refinement of internal reasoning structures, action scheduling policies, and learning mechanisms themselves. In this paper, we propose a human-inspired continuous learning framework that unifies reasoning, action, reflection, and verification within a sequential reasoning model enhanced by parallel learning. The framework explicitly treats internal thinking processes as primary learning objects. It systematically records internal reasoning trajectories and environmental interactions as structured learning material, enabling the system to optimize not only task-level content but also the organization, scheduling, and evolution of reasoning activities. This design realizes learning alongside processing, allowing cognitive structures to improve during execution. Furthermore, the framework supports controlled replacement of predefined logic with learned procedures and introduces a hierarchical learning-to-learn mechanism that jointly adapts task-level parameters and learning strategies. As a result, the system progressively evolves its internal cognitive architecture while preserving operational stability. Experimental results on a temperature sensor abnormality detection task show that incorporating internal-process learning reduces average runtime by 23.9%.

摘要（中文）: 学习内部推理过程对于开发能够在动态现实环境中持续适应的人工智能系统至关重要。然而，现有的大多数方法主要强调学习特定于任务的输出或静态知识表示，而忽略了内部推理结构、行动调度策略和学习机制本身的持续改进。在本文中，我们提出了一种受人类启发的连续学习框架，该框架在并行学习增强的顺序推理模型中统一了推理、行动、反思和验证。该框架将内部思维过程明确地视为主要的学习对象。它系统地记录内部推理轨迹和环境交互作为结构化学习材料，使系统不仅能够优化任务级的内容，还能优化推理活动的组织、调度和演化。这种设计实现了伴随处理的学习，从而允许认知结构在执行过程中得到改进。此外，该框架支持用学习的程序替换预定义的逻辑，并引入了一种分层学习-去-学习机制，该机制联合调整任务级参数和学习策略。因此，系统在保持运行稳定性的同时，逐步演化其内部认知架构。在温度传感器异常检测任务上的实验结果表明，结合内部过程学习可将平均运行时间减少23.9%。

TLDR: This paper presents a framework for AI systems to continuously learn and refine their internal reasoning processes, including action scheduling and learning mechanisms, leading to improved performance and efficiency. The proposed framework enables optimization of how the system thinks alongside task-level content.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个框架，使人工智能系统能够持续学习和改进其内部推理过程，包括行动调度和学习机制，从而提高性能和效率。该框架能够优化系统思考的方式，同时优化任务级内容。

Authors: Hong Su

Distributionally Robust Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via Robust Value Factorization

Abstract (English): Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) commonly adopts centralized training with decentralized execution, where value-factorization methods enforce the individual-global-maximum (IGM) principle so that decentralized greedy actions recover the team-optimal joint action. However, the reliability of this recipe in real-world settings remains unreliable due to environmental uncertainties arising from the sim-to-real gap, model mismatch, and system noise. We address this gap by introducing Distributionally robust IGM (DrIGM), a principle that requires each agent's robust greedy action to align with the robust team-optimal joint action. We show that DrIGM holds for a novel definition of robust individual action values, which is compatible with decentralized greedy execution and yields a provable robustness guarantee for the whole system. Building on this foundation, we derive DrIGM-compliant robust variants of existing value-factorization architectures (e.g., VDN/QMIX/QTRAN) that (i) train on robust Q-targets, (ii) preserve scalability, and (iii) integrate seamlessly with existing codebases without bespoke per-agent reward shaping. Empirically, on high-fidelity SustainGym simulators and a StarCraft game environment, our methods consistently improve out-of-distribution performance. Code and data are available at https://github.com/crqu/robust-coMARL.

摘要（中文）: 合作式多智能体强化学习(MARL)通常采用集中式训练和分散式执行，其中价值分解方法强制执行个体-全局-最大化(IGM)原则，以便分散式的贪婪动作能够恢复团队最优的联合动作。然而，由于来源于从仿真到真实环境的差距、模型不匹配和系统噪声等环境不确定性，这种方法在实际环境中的可靠性仍然不稳定。我们通过引入分布鲁棒IGM (DrIGM)来解决这一问题，该原则要求每个智能体的鲁棒贪婪动作与鲁棒的团队最优联合动作对齐。我们证明，DrIGM对于鲁棒个体动作价值的新定义成立，该定义与分散式贪婪执行兼容，并为整个系统提供可证明的鲁棒性保证。在此基础上，我们推导出与DrIGM兼容的现有价值分解架构(例如VDN/QMIX/QTRAN)的鲁棒变体，这些变体(i)基于鲁棒Q-目标进行训练，(ii)保持可扩展性，并且(iii)与现有代码库无缝集成，无需定制的每个智能体的奖励塑造。在真实度高的SustainGym模拟器和星际争霸游戏环境中进行的实证表明，我们的方法始终能够提高分布外(out-of-distribution)性能。代码和数据可在https://github.com/crqu/robust-coMARL上获取。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Distributionally Robust Individual-Global-Maximum (DrIGM) principle for cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning to improve out-of-distribution performance in uncertain environments, and proposes DrIGM-compliant robust variants of existing value-factorization architectures.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于合作式多智能体强化学习的分布鲁棒个体-全局最大（DrIGM）原则，以提高在不确定环境中的分布外性能，并提出了与DrIGM兼容的现有价值分解架构的鲁棒变体。

Authors: Chengrui Qu, Christopher Yeh, Kishan Panaganti, Eric Mazumdar, Adam Wierman

TRACER: Trajectory Risk Aggregation for Critical Episodes in Agentic Reasoning

Abstract (English): Estimating uncertainty for AI agents in real-world multi-turn tool-using interaction with humans is difficult because failures are often triggered by sparse critical episodes (e.g., looping, incoherent tool use, or user-agent miscoordination) even when local generation appears confident. Existing uncertainty proxies focus on single-shot text generation and therefore miss these trajectory-level breakdown signals. We introduce TRACER, a trajectory-level uncertainty metric for dual-control Tool-Agent-User interaction. TRACER combines content-aware surprisal with situational-awareness signals, semantic and lexical repetition, and tool-grounded coherence gaps, and aggregates them using a tail-focused risk functional with a MAX-composite step risk to surface decisive anomalies. We evaluate TRACER on $τ^2$-bench by predicting task failure and selective task execution. To this end, TRACER improves AUROC by up to 37.1% and AUARC by up to 55% over baselines, enabling earlier and more accurate detection of uncertainty in complex conversational tool-use settings. Our code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/sinatayebati/agent-tracer.

摘要（中文）: 在与人类进行真实世界多轮工具使用交互中，为人工智能主体估计不确定性是困难的，因为即使局部生成看起来很自信，失败通常是由稀疏的关键事件触发的（例如，循环、不连贯的工具使用，或用户-主体不协调）。现有的不确定性代理主要关注单次文本生成，因此错过了这些轨迹级别的崩溃信号。我们引入了 TRACER，一种用于双控制工具-主体-用户交互的轨迹级别不确定性度量。TRACER 将内容感知的惊异度与情境感知信号、语义和词汇重复，以及工具关联的连贯性 gap 相结合，并使用尾部聚焦的风险泛函，结合 MAX 复合步骤风险来聚合它们，以突出决定性的异常。我们通过预测任务失败和选择性任务执行在 $τ^2$-bench 上评估 TRACER。为此，TRACER 相比基线提高了 AUROC 高达 37.1%，AUARC 高达 55%，从而能够在复杂的对话式工具使用环境中更早，更准确地检测不确定性。我们的代码和基准测试可在 https://github.com/sinatayebati/agent-tracer 上获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces TRACER, a trajectory-level uncertainty metric for tool-using agents in human interaction, which combines various signals to detect critical failures, achieving significant improvement in predicting task failure compared to baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TRACER，一种用于人机交互工具使用代理的轨迹级不确定性度量指标，它结合了各种信号来检测关键故障，与基线相比，在预测任务失败方面取得了显著改进。

AssetFormer: Modular 3D Assets Generation with Autoregressive Transformer

Abstract (English): The digital industry demands high-quality, diverse modular 3D assets, especially for user-generated content~(UGC). In this work, we introduce AssetFormer, an autoregressive Transformer-based model designed to generate modular 3D assets from textual descriptions. Our pilot study leverages real-world modular assets collected from online platforms. AssetFormer tackles the challenge of creating assets composed of primitives that adhere to constrained design parameters for various applications. By innovatively adapting module sequencing and decoding techniques inspired by language models, our approach enhances asset generation quality through autoregressive modeling. Initial results indicate the effectiveness of AssetFormer in streamlining asset creation for professional development and UGC scenarios. This work presents a flexible framework extendable to various types of modular 3D assets, contributing to the broader field of 3D content generation. The code is available at https://github.com/Advocate99/AssetFormer.

摘要（中文）: 数字产业对高质量、多样化的模块化 3D 资产有着迫切需求，尤其是在用户生成内容 (UGC) 方面。 在这项工作中，我们推出 AssetFormer，一种基于自回归 Transformer 的模型，旨在从文本描述中生成模块化 3D 资产。 我们的初步研究利用了从在线平台收集的真实模块化资产。 AssetFormer 解决了创建由基元组成的资产的挑战，这些基元必须遵守各种应用的约束性设计参数。 通过创新性地调整受语言模型启发的模块序列化和解码技术，我们的方法通过自回归建模提高了资产生成质量。 初步结果表明，AssetFormer 在简化专业开发和 UGC 场景的资产创建方面是有效的。 这项工作提出了一个可扩展到各种类型模块化 3D 资产的灵活框架，为更广泛的 3D 内容生成领域做出了贡献。 代码见 https://github.com/Advocate99/AssetFormer。

Authors: Lingting Zhu, Shengju Qian, Haidi Fan, Jiayu Dong, Zhenchao Jin, Siwei Zhou, Gen Dong, Xin Wang, Lequan Yu

Efficient Segment Anything with Depth-Aware Fusion and Limited Training Data

Abstract (English): Segment Anything Models (SAM) achieve impressive universal segmentation performance but require massive datasets (e.g., 11M images) and rely solely on RGB inputs. Recent efficient variants reduce computation but still depend on large-scale training. We propose a lightweight RGB-D fusion framework that augments EfficientViT-SAM with monocular depth priors. Depth maps are generated with a pretrained estimator and fused mid-level with RGB features through a dedicated depth encoder. Trained on only 11.2k samples (less than 0.1\% of SA-1B), our method achieves higher accuracy than EfficientViT-SAM, showing that depth cues provide strong geometric priors for segmentation.

摘要（中文）: 分割一切模型（SAM）实现了令人印象深刻的通用分割性能，但需要海量数据集（例如，1100万张图像）并且仅依赖于RGB输入。近期的效率变体降低了计算量，但仍依赖于大规模训练。我们提出了一种轻量级的RGB-D融合框架，该框架使用单目深度先验来增强EfficientViT-SAM。深度图使用预训练的估计器生成，并通过专用深度编码器在中间层与RGB特征融合。仅在1.12万个样本（不到SA-1B的0.1％）上进行训练，我们的方法就实现了比EfficientViT-SAM更高的精度，表明深度线索为分割提供了强大的几何先验。

TLDR: This paper introduces a lightweight RGB-D fusion framework to improve the efficiency of Segment Anything Models (SAM) by incorporating monocular depth priors and requiring significantly less training data.

Authors: Yiming Zhou, Xuenjie Xie, Panfeng Li, Albrecht Kunz, Ahmad Osman, Xavier Maldague

Move What Matters: Parameter-Efficient Domain Adaptation via Optimal Transport Flow for Collaborative Perception

Abstract (English): Fast domain adaptation remains a fundamental challenge for deploying multi-agent systems across diverse environments in Vehicle-to-Everything (V2X) collaborative perception. Despite the success of Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) in natural language processing and conventional vision tasks, directly applying PEFT to multi-agent settings leads to significant performance degradation and training instability. In this work, we conduct a detailed analysis and identify two key factors: (i) inter-frame redundancy in heterogeneous sensory streams, and (ii) erosion of fine-grained semantics in deep-layer representations under PEFT adaptation. To address these issues, we propose FlowAdapt, a parameter-efficient framework grounded in optimal transport theory, which minimizes information transport costs across both data distributions and network hierarchies. Specifically, we introduce a Wasserstein Greedy Sampling strategy to selectively filter redundant samples via a bounded covering radius. Furthermore, Progressive Knowledge Transfer module is designed to progressively inject compressed early-stage representations into later stages through learnable pathways, alleviating semantic degradation in late-stage adaptation. Extensive experiments on three benchmarks demonstrate that FlowAdapt achieves state-of-the-art performance with only 1% of trainable parameters, effectively bridging domain gaps with superior sample efficiency and generalization.

摘要（中文）: 快速领域适应仍然是车辆与一切互联（V2X）协同感知中，在多样化环境中部署多智能体系统的一项根本挑战。尽管参数高效微调（PEFT）在自然语言处理和传统视觉任务中取得了成功，但直接将PEFT应用于多智能体环境会导致显著的性能下降和训练不稳定。在这项工作中，我们进行了详细的分析，并确定了两个关键因素：（i）异构传感器流中的帧间冗余，以及（ii）PEFT适应下深层表示中细粒度语义的侵蚀。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了FlowAdapt，一个基于最优传输理论的参数高效框架，它最小化了数据分布和网络层次结构上的信息传输成本。具体而言，我们引入了一种 Wasserstein 贪婪采样策略，通过有界覆盖半径选择性地过滤冗余样本。此外，设计了渐进知识迁移模块，通过可学习的路径将压缩的早期阶段表示逐渐注入到后期阶段，以缓解后期阶段适应中的语义退化。在三个基准数据集上的大量实验表明，FlowAdapt仅用 1% 的可训练参数就实现了最先进的性能，有效地弥合了领域差距，并具有卓越的样本效率和泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces FlowAdapt, a parameter-efficient domain adaptation framework for collaborative perception in V2X systems, using optimal transport to address inter-frame redundancy and semantic degradation issues, achieving SOTA performance with minimal trainable parameters.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FlowAdapt，一个参数高效的领域自适应框架，用于V2X系统中的协同感知。该方法利用最优传输理论解决帧间冗余和语义退化问题，并以极少的训练参数实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Zesheng Jia, Jin Wang, Siao Liu, Lingzhi Li, Ziyao Huang, Yunjiang Xu, Jianping Wang

Ctrl&Shift: High-Quality Geometry-Aware Object Manipulation in Visual Generation

Abstract (English): Object-level manipulation, relocating or reorienting objects in images or videos while preserving scene realism, is central to film post-production, AR, and creative editing. Yet existing methods struggle to jointly achieve three core goals: background preservation, geometric consistency under viewpoint shifts, and user-controllable transformations. Geometry-based approaches offer precise control but require explicit 3D reconstruction and generalize poorly; diffusion-based methods generalize better but lack fine-grained geometric control. We present Ctrl&Shift, an end-to-end diffusion framework to achieve geometry-consistent object manipulation without explicit 3D representations. Our key insight is to decompose manipulation into two stages, object removal and reference-guided inpainting under explicit camera pose control, and encode both within a unified diffusion process. To enable precise, disentangled control, we design a multi-task, multi-stage training strategy that separates background, identity, and pose signals across tasks. To improve generalization, we introduce a scalable real-world dataset construction pipeline that generates paired image and video samples with estimated relative camera poses. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Ctrl&Shift achieves state-of-the-art results in fidelity, viewpoint consistency, and controllability. To our knowledge, this is the first framework to unify fine-grained geometric control and real-world generalization for object manipulation, without relying on any explicit 3D modeling.

摘要（中文）: 目标级别的操控，即在图像或视频中重新定位或调整物体方向，同时保持场景的真实感，是电影后期制作、增强现实和创意编辑的核心。然而，现有方法难以同时实现三个核心目标：背景保持、视角变换下的几何一致性以及用户可控的变换。基于几何的方法能够提供精确的控制，但需要显式的3D重建，并且泛化能力较差；基于扩散模型的方法泛化能力较好，但缺乏细粒度的几何控制。我们提出 Ctrl&Shift，一个端到端扩散框架，无需显式的3D表示即可实现几何一致的物体操控。我们的关键洞察在于将操控分解为两个阶段：物体移除和显式相机姿态控制下的参考引导式图像修复，并将这两者编码在一个统一的扩散过程中。为实现精确的、解耦的控制，我们设计了一种多任务、多阶段的训练策略，将背景、身份和姿态信号在不同任务之间进行分离。为了提高泛化能力，我们引入了一种可扩展的真实世界数据集构建流程，生成带有估计的相对相机姿态的配对图像和视频样本。大量实验表明，Ctrl&Shift 在保真度、视角一致性和可控性方面均实现了最先进的结果。据我们所知，这是第一个统一了细粒度几何控制和真实世界泛化的物体操控框架，并且不依赖于任何显式的3D建模。

TLDR: The paper introduces Ctrl&Shift, a diffusion-based framework for geometry-consistent object manipulation in images and videos, achieving state-of-the-art results in fidelity, viewpoint consistency, and controllability without explicit 3D modeling.

简要说明: 本文介绍Ctrl&Shift，一个基于扩散模型的框架，用于在图像和视频中实现几何一致的物体操作。该框架在保真度、视点一致性和可控性方面达到了最先进的水平，且无需显式的3D建模。

Authors: Penghui Ruan, Bojia Zi, Xianbiao Qi, Youze Huang, Rong Xiao, Pichao Wang, Jiannong Cao, Yuhui Shi

MDE-VIO: Enhancing Visual-Inertial Odometry Using Learned Depth Priors

Abstract (English): Traditional monocular Visual-Inertial Odometry (VIO) systems struggle in low-texture environments where sparse visual features are insufficient for accurate pose estimation. To address this, dense Monocular Depth Estimation (MDE) has been widely explored as a complementary information source. While recent Vision Transformer (ViT) based complex foundational models offer dense, geometrically consistent depth, their computational demands typically preclude them from real-time edge deployment. Our work bridges this gap by integrating learned depth priors directly into the VINS-Mono optimization backend. We propose a novel framework that enforces affine-invariant depth consistency and pairwise ordinal constraints, explicitly filtering unstable artifacts via variance-based gating. This approach strictly adheres to the computational limits of edge devices while robustly recovering metric scale. Extensive experiments on the TartanGround and M3ED datasets demonstrate that our method prevents divergence in challenging scenarios and delivers significant accuracy gains, reducing Absolute Trajectory Error (ATE) by up to 28.3%. Code will be made available.

摘要（中文）: 传统单目视觉惯性里程计（VIO）系统在低纹理环境中表现不佳，因为稀疏的视觉特征不足以进行精确的位姿估计。为了解决这个问题，密集的单目深度估计（MDE）已被广泛探索作为一种补充信息来源。虽然最近基于视觉Transformer（ViT）的复杂基础模型提供了密集、几何一致的深度信息，但它们的计算需求通常使其无法在实时边缘部署中使用。我们的工作通过将学习到的深度先验直接集成到VINS-Mono优化后端来弥合这一差距。我们提出了一种新颖的框架，该框架强制执行仿射不变的深度一致性和成对序数约束，并通过基于方差的门控显式地过滤不稳定的伪影。这种方法严格遵守边缘设备的计算限制，同时稳健地恢复尺度。在TartanGround和M3ED数据集上的大量实验表明，我们的方法可以防止在具有挑战性的场景中出现发散，并显著提高精度，将绝对轨迹误差（ATE）降低高达28.3%。代码将会开源。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method to enhance Visual-Inertial Odometry (VIO) in low-texture environments by integrating learned depth priors into the VINS-Mono backend, achieving real-time performance on edge devices with improved accuracy and robustness.

Authors: Arda Alniak, Sinan Kalkan, Mustafa Mert Ankarali, Afsar Saranli, Abdullah Aydin Alatan

Few-Shot Design Optimization by Exploiting Auxiliary Information

Abstract (English): Many real-world design problems involve optimizing an expensive black-box function $f(x)$, such as hardware design or drug discovery. Bayesian Optimization has emerged as a sample-efficient framework for this problem. However, the basic setting considered by these methods is simplified compared to real-world experimental setups, where experiments often generate a wealth of useful information. We introduce a new setting where an experiment generates high-dimensional auxiliary information $h(x)$ along with the performance measure $f(x)$; moreover, a history of previously solved tasks from the same task family is available for accelerating optimization. A key challenge of our setting is learning how to represent and utilize $h(x)$ for efficiently solving new optimization tasks beyond the task history. We develop a novel approach for this setting based on a neural model which predicts $f(x)$ for unseen designs given a few-shot context containing observations of $h(x)$. We evaluate our method on two challenging domains, robotic hardware design and neural network hyperparameter tuning, and introduce a novel design problem and large-scale benchmark for the former. On both domains, our method utilizes auxiliary feedback effectively to achieve more accurate few-shot prediction and faster optimization of design tasks, significantly outperforming several methods for multi-task optimization.

摘要（中文）: 许多现实世界的设计问题都涉及优化一个昂贵的黑盒函数 $f(x)$，例如硬件设计或药物发现。贝叶斯优化已经成为解决此类问题的一种具有样本效率的框架。然而，这些方法所考虑的基本设置相对于真实的实验设置而言过于简化，因为实验通常产生大量有用的信息。我们引入一个新的设置，其中实验产生高维辅助信息 $h(x)$ 以及性能指标 $f(x)$；此外，还可以利用同一任务族中先前已解决任务的历史记录来加速优化。我们这一设置的一个关键挑战是如何学习表示和利用 $h(x)$，从而在任务历史之外高效地解决新的优化任务。我们基于神经模型为此设置开发了一种新方法，该神经模型能够在给定包含 $h(x)$ 观测值的少量样本上下文的情况下，预测未见设计的 $f(x)$。我们在两个具有挑战性的领域，即机器人硬件设计和神经网络超参数调优方面评估了我们的方法，并为前者引入了一个新的设计问题和大规模基准。在这两个领域，我们的方法都能有效地利用辅助反馈，从而实现更准确的少量样本预测和更快的设计任务优化，显著优于几种多任务优化方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new Bayesian Optimization setting for expensive black-box function optimization utilizing high-dimensional auxiliary information and task history. Authors: Arjun Mani, Carl Vondrick, Richard Zemel

Improving HPC Code Generation Capability of LLMs via Online Reinforcement Learning with Real-Machine Benchmark Rewards

Abstract (English): Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong code generation capabilities, yet the runtime performance of generated code is not guaranteed, and there have been few attempts to train LLMs using runtime performance as a reward in the HPC domain. We propose an online reinforcement learning approach that executes LLM-generated code on a supercomputer and directly feeds back the measured runtime performance (GFLOPS) as a reward. We further introduce a Staged Quality-Diversity (SQD) algorithm that progressively varies the permitted optimization techniques on a per-problem basis, enabling the model to learn code optimization from diverse perspectives. We build a distributed system connecting a GPU training cluster with a CPU benchmarking cluster, and train Qwen2.5 Coder 14B on a double-precision matrix multiplication task using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Through two experiments, we show that reinforcement learning combining runtime performance feedback with staged optimization can improve the HPC code generation capability of LLMs.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）已展现出强大的代码生成能力，但生成代码的运行时性能却无法得到保证，且鲜有尝试在高性能计算（HPC）领域中使用运行时性能作为奖励来训练LLMs。我们提出了一种在线强化学习方法，该方法在超级计算机上执行LLM生成的代码，并将测量的运行时性能（GFLOPS）直接反馈作为奖励。我们进一步引入了一种分阶段质量-多样性（SQD）算法，该算法在每个问题基础上逐步改变允许的优化技术，使模型能够从不同的角度学习代码优化。我们构建了一个分布式系统，将GPU训练集群与CPU基准测试集群相连接，并使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）在双精度矩阵乘法任务上训练Qwen2.5 Coder 14B。通过两个实验，我们证明了将运行时性能反馈与分阶段优化相结合的强化学习可以提高LLMs的高性能计算代码生成能力。

TLDR: This paper presents an online reinforcement learning approach to train LLMs for HPC code generation using runtime performance as a reward, incorporating a staged quality-diversity algorithm for code optimization.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种在线强化学习方法，利用运行时性能作为奖励来训练LLM进行HPC代码生成，并结合分阶段质量多样性算法进行代码优化。

Authors: Ryo Mikasa, Shun-ichiro Hayashi, Daichi Mukunoki, Tetsuya Hoshino, Takahiro Katagiri

FedGRPO: Privately Optimizing Foundation Models with Group-Relative Rewards from Domain Client

Abstract (English): One important direction of Federated Foundation Models (FedFMs) is leveraging data from small client models to enhance the performance of a large server-side foundation model. Existing methods based on model level or representation level knowledge transfer either require expensive local training or incur high communication costs and introduce unavoidable privacy risks. We reformulate this problem as a reinforcement learning style evaluation process and propose FedGRPO, a privacy preserving framework comprising two modules. The first module performs competence-based expert selection by building a lightweight confidence graph from auxiliary data to identify the most suitable clients for each question. The second module leverages the "Group Relative" concept from the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) framework by packaging each question together with its solution rationale into candidate policies, dispatching these policies to a selected subset of expert clients, and aggregating solely the resulting scalar reward signals via a federated group-relative loss function. By exchanging reward values instead of data or model updates, FedGRPO reduces privacy risk and communication overhead while enabling parallel evaluation across heterogeneous devices. Empirical results on diverse domain tasks demonstrate that FedGRPO achieves superior downstream accuracy and communication efficiency compared to conventional FedFMs baselines.

摘要（中文）: 联邦基础模型（FedFMs）的一个重要方向是利用小型客户端模型的数据来增强大型服务器端基础模型的性能。现有的基于模型层面或表示层面知识迁移的方法要么需要昂贵的本地训练，要么产生高昂的通信成本，并引入不可避免的隐私风险。我们将此问题重新定义为一个强化学习风格的评估过程，并提出了FedGRPO，一个包含两个模块的隐私保护框架。第一个模块通过从辅助数据构建轻量级置信图来执行基于能力的专家选择，从而为每个问题识别最合适的客户端。第二个模块利用Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)框架中的“群体相对”概念，将每个问题及其解决方案原理打包成候选策略，并将这些策略分派到选定的专家客户端子集，并通过联邦群体相对损失函数聚合仅由此产生的标量奖励信号。通过交换奖励值而不是数据或模型更新，FedGRPO降低了隐私风险和通信开销，同时实现了异构设备上的并行评估。在不同领域任务上的实证结果表明，与传统的FedFMs基线相比，FedGRPO实现了卓越的下游精度和通信效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces FedGRPO, a privacy-preserving federated learning framework for optimizing foundation models using group-relative rewards from domain client feedback, achieving better accuracy and communication efficiency compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了FedGRPO，一个隐私保护的联邦学习框架，通过利用领域客户端的组相对奖励来优化基础模型，相比现有方法，实现了更高的准确性和通信效率。

Authors: Gongxi Zhu, Hanlin Gu, Lixin Fan, Qiang Yang, Yuxing Han

Temporal Difference Learning with Constrained Initial Representations

Abstract (English): Recently, there have been numerous attempts to enhance the sample efficiency of off-policy reinforcement learning (RL) agents when interacting with the environment, including architecture improvements and new algorithms. Despite these advances, they overlook the potential of directly constraining the initial representations of the input data, which can intuitively alleviate the distribution shift issue and stabilize training. In this paper, we introduce the Tanh function into the initial layer to fulfill such a constraint. We theoretically unpack the convergence property of the temporal difference learning with the Tanh function under linear function approximation. Motivated by theoretical insights, we present our Constrained Initial Representations framework, tagged CIR, which is made up of three components: (i) the Tanh activation along with normalization methods to stabilize representations; (ii) the skip connection module to provide a linear pathway from the shallow layer to the deep layer; (iii) the convex Q-learning that allows a more flexible value estimate and mitigates potential conservatism. Empirical results show that CIR exhibits strong performance on numerous continuous control tasks, even being competitive or surpassing existing strong baseline methods.

摘要（中文）: 近年来，出现了很多尝试提升离策略强化学习（RL）智能体与环境交互时的样本效率的方法，包括架构改进和新算法。尽管取得了这些进展，但它们忽略了直接约束输入数据的初始表征的潜力，而这直观上可以缓解分布偏移问题并稳定训练。在本文中，我们引入Tanh函数到初始层以实现这种约束。我们从理论上分析了在线性函数逼近下，带Tanh函数的时间差分学习的收敛性。受到理论洞见的启发，我们提出了我们的约束初始表征框架，标记为CIR，它由三个部分组成：（i）Tanh激活函数及规范化方法，以稳定表征；（ii）跳跃连接模块，提供从浅层到深层的线性通路；（iii）凸Q学习，允许更灵活的价值估计并减轻潜在的保守性。实验结果表明，CIR在许多连续控制任务上表现出强大的性能，甚至可以与现有的强大基线方法竞争或超越这些方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Constrained Initial Representations (CIR) framework for off-policy RL, using a Tanh function and other components to improve sample efficiency and stabilize training, achieving competitive performance on continuous control tasks.

Authors: Jiafei Lyu, Jingwen Yang, Zhongjian Qiao, Runze Liu, Zeyuan Liu, Deheng Ye, Zongqing Lu, Xiu Li

Partial GFlowNet: Accelerating Convergence in Large State Spaces via Strategic Partitioning

Abstract (English): Generative Flow Networks (GFlowNets) have shown promising potential to generate high-scoring candidates with probability proportional to their rewards. As existing GFlowNets freely explore in state space, they encounter significant convergence challenges when scaling to large state spaces. Addressing this issue, this paper proposes to restrict the exploration of actor. A planner is introduced to partition the entire state space into overlapping partial state spaces. Given their limited size, these partial state spaces allow the actor to efficiently identify subregions with higher rewards. A heuristic strategy is introduced to switch partial regions thus preventing the actor from wasting time exploring fully explored or low-reward partial regions. By iteratively exploring these partial state spaces, the actor learns to converge towards the high-reward subregions within the entire state space. Experiments on several widely used datasets demonstrate that \modelname converges faster than existing works on large state spaces. Furthermore, \modelname not only generates candidates with higher rewards but also significantly improves their diversity.

摘要（中文）: 生成流网络（GFlowNets）已经在生成概率与其回报成比例的高分候选者方面显示出很有希望的潜力。由于现有的GFlowNets在状态空间中自由探索，因此在扩展到大型状态空间时，它们会遇到显著的收敛挑战。为了解决这个问题，本文提出限制actor的探索。引入一个规划器，将整个状态空间划分为重叠的部分状态空间。鉴于其有限的尺寸，这些部分状态空间允许actor有效地识别具有更高回报的子区域。引入一种启发式策略来切换部分区域，从而防止actor浪费时间探索已充分探索或低回报的部分区域。通过迭代地探索这些部分状态空间，actor学习收敛到整个状态空间内的高回报子区域。在几个广泛使用的数据集上的实验表明，\modelname比现有工作在大型状态空间上收敛得更快。此外，\modelname不仅生成具有更高回报的候选者，而且还显著提高了它们的多样性。

TLDR: This paper introduces Partial GFlowNet, a method to accelerate GFlowNet convergence in large state spaces by partitioning the space and strategically switching between regions. It claims faster convergence, higher rewards, and improved diversity in generated candidates.

Authors: Xuan Yu, Xu Wang, Rui Zhu, Yudong Zhang, Yang Wang

Optimizing Agent Planning for Security and Autonomy

Abstract (English): Indirect prompt injection attacks threaten AI agents that execute consequential actions, motivating deterministic system-level defenses. Such defenses can provably block unsafe actions by enforcing confidentiality and integrity policies, but currently appear costly: they reduce task completion rates and increase token usage compared to probabilistic defenses. We argue that existing evaluations miss a key benefit of system-level defenses: reduced reliance on human oversight. We introduce autonomy metrics to quantify this benefit: the fraction of consequential actions an agent can execute without human-in-the-loop (HITL) approval while preserving security. To increase autonomy, we design a security-aware agent that (i) introduces richer HITL interactions, and (ii) explicitly plans for both task progress and policy compliance. We implement this agent design atop an existing information-flow control defense against prompt injection and evaluate it on the AgentDojo and WASP benchmarks. Experiments show that this approach yields higher autonomy without sacrificing utility.

摘要（中文）: 间接提示注入攻击威胁着执行重要行动的AI智能体，因此需要确定性的系统级防御。 这种防御可以通过强制执行保密性和完整性策略来可靠地阻止不安全的行为，但目前看来代价高昂：与概率性防御相比，它们降低了任务完成率并增加了token使用量。我们认为，现有的评估忽略了系统级防御的一个关键优势：减少对人工监督的依赖。我们引入自主性指标来量化这一优势：在保持安全性的前提下，智能体无需人工干预(HITL)许可即可执行的重要行动的比例。为了提高自主性，我们设计了一个具有安全意识的智能体，该智能体（i）引入更丰富的HITL交互，以及（ii）明确规划任务进度和策略合规性。我们在现有的针对提示注入的信息流控制防御之上实施此智能体设计，并在AgentDojo和WASP基准测试上对其进行评估。实验表明，这种方法可在不牺牲效用的情况下产生更高的自主性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a security-aware agent that optimizes autonomy by planning for both task progress and policy compliance, evaluated with increased autonomy without sacrificing utility on standard benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种安全感知代理，通过规划任务进度和策略合规性来优化自主性，并在标准基准上评估其自主性，而无需牺牲实用性。

Authors: Aashish Kolluri, Rishi Sharma, Manuel Costa, Boris Köpf, Tobias Nießen, Mark Russinovich, Shruti Tople, Santiago Zanella-Béguelin

Provably Efficient Algorithms for S- and Non-Rectangular Robust MDPs with General Parameterization

Abstract (English): We study robust Markov decision processes (RMDPs) with general policy parameterization under s-rectangular and non-rectangular uncertainty sets. Prior work is largely limited to tabular policies, and hence either lacks sample complexity guarantees or incurs high computational cost. Our method reduces the average reward RMDPs to entropy-regularized discounted robust MDPs, restoring strong duality and enabling tractable equilibrium computation. We prove novel Lipschitz and Lipschitz-smoothness properties for general policy parameterizations that extends to infinite state spaces. To address infinite-horizon gradient estimation, we introduce a multilevel Monte Carlo gradient estimator with $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity, a factor of $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-2})$ improvement over prior work. Building on this, we design a projected gradient descent algorithm for s-rectangular uncertainty ($\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$) and a Frank--Wolfe algorithm for non-rectangular uncertainty ($\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$ discounted, $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10.5})$ average reward), significantly improving prior results in both the discounted setting and average reward setting. Our work is the first one to provide sample complexity guarantees for RMDPs with general policy parameterization beyond $(s, a)$-rectangularity. It also provides the first such guarantees in the average reward setting and improves existing bounds for discounted robust MDPs.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了具有一般策略参数化下的稳健马尔可夫决策过程（RMDPs），包括s-矩形和非矩形不确定性集合。先前的工作在很大程度上局限于表格型策略，因此要么缺乏样本复杂度保证，要么导致高昂的计算成本。我们的方法将平均奖励RMDPs转化为熵正则化的折扣稳健MDPs，从而恢复了强对偶性，并实现了易于处理的均衡计算。我们证明了对于一般策略参数化的新的 Lipschitz 和 Lipschitz 光滑性属性，该属性可扩展到无限状态空间。为了解决无限视界梯度估计问题，我们引入了一种多层蒙特卡洛梯度估计器，其样本复杂度为 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$，比先前的工作提高了 $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-2})$ 倍。在此基础上，我们为 s-矩形不确定性设计了一种投影梯度下降算法（$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$），并为非矩形不确定性设计了一种 Frank--Wolfe 算法（折扣奖励 $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$，平均奖励 $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10.5})$），显著改进了折扣设置和平均奖励设置中的先前结果。我们的工作是第一个为除 $(s, a)$-矩形性之外的具有一般策略参数化的 RMDPs 提供样本复杂度保证的工作。它还提供了第一个平均奖励设置中的此类保证，并改进了现有折扣稳健 MDPs 的界限。

TLDR: This paper proposes provably efficient algorithms for robust MDPs with general policy parameterization, improving sample complexity in both discounted and average reward settings, including the first such guarantees beyond (s, a)-rectangularity and in the average reward setting.

简要说明: 本文提出了针对具有通用策略参数化的鲁棒MDP的高效算法，改进了折扣和平均奖励环境下的样本复杂度，包括在(s, a)-矩形之外和平均奖励环境中的第一个此类保证。

Authors: Anirudh Satheesh, Ziyi Chen, Furong Huang, Heng Huang

Decentralized Multi-Robot Obstacle Detection and Tracking in a Maritime Scenario

Abstract (English): Autonomous aerial-surface robot teams are promising for maritime monitoring. Robust deployment requires reliable perception over reflective water and scalable coordination under limited communication. We present a decentralized multi-robot framework for detecting and tracking floating containers using multiple UAVs cooperating with an autonomous surface vessel. Each UAV performs YOLOv8 and stereo-disparity-based visual detection, then tracks targets with per-object EKFs using uncertainty-aware data association. Compact track summaries are exchanged and fused conservatively via covariance intersection, ensuring consistency under unknown correlations. An information-driven assignment module allocates targets and selects UAV hover viewpoints by trading expected uncertainty reduction against travel effort and safety separation. Simulation results in a maritime scenario demonstrate improved coverage, localization accuracy, and tracking consistency while maintaining modest communication requirements.

摘要（中文）: 以下是翻译结果： 自主水空机器人团队在海洋监测方面具有广阔前景。鲁棒的部署需要对反射水面的可靠感知以及在有限通信下的可扩展协调。我们提出了一种去中心化的多机器人框架，用于利用多个无人机与自主水面船只合作，探测和跟踪漂浮集装箱。每个无人机执行YOLOv8和基于立体视差的视觉检测，然后使用基于物体卡尔曼滤波器（EKF）并采用不确定性感知的数据关联来跟踪目标。紧凑的轨迹摘要通过协方差交叉（covariance intersection）进行保守的交换和融合，从而确保在未知相关性下的数据一致性。一个信息驱动的分配模块通过权衡预期不确定性降低与行程努力和安全间距，来分配目标并选择无人机的悬停视点。海上场景的仿真结果表明，在保持适度通信需求的同时，覆盖范围、定位精度和跟踪一致性均得到改善。

Authors: Muhammad Farhan Ahmed, Vincent Frémont

PhyNiKCE: A Neurosymbolic Agentic Framework for Autonomous Computational Fluid Dynamics

Abstract (English): The deployment of autonomous agents for Computational Fluid Dynamics (CFD), is critically limited by the probabilistic nature of Large Language Models (LLMs), which struggle to enforce the strict conservation laws and numerical stability required for physics-based simulations. Reliance on purely semantic Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) often leads to "context poisoning," where agents generate linguistically plausible but physically invalid configurations due to a fundamental Semantic-Physical Disconnect. To bridge this gap, this work introduces PhyNiKCE (Physical and Numerical Knowledgeable Context Engineering), a neurosymbolic agentic framework for trustworthy engineering. Unlike standard black-box agents, PhyNiKCE decouples neural planning from symbolic validation. It employs a Symbolic Knowledge Engine that treats simulation setup as a Constraint Satisfaction Problem, rigidly enforcing physical constraints via a Deterministic RAG Engine with specialized retrieval strategies for solvers, turbulence models, and boundary conditions. Validated through rigorous OpenFOAM experiments on practical, non-tutorial CFD tasks using Gemini-2.5-Pro/Flash, PhyNiKCE demonstrates a 96% relative improvement over state-of-the-art baselines. Furthermore, by replacing trial-and-error with knowledge-driven initialization, the framework reduced autonomous self-correction loops by 59% while simultaneously lowering LLM token consumption by 17%. These results demonstrate that decoupling neural generation from symbolic constraint enforcement significantly enhances robustness and efficiency. While validated on CFD, this architecture offers a scalable, auditable paradigm for Trustworthy Artificial Intelligence in broader industrial automation.

摘要（中文）: 用于计算流体动力学（CFD）的自主智能体的部署受到大语言模型（LLM）概率性质的严重限制，因为它们难以执行基于物理仿真的严格守恒定律和数值稳定性要求。仅仅依赖语义检索增强生成（RAG）常常导致“上下文污染”，即智能体生成语言上看似合理但物理上无效的配置，这是由于根本性的语义-物理脱节造成的。为了弥合这一差距，本研究引入了PhyNiKCE（物理与数值知识化上下文工程），这是一个用于可信工程的神经符号智能体框架。与标准的黑盒智能体不同，PhyNiKCE将神经规划与符号验证解耦。它采用一个符号知识引擎，将仿真设置视为一个约束满足问题，通过具有专业检索策略（用于求解器、湍流模型和边界条件）的确定性RAG引擎，严格执行物理约束。通过使用Gemini-2.5-Pro/Flash在实际的、非教程CFD任务上进行的严格OpenFOAM实验验证，PhyNiKCE比最先进的基线方法表现出96%的相对改进。此外，通过用知识驱动的初始化代替试错法，该框架将自主自纠正循环减少了59%，同时降低了17%的LLM Token消耗。这些结果表明，将神经生成与符号约束执行解耦可以显著提高鲁棒性和效率。虽然在CFD上进行了验证，但这种架构为更广泛的工业自动化领域中的可信人工智能提供了一个可扩展、可审计的范例。

TLDR: PhyNiKCE is a neurosymbolic framework that improves the accuracy and efficiency of autonomous agents for CFD by decoupling neural planning from symbolic validation and enforcing physical constraints.

简要说明: PhyNiKCE是一个神经符号框架，通过将神经规划与符号验证分离并强制执行物理约束，提高了用于CFD的自主代理的准确性和效率。

Authors: E Fan, Lisong Shi, Zhengtong Li, Chih-yung Wen

How to Sample High Quality 3D Fractals for Action Recognition Pre-Training?

Abstract (English): Synthetic datasets are being recognized in the deep learning realm as a valuable alternative to exhaustively labeled real data. One such synthetic data generation method is Formula Driven Supervised Learning (FDSL), which can provide an infinite number of perfectly labeled data through a formula driven approach, such as fractals or contours. FDSL does not have common drawbacks like manual labor, privacy and other ethical concerns. In this work we generate 3D fractals using 3D Iterated Function Systems (IFS) for pre-training an action recognition model. The fractals are temporally transformed to form a video that is used as a pre-training dataset for downstream task of action recognition. We find that standard methods of generating fractals are slow and produce degenerate 3D fractals. Therefore, we systematically explore alternative ways of generating fractals and finds that overly-restrictive approaches, while generating aesthetically pleasing fractals, are detrimental for downstream task performance. We propose a novel method, Targeted Smart Filtering, to address both the generation speed and fractal diversity issue. The method reports roughly 100 times faster sampling speed and achieves superior downstream performance against other 3D fractal filtering methods.

摘要（中文）: 合成数据集正逐渐被深度学习领域认可为一种替代详尽标注的真实数据的有价值方案。其中一种合成数据生成方法是公式驱动的监督学习 (FDSL)，它可以通过公式驱动的方式，如分形或轮廓，提供无限数量的完美标注数据。FDSL 不存在人工劳动、隐私和其他伦理问题等常见缺点。在这项工作中，我们使用 3D 迭代函数系统 (IFS) 生成 3D 分形来预训练一个动作识别模型。这些分形经过时间变换形成视频，用作动作识别下游任务的预训练数据集。我们发现，生成分形的标准方法速度慢且会产生退化的 3D 分形。因此，我们系统地探索了生成分形的替代方法，并发现过于严格的方法虽然能生成美观的分形，但对下游任务的性能不利。我们提出了一种新颖的方法，称为定向智能过滤，以解决生成速度和分形多样性问题。该方法报告了大约快 100 倍的采样速度，并实现了优于其他 3D 分形过滤方法的下游性能。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel method called Targeted Smart Filtering for generating 3D fractals for action recognition pre-training, achieving faster sampling speeds and superior downstream performance compared to other fractal filtering methods.

Authors: Marko Putak, Thomas B. Moeslund, Joakim Bruslund Haurum

From Circuits to Dynamics: Understanding and Stabilizing Failure in 3D Diffusion Transformers

Abstract (English): Reliable surface completion from sparse point clouds underpins many applications spanning content creation and robotics. While 3D diffusion transformers attain state-of-the-art results on this task, we uncover that they exhibit a catastrophic mode of failure: arbitrarily small on-surface perturbations to the input point cloud can fracture the output into multiple disconnected pieces -- a phenomenon we call Meltdown. Using activation-patching from mechanistic interpretability, we localize Meltdown to a single early denoising cross-attention activation. We find that the singular-value spectrum of this activation provides a scalar proxy: its spectral entropy rises when fragmentation occurs and returns to baseline when patched. Interpreted through diffusion dynamics, we show that this proxy tracks a symmetry-breaking bifurcation of the reverse process. Guided by this insight, we introduce PowerRemap, a test-time control that stabilizes sparse point-cloud conditioning. We demonstrate that Meltdown persists across state-of-the-art architectures (WaLa, Make-a-Shape), datasets (GSO, SimJEB) and denoising strategies (DDPM, DDIM), and that PowerRemap effectively counters this failure with stabilization rates of up to 98.3%. Overall, this work is a case study on how diffusion model behavior can be understood and guided based on mechanistic analysis, linking a circuit-level cross-attention mechanism to diffusion-dynamics accounts of trajectory bifurcations.

摘要（中文）: 从稀疏点云进行可靠的表面补全支撑着内容创作和机器人领域的诸多应用。虽然3D扩散Transformer在这项任务上取得了最先进的结果，但我们发现它们表现出一种灾难性的失效模式：输入点云上任意小的表面扰动都可能使输出破碎成多个不连通的部分——我们称之为“熔毁”。利用来自机制可解释性的激活补丁技术，我们将“熔毁”定位到单个早期去噪交叉注意力激活。我们发现，该激活的奇异值谱提供了一个标量代理：其谱熵在分段发生时升高，并在打补丁时恢复到基线水平。通过扩散动力学解释，我们表明该代理跟踪了逆过程的一个对称性破缺分叉。受此启发，我们引入了PowerRemap，这是一种测试时控件，用于稳定稀疏点云条件反射。我们证明了“熔毁”在最先进的架构（WaLa、Make-a-Shape）、数据集（GSO、SimJEB）和去噪策略（DDPM、DDIM）中持续存在，并且PowerRemap通过高达98.3%的稳定率有效地克服了这种失效。总而言之，这项工作是一个案例研究，展示了扩散模型行为如何基于机制分析来理解和引导，将电路级的交叉注意力机制与关于轨迹分叉的扩散动力学解释联系起来。

TLDR: The paper identifies and mitigates a fragility (Meltdown) in 3D diffusion transformers for surface completion, linking it to a cross-attention mechanism and diffusion dynamics, and proposes a stabilization method (PowerRemap).

简要说明: 该论文发现并缓解了3D扩散Transformer用于表面补全时的一种缺陷（Meltdown），将其与交叉注意力机制和扩散动力学联系起来，并提出了一种稳定方法（PowerRemap）。

Authors: Maximilian Plattner, Fabian Paischer, Johannes Brandstetter, Arturs Berzins

Convex Markov Games and Beyond: New Proof of Existence, Characterization and Learning Algorithms for Nash Equilibria

Abstract (English): Convex Markov Games (cMGs) were recently introduced as a broad class of multi-agent learning problems that generalize Markov games to settings where strategic agents optimize general utilities beyond additive rewards. While cMGs expand the modeling frontier, their theoretical foundations, particularly the structure of Nash equilibria (NE) and guarantees for learning algorithms, are not yet well understood. In this work, we address these gaps for an extension of cMGs, which we term General Utility Markov Games (GUMGs), capturing new applications requiring coupling between agents' occupancy measures. We prove that in GUMGs, Nash equilibria coincide with the fixed points of projected pseudo-gradient dynamics (i.e., first-order stationary points), enabled by a novel agent-wise gradient domination property. This insight also yields a simple proof of NE existence using Brouwer's fixed-point theorem. We further show the existence of Markov perfect equilibria. Building on this characterization, we establish a policy gradient theorem for GUMGs and design a model-free policy gradient algorithm. For potential GUMGs, we establish iteration complexity guarantees for computing approximate-NE under exact gradients and provide sample complexity bounds in both the generative model and on-policy settings. Our results extend beyond prior work restricted to zero-sum cMGs, providing the first theoretical analysis of common-interest cMGs.

摘要（中文）: 凸马尔可夫博弈（cMGs）最近被引入，作为一种广泛的多智能体学习问题，它将马尔可夫博弈推广到博弈参与者优化超出加性奖励的一般效用的环境。尽管cMGs扩展了建模的前沿，但它们的理论基础，特别是纳什均衡（NE）的结构以及学习算法的保证，尚未得到充分理解。在这项工作中，我们针对cMGs的扩展形式，即一般效用马尔可夫博弈（GUMGs），填补了这些空白，它捕捉了需要智能体占用度量之间耦合的新应用。我们证明了在GUMGs中，纳什均衡与投影伪梯度动力学的固定点（即，一阶静止点）重合，这得益于一种新颖的智能体层面的梯度支配性质。这一洞见也促成了一种使用布劳威尔不动点定理证明纳什均衡存在性的简单方法。我们进一步证明了马尔可夫完美均衡的存在性。基于这一表征，我们建立了GUMGs的策略梯度定理，并设计了一种无模型的策略梯度算法。对于势GUMGs，我们建立了在精确梯度下计算近似纳什均衡的迭代复杂性保证，并在生成模型和在线策略设置中提供了样本复杂性界限。我们的结果超越了先前局限于零和cMGs的工作，提供了对共同利益cMGs的首次理论分析。

TLDR: This paper introduces General Utility Markov Games (GUMGs), an extension of Convex Markov Games, proves Nash equilibria properties, derives a policy gradient theorem, and provides learning algorithm analysis, including complexity guarantees.

简要说明: 本文介绍了通用效用马尔可夫博弈（GUMGs），它是凸马尔可夫博弈的扩展。论文证明了纳什均衡性质，推导了策略梯度定理，并提供了学习算法分析，包括复杂性保证。

Authors: Anas Barakat, Ioannis Panageas, Antonios Varvitsiotis

A$^{2}$V-SLP: Alignment-Aware Variational Modeling for Disentangled Sign Language Production

Abstract (English): Building upon recent structural disentanglement frameworks for sign language production, we propose A$^{2}$V-SLP, an alignment-aware variational framework that learns articulator-wise disentangled latent distributions rather than deterministic embeddings. A disentangled Variational Autoencoder (VAE) encodes ground-truth sign pose sequences and extracts articulator-specific mean and variance vectors, which are used as distributional supervision for training a non-autoregressive Transformer. Given text embeddings, the Transformer predicts both latent means and log-variances, while the VAE decoder reconstructs the final sign pose sequences through stochastic sampling at the decoding stage. This formulation maintains articulator-level representations by avoiding deterministic latent collapse through distributional latent modeling. In addition, we integrate a gloss attention mechanism to strengthen alignment between linguistic input and articulated motion. Experimental results show consistent gains over deterministic latent regression, achieving state-of-the-art back-translation performance and improved motion realism in a fully gloss-free setting.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了A$^{2}$V-SLP，这是一种对齐感知的变分框架，基于近期的手语生成结构解耦框架构建，它学习关节级别的解耦潜在分布，而非确定性嵌入。 一个解耦的变分自编码器（VAE）编码真实的手语姿势序列，并提取关节特定的均值和方差向量，这些向量被用作分布监督来训练一个非自回归的Transformer。 给定文本嵌入，Transformer预测潜在均值和对数方差，而VAE解码器在解码阶段通过随机采样重建最终的手语姿势序列。 这种公式通过分布式的潜在建模避免了确定性潜在塌缩，从而保持了关节级别的表示。 此外，我们集成了一种手势词注意力机制，以加强语言输入和关节运动之间的对齐。 实验结果表明，与确定性潜在回归相比，该方法获得了持续的提升，在完全无手势词设置下实现了最先进的反向翻译性能，并提高了运动真实感。

TLDR: The paper introduces A$^{2}$V-SLP, a novel alignment-aware variational framework for sign language production that leverages articulator-wise disentangled latent distributions and a gloss attention mechanism, achieving state-of-the-art back-translation performance and improved motion realism.
