Authors: Sümeyye Meryem Taşyürek, Enis Mücahid İskender, Hacer Yalim Keles

Sample-Free Safety Assessment of Neural Network Controllers via Taylor Methods

Abstract (English): In recent years, artificial neural networks have been increasingly studied as feedback controllers for guidance problems. While effective in complex scenarios, they lack the verification guarantees found in classical guidance policies. Their black-box nature creates significant concerns regarding trustworthiness, limiting their adoption in safety-critical spaceflight applications. This work addresses this gap by developing a method to assess the safety of a trained neural network feedback controller via automatic domain splitting and polynomial bounding. The methodology involves embedding the trained neural network into the system's dynamical equations, rendering the closed-loop system autonomous. The system flow is then approximated by high-order Taylor polynomials, which are subsequently manipulated to construct polynomial maps that project state uncertainties onto an event manifold. Automatic domain splitting ensures the polynomials are accurate over their relevant subdomains, whilst also allowing an extensive state-space to be analysed efficiently. Utilising polynomial bounding techniques, the resulting event values may be rigorously constrained and analysed within individual subdomains, thereby establishing bounds on the range of possible closed-loop outcomes from using such neural network controllers and supporting safety assessment and informed operational decision-making in real-world missions.

摘要（中文）: 近年来，人工神经网络作为制导问题的反馈控制器受到了越来越多的研究。虽然它们在复杂场景中有效，但却缺乏经典制导策略中固有的验证保证。它们的黑箱特性引起了对可信度的重大担忧，限制了它们在安全攸关的航天应用中的采用。本工作通过开发一种通过自动域分割和多项式有界来评估训练后的神经网络反馈控制器安全性的方法，来弥补这一差距。该方法包括将训练后的神经网络嵌入到系统的动力学方程中，使闭环系统成为自治系统。然后，系统流通过高阶泰勒多项式来近似，随后对其进行处理以构建多项式映射，将状态不确定性投影到事件流形上。自动域分割确保多项式在其相关子域内是准确的，同时也允许有效地分析广泛的状态空间。利用多项式有界技术，可以严格约束和分析所得的事件值在各个子域内，从而建立在使用此类神经网络控制器时可能出现的闭环结果范围的界限，并支持真实任务中的安全评估和知情决策。

TLDR: This paper presents a method for assessing the safety of neural network controllers using Taylor methods and domain splitting, aiming to provide verification guarantees for safety-critical applications.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种使用泰勒方法和域分割来评估神经网络控制器安全性的方法，旨在为安全关键型应用提供验证保证。

Authors: Adam Evans, Roberto Armellin

Sub--Riemannian boundary value problems for Optimal Geometric Locomotion

Abstract (English): We propose a geometric model for optimal shape-change-induced motions of slender locomotors, e.g., snakes slithering on sand. In these scenarios, the motion of a body in world coordinates is completely determined by the sequence of shapes it assumes. Specifically, we formulate Lagrangian least-dissipation principles as boundary value problems whose solutions are given by sub-Riemannian geodesics. Notably, our geometric model accounts not only for the energy dissipated by the body's displacement through the environment, but also for the energy dissipated by the animal's metabolism or a robot's actuators to induce shape changes such as bending and stretching, thus capturing overall locomotion efficiency. Our continuous model, together with a consistent time and space discretization, enables numerical computation of sub-Riemannian geodesics for three different types of boundary conditions, i.e., fixing initial and target body, restricting to cyclic motion, or solely prescribing body displacement and orientation. The resulting optimal deformation gaits qualitatively match observed motion trajectories of organisms such as snakes and spermatozoa, as well as known optimality results for low-dimensional systems such as Purcell's swimmers. Moreover, being geometrically less rigid than previous frameworks, our model enables new insights into locomotion mechanisms of, e.g., generalized Purcell's swimmers. The code is publicly available.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种几何模型，用于研究细长运动体（例如在沙地上滑行的蛇）由形状改变引起的最佳运动。在这些情况下，物体在世界坐标系中的运动完全由其所呈现的形状序列决定。具体而言，我们将拉格朗日最小耗散原理表述为边值问题，其解由亚黎曼测地线给出。值得注意的是，我们的几何模型不仅考虑了物体在环境中位移所消耗的能量，还考虑了动物新陈代谢或机器人执行器为诱导形状改变（如弯曲和伸展）所消耗的能量，从而捕捉了整体的运动效率。我们的连续模型与一致的时空离散化方法相结合，可以对三种不同类型的边界条件进行亚黎曼测地线的数值计算，即固定初始和目标物身、限制为循环运动，或仅指定物体的位移和姿态。由此产生的最佳变形步态在定性上与观察到的生物（如蛇和精子）的运动轨迹相匹配，也与低维系统 (如 Purcell 游泳者) 的已知最优结果相符。此外，由于我们的模型在几何上比以往的框架更灵活，因此能够提供对运动机制的新见解，例如广义 Purcell 游泳者的运动机制。代码已公开提供。

TLDR: This paper presents a geometric model for optimal shape-change-induced locomotion of slender locomotors, formulated as a sub-Riemannian boundary value problem, accounting for both movement and shape-change energy dissipation. The model enables computation of optimal gaits that qualitatively match observed motion trajectories. The code is publicly available.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个用于细长运动体最优形变诱导运动的几何模型，将其公式化为一个次黎曼边界值问题，同时考虑了运动和形变能量耗散。该模型能够计算出与观测到的运动轨迹定性匹配的最优步态。代码已公开。

Authors: Oliver Gross, Florine Hartwig, Martin Rumpf, Peter Schröder

Multi Graph Search for High-Dimensional Robot Motion Planning

Abstract (English): Efficient motion planning for high-dimensional robotic systems, such as manipulators and mobile manipulators, is critical for real-time operation and reliable deployment. Although advances in planning algorithms have enhanced scalability to high-dimensional state spaces, these improvements often come at the cost of generating unpredictable, inconsistent motions or requiring excessive computational resources and memory. In this work, we introduce Multi-Graph Search (MGS), a search-based motion planning algorithm that generalizes classical unidirectional and bidirectional search to a multi-graph setting. MGS maintains and incrementally expands multiple implicit graphs over the state space, focusing exploration on high-potential regions while allowing initially disconnected subgraphs to be merged through feasible transitions as the search progresses. We prove that MGS is complete and bounded-suboptimal, and empirically demonstrate its effectiveness on a range of manipulation and mobile manipulation tasks. Demonstrations, benchmarks and code are available at https://multi-graph-search.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 高效的针对高维机器人系统的运动规划，例如机械臂和移动机械臂，对于实时操作和可靠部署至关重要。尽管规划算法的进步提高了对高维状态空间的可扩展性，但这些改进通常以生成不可预测的、不一致的运动或需要过多的计算资源和内存为代价。在这项工作中，我们引入了多图搜索（MGS），一种基于搜索的运动规划算法，它将经典单向和双向搜索推广到多图设置。MGS维护并增量式地扩展状态空间上的多个隐式图，将探索重点放在高潜力区域，同时允许最初断开连接的子图随着搜索的进行通过可行的转换进行合并。我们证明了MGS是完备的且有界次优的，并通过一系列操作和移动操作任务的实验证明了其有效性。演示、基准和代码可在https://multi-graph-search.github.io/获得。

TLDR: The paper introduces Multi-Graph Search (MGS), a complete and bounded-suboptimal search-based motion planning algorithm for high-dimensional robotic systems, improving efficiency and consistency in motion generation.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为多图搜索(MGS)的算法，它是一种完备且有界次优的基于搜索的运动规划算法，用于高维机器人系统，旨在提高运动生成过程中的效率和一致性。

Authors: Itamar Mishani, Maxim Likhachev

Multi UAVs Preflight Planning in a Shared and Dynamic Airspace

Abstract (English): Preflight planning for large-scale Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) fleets in dynamic, shared airspace presents significant challenges, including temporal No-Fly Zones (NFZs), heterogeneous vehicle profiles, and strict delivery deadlines. While Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) provides a formal framework, existing methods often lack the scalability and flexibility required for real-world Unmanned Traffic Management (UTM). We propose DTAPP-IICR: a Delivery-Time Aware Prioritized Planning method with Incremental and Iterative Conflict Resolution. Our framework first generates an initial solution by prioritizing missions based on urgency. Secondly, it computes roundtrip trajectories using SFIPP-ST, a novel 4D single-agent planner (Safe Flight Interval Path Planning with Soft and Temporal Constraints). SFIPP-ST handles heterogeneous UAVs, strictly enforces temporal NFZs, and models inter-agent conflicts as soft constraints. Subsequently, an iterative Large Neighborhood Search, guided by a geometric conflict graph, efficiently resolves any residual conflicts. A completeness-preserving directional pruning technique further accelerates the 3D search. On benchmarks with temporal NFZs, DTAPP-IICR achieves near-100% success with fleets of up to 1,000 UAVs and gains up to 50% runtime reduction from pruning, outperforming batch Enhanced Conflict-Based Search in the UTM context. Scaling successfully in realistic city-scale operations where other priority-based methods fail even at moderate deployments, DTAPP-IICR is positioned as a practical and scalable solution for preflight planning in dense, dynamic urban airspace.

摘要（中文）: 大规模无人机（UAV）机队在动态共享空域中的飞行前规划面临着严峻的挑战，包括时间禁飞区（NFZ）、异构飞行器特性和严格的交付期限。虽然多智能体路径搜索（MAPF）提供了一个正式的框架，但现有方法通常缺乏现实世界无人交通管理（UTM）所需的可扩展性和灵活性。我们提出DTAPP-IICR：一种具有增量和迭代冲突解决的交付时间感知优先级规划方法。我们的框架首先通过基于紧急程度对任务进行优先级排序来生成初始解。其次，它使用SFIPP-ST（一种新型4D单智能体规划器，即具有软约束和时间约束的安全飞行间隔路径规划）计算往返轨迹。SFIPP-ST处理异构无人机，严格执行时间禁飞区，并将智能体间冲突建模为软约束。随后，由几何冲突图引导的迭代大规模邻域搜索有效地解决任何剩余冲突。一种保持完备性的定向剪枝技术进一步加速了3D搜索。在使用时间禁飞区的基准测试中，DTAPP-IICR在使用高达1,000架无人机的机队时实现了接近100%的成功率，并且剪枝带来了高达50%的运行时间缩减，优于UTM环境中的批量增强冲突搜索。DTAPP-IICR在现实城市规模的运营中成功扩展，而其他基于优先级的方法即使在中等部署规模下也会失败，这使其成为密集、动态城市空域中飞行前规划的一种实用且可扩展的解决方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces DTAPP-IICR, a novel and scalable preflight planning method for large UAV fleets in dynamic urban airspace, handling temporal No-Fly Zones, heterogeneous vehicle profiles, and strict delivery deadlines, outperforming existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为DTAPP-IICR的新型可扩展的无人机机群预飞行规划方法，用于应对动态城市空域中大型无人机机群面临的挑战，包括临时禁飞区、异构飞行器配置和严格的交付期限，其性能优于现有方法。

Authors: Amath Sow, Mauricio Rodriguez Cesen, Fabiola Martins Campos de Oliveira, Mariusz Wzorek, Daniel de Leng, Mattias Tiger, Fredrik Heintz, Christian Esteve Rothenberg

Adaptive-Horizon Conflict-Based Search for Closed-Loop Multi-Agent Path Finding

Abstract (English): MAPF is a core coordination problem for large robot fleets in automated warehouses and logistics. Existing approaches are typically either open-loop planners, which generate fixed trajectories and struggle to handle disturbances, or closed-loop heuristics without reliable performance guarantees, limiting their use in safety-critical deployments. This paper presents ACCBS, a closed-loop algorithm built on a finite-horizon variant of CBS with a horizon-changing mechanism inspired by iterative deepening in MPC. ACCBS dynamically adjusts the planning horizon based on the available computational budget, and reuses a single constraint tree to enable seamless transitions between horizons. As a result, it produces high-quality feasible solutions quickly while being asymptotically optimal as the budget increases, exhibiting anytime behavior. Extensive case studies demonstrate that ACCBS combines flexibility to disturbances with strong performance guarantees, effectively bridging the gap between theoretical optimality and practical robustness for large-scale robot deployment.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体路径规划（MAPF）是自动化仓库和物流中大型机器人集群的核心协调问题。现有方法通常要么是开环规划器，生成固定轨迹且难以应对扰动；要么是闭环启发式算法，缺乏可靠的性能保证，限制了其在安全关键部署中的应用。本文提出了一种名为ACCBS的闭环算法，该算法基于CBS的有限视界变体构建，并采用受模型预测控制（MPC）中迭代加深法启发的视界变化机制。ACCBS根据可用的计算预算动态调整规划视界，并重用单个约束树，以实现视界之间的无缝过渡。因此，它能够快速生成高质量的可行解，并在预算增加时渐近最优，展现出随时可用的行为。大量的案例研究表明，ACCBS将应对扰动的灵活性与强大的性能保证相结合，有效地弥合了大规模机器人部署中理论最优性和实际鲁棒性之间的差距。

TLDR: This paper introduces ACCBS, a closed-loop Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) algorithm that dynamically adjusts the planning horizon to balance solution quality and computational efficiency, offering a practical solution for large-scale robot deployments with performance guarantees.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种闭环的多智能体路径规划算法ACCBS，该算法动态调整规划范围，平衡了解决方案的质量和计算效率，为大规模机器人部署提供了一种具有性能保证的实用解决方案。

Authors: Jiarui Li, Federico Pecora, Runyu Zhang, Gioele Zardini

GSO-SLAM: Bidirectionally Coupled Gaussian Splatting and Direct Visual Odometry

Abstract (English): We propose GSO-SLAM, a real-time monocular dense SLAM system that leverages Gaussian scene representation. Unlike existing methods that couple tracking and mapping with a unified scene, incurring computational costs, or loosely integrate them with well-structured tracking frameworks, introducing redundancies, our method bidirectionally couples Visual Odometry (VO) and Gaussian Splatting (GS). Specifically, our approach formulates joint optimization within an Expectation-Maximization (EM) framework, enabling the simultaneous refinement of VO-derived semi-dense depth estimates and the GS representation without additional computational overhead. Moreover, we present Gaussian Splat Initialization, which utilizes image information, keyframe poses, and pixel associations from VO to produce close approximations to the final Gaussian scene, thereby eliminating the need for heuristic methods. Through extensive experiments, we validate the effectiveness of our method, showing that it not only operates in real time but also achieves state-of-the-art geometric/photometric fidelity of the reconstructed scene and tracking accuracy.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了GSO-SLAM，一种利用高斯场景表示的实时单目稠密SLAM系统。与将跟踪和地图构建耦合在统一场景中，导致计算成本增加，或将它们与结构良好的跟踪框架松散集成，引入冗余的现有方法不同，我们的方法双向耦合视觉里程计(VO)和高斯溅射(GS)。具体来说，我们的方法在期望最大化(EM)框架内制定联合优化，从而能够同时细化VO导出的半稠密深度估计和GS表示，而无需额外的计算开销。此外，我们提出了高斯溅射初始化，它利用图像信息、关键帧位姿和来自VO的像素关联，以产生接近最终高斯场景的近似值，从而消除了对启发式方法的需求。通过广泛的实验，我们验证了我们方法的有效性，表明它不仅能够实时运行，而且实现了重建场景和跟踪精度的最先进的几何/光度保真度。

TLDR: GSO-SLAM introduces a real-time monocular dense SLAM system that bidirectionally couples Visual Odometry and Gaussian Splatting within an EM framework, achieving state-of-the-art performance without extra computation, and presents a novel Gaussian Splat Initialization method.

简要说明: GSO-SLAM 提出了一种实时单目稠密SLAM系统，在EM框架内双向耦合了视觉里程计和高斯溅射，无需额外计算即可实现最先进的性能，并提出了一种新颖的高斯溅射初始化方法。

Authors: Jiung Yeon, Seongbo Ha, Hyeonwoo Yu

HyperDet: 3D Object Detection with Hyper 4D Radar Point Clouds

Abstract (English): 4D mmWave radar provides weather-robust, velocity-aware measurements and is more cost-effective than LiDAR. However, radar-only 3D detection still trails LiDAR-based systems because radar point clouds are sparse, irregular, and often corrupted by multipath noise, yielding weak and unstable geometry. We present HyperDet, a detector-agnostic radar-only 3D detection framework that constructs a task-aware hyper 4D radar point cloud for standard LiDAR-oriented detectors. HyperDet aggregates returns from multiple surround-view 4D radars over consecutive frames to improve coverage and density, then applies geometry-aware cross-sensor consensus validation with a lightweight self-consistency check outside overlap regions to suppress inconsistent returns. It further integrates a foreground-focused diffusion module with training-time mixed radar-LiDAR supervision to densify object structures while lifting radar attributes (e.g., Doppler, RCS); the model is distilled into a consistency model for single-step inference. On MAN TruckScenes, HyperDet consistently improves over raw radar inputs with VoxelNeXt and CenterPoint, partially narrowing the radar-LiDAR gap. These results show that input-level refinement enables radar to better leverage LiDAR-oriented detectors without architectural modifications.

摘要（中文）: 4D毫米波雷达能够提供抗恶劣天气、感知速度的测量数据，并且比激光雷达更具成本效益。然而，纯雷达的3D目标检测性能仍然落后于基于激光雷达的系统，因为雷达点云稀疏、不规则，并且经常被多径噪声干扰，导致几何信息微弱且不稳定。我们提出了HyperDet，一个与检测器无关的纯雷达3D目标检测框架，它构建了一个任务相关的超4D雷达点云，供标准的、面向激光雷达的检测器使用。HyperDet聚合了来自多个环视4D雷达在连续帧上的回波，以提高覆盖率和密度，然后应用几何感知的跨传感器一致性验证，并在重叠区域外进行轻量级的自洽性检查，以抑制不一致的回波。它进一步整合了一个以前景为中心的扩散模块，在训练时采用混合雷达-激光雷达监督，以增强目标结构的密度，同时提升雷达属性（例如，多普勒、雷达截面积）；该模型被提炼成一个一致性模型，用于单步推理。在MAN TruckScenes数据集上，HyperDet在使用VoxelNeXt和CenterPoint时，始终优于原始雷达输入的结果，部分缩小了雷达与激光雷达之间的差距。这些结果表明，输入层面的优化能够使雷达更好地利用面向激光雷达的检测器，而无需进行架构上的修改。

TLDR: The paper introduces HyperDet, a radar-only 3D object detection framework that refines radar point clouds through aggregation, validation, and diffusion, demonstrating improved performance on the MAN TruckScenes dataset when used with standard LiDAR-oriented detectors.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HyperDet，一个纯雷达的3D目标检测框架，通过聚合、验证和扩散来优化雷达点云，并在MAN TruckScenes数据集上展示了与标准激光雷达检测器结合使用时性能的提升。

Authors: Yichun Xiao, Runwei Guan, Fangqiang Ding

Multi-UAV Trajectory Optimization for Bearing-Only Localization in GPS Denied Environments

Abstract (English): Accurate localization of maritime targets by unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) remains challenging in GPS-denied environments. UAVs equipped with gimballed electro-optical sensors are typically used to localize targets, however, reliance on these sensors increases mechanical complexity, cost, and susceptibility to single-point failures, limiting scalability and robustness in multi-UAV operations. This work presents a new trajectory optimization framework that enables cooperative target localization using UAVs with fixed, non-gimballed cameras operating in coordination with a surface vessel. This estimation-aware optimization generates dynamically feasible trajectories that explicitly account for mission constraints, platform dynamics, and out-of-frame events. Estimation-aware trajectories outperform heuristic paths by reducing localization error by more than a factor of two, motivating their use in cooperative operations. Results further demonstrate that coordinated UAVs with fixed, non-gimballed cameras achieve localization accuracy that meets or exceeds that of single gimballed systems, while substantially lowering system complexity and cost, enabling scalability, and enhancing mission resilience.

摘要（中文）: 在GPS拒止环境中，利用无人机(UAV)对海上目标进行精确定位仍然具有挑战性。通常使用配备万向节光电传感器的无人机来定位目标，然而，对这些传感器的依赖增加了机械复杂性、成本以及对单点故障的敏感性，限制了多无人机操作的可扩展性和稳健性。本研究提出了一个全新的轨迹优化框架，使配备固定式非万向节相机的无人机能够与水面舰艇协同进行目标协同定位。这种估计感知优化方法生成动态可行的轨迹，明确考虑任务约束、平台动力学和视场外事件。估计感知轨迹在降低定位误差方面优于启发式路径超过两倍，这促使它们应用于协同操作中。结果进一步表明，配备固定式非万向节相机的协同无人机能够实现达到或超过单个万向节系统的定位精度，同时显著降低系统复杂度和成本，从而实现可扩展性并增强任务弹性。

Authors: Alfonso Sciacchitano, Liraz Mudrik, Sean Kragelund, Isaac Kaminer

Resource-Aware Deployment Optimization for Collaborative Intrusion Detection in Layered Networks

Abstract (English): Collaborative Intrusion Detection Systems (CIDS) are increasingly adopted to counter cyberattacks, as their collaborative nature enables them to adapt to diverse scenarios across heterogeneous environments. As distributed critical infrastructure operates in rapidly evolving environments, such as drones in both civil and military domains, there is a growing need for CIDS architectures that can flexibly accommodate these dynamic changes. In this study, we propose a novel CIDS framework designed for easy deployment across diverse distributed environments. The framework dynamically optimizes detector allocation per node based on available resources and data types, enabling rapid adaptation to new operational scenarios with minimal computational overhead. We first conducted a comprehensive literature review to identify key characteristics of existing CIDS architectures. Based on these insights and real-world use cases, we developed our CIDS framework, which we evaluated using several distributed datasets that feature different attack chains and network topologies. Notably, we introduce a public dataset based on a realistic cyberattack targeting a ground drone aimed at sabotaging critical infrastructure. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed CIDS framework can achieve adaptive, efficient intrusion detection in distributed settings, automatically reconfiguring detectors to maintain an optimal configuration, without requiring heavy computation, since all experiments were conducted on edge devices.

摘要（中文）: 协同入侵检测系统（CIDS）正日益被采用来对抗网络攻击，因为其协同特性使其能够适应异构环境中的各种场景。随着分布式关键基础设施在快速演进的环境中运行，例如民用和军用领域的无人机，对能够灵活适应这些动态变化的CIDS架构的需求日益增长。在本研究中，我们提出了一种新型CIDS框架，旨在便于在各种分布式环境中部署。该框架基于可用资源和数据类型，动态优化每个节点的检测器分配，从而能够快速适应新的操作场景，且计算开销最小。我们首先进行了全面的文献综述，以识别现有CIDS架构的关键特征。基于这些见解和实际用例，我们开发了我们的CIDS框架，并使用包含不同攻击链和网络拓扑的多个分布式数据集对其进行了评估。值得注意的是，我们引入了一个公开数据集，该数据集基于针对地面无人机的真实网络攻击，旨在破坏关键基础设施。实验结果表明，所提出的CIDS框架能够在分布式环境中实现自适应、高效的入侵检测，自动重新配置检测器以维持最佳配置，而无需大量的计算，因为所有实验都是在边缘设备上进行的。

Authors: André García Gómez, Ines Rieger, Wolfgang Hotwagner, Max Landauer, Markus Wurzenberger, Florian Skopik, Edgar Weippl

OMEGA-Avatar: One-shot Modeling of 360° Gaussian Avatars

Abstract (English): Creating high-fidelity, animatable 3D avatars from a single image remains a formidable challenge. We identified three desirable attributes of avatar generation: 1) the method should be feed-forward, 2) model a 360° full-head, and 3) should be animation-ready. However, current work addresses only two of the three points simultaneously. To address these limitations, we propose OMEGA-Avatar, the first feed-forward framework that simultaneously generates a generalizable, 360°-complete, and animatable 3D Gaussian head from a single image. Starting from a feed-forward and animatable framework, we address the 360° full-head avatar generation problem with two novel components. First, to overcome poor hair modeling in full-head avatar generation, we introduce a semantic-aware mesh deformation module that integrates multi-view normals to optimize a FLAME head with hair while preserving its topology structure. Second, to enable effective feed-forward decoding of full-head features, we propose a multi-view feature splatting module that constructs a shared canonical UV representation from features across multiple views through differentiable bilinear splatting, hierarchical UV mapping, and visibility-aware fusion. This approach preserves both global structural coherence and local high-frequency details across all viewpoints, ensuring 360° consistency without per-instance optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OMEGA-Avatar achieves state-of-the-art performance, significantly outperforming existing baselines in 360° full-head completeness while robustly preserving identity across different viewpoints.

摘要（中文）: 从单张图像创建高保真、可动画的3D头像仍然是一个巨大的挑战。我们确定了头像生成的三个理想属性：1) 该方法应该是前馈的， 2) 对360°全头部进行建模，以及3) 应当是为动画而生的。然而，目前的工作仅能同时满足这三点中的两点。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了OMEGA-Avatar，这是第一个前馈框架，它能同时从单张图像生成可泛化、360°完整且可动画的3D高斯头部。从一个前馈且可动画的框架出发，我们通过两个新颖的组件来解决360°全头部头像生成问题。首先，为了克服全头部头像生成中糟糕的头发建模问题，我们引入了一个语义感知的网格变形模块，该模块整合了多视角法线来优化带有头发的FLAME头部，同时保留其拓扑结构。其次，为了实现全头部特征的有效前馈解码，我们提出了一个多视角特征喷溅模块，该模块通过可微的双线性喷溅、分层UV映射和可见性感知的融合，从多个视角的特征构建一个共享的规范UV表示。这种方法保留了所有视点的全局结构一致性和局部高频细节，确保了360°一致性，而无需进行逐实例优化。大量实验表明，OMEGA-Avatar实现了最先进的性能，在360°全头部完整性方面显著优于现有基线，同时稳健地保留了不同视角的身份信息。

TLDR: The paper introduces OMEGA-Avatar, a novel feed-forward framework for generating animatable, 360-degree complete 3D Gaussian head avatars from a single image, addressing limitations in existing approaches regarding full-head modeling and animation readiness.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了OMEGA-Avatar，一种新颖的前馈框架，用于从单张图像生成可动画的、360度完整的3D高斯头部化身，解决了现有方法在全头部建模和动画就绪方面的局限性。

Authors: Zehao Xia, Yiqun Wang, Zhengda Lu, Kai Liu, Jun Xiao, Peter Wonka

WorldTree: Towards 4D Dynamic Worlds from Monocular Video using Tree-Chains

Abstract (English): Dynamic reconstruction has achieved remarkable progress, but there remain challenges in monocular input for more practical applications. The prevailing works attempt to construct efficient motion representations, but lack a unified spatiotemporal decomposition framework, suffering from either holistic temporal optimization or coupled hierarchical spatial composition. To this end, we propose WorldTree, a unified framework comprising Temporal Partition Tree (TPT) that enables coarse-to-fine optimization based on the inheritance-based partition tree structure for hierarchical temporal decomposition, and Spatial Ancestral Chains (SAC) that recursively query ancestral hierarchical structure to provide complementary spatial dynamics while specializing motion representations across ancestral nodes. Experimental results on different datasets indicate that our proposed method achieves 8.26% improvement of LPIPS on NVIDIA-LS and 9.09% improvement of mLPIPS on DyCheck compared to the second-best method. Code: https://github.com/iCVTEAM/WorldTree.

摘要（中文）: 动态重建已经取得了显著进展，但在单目输入方面仍然存在挑战，限制了其在更实际应用中的普及。现有的工作致力于构建高效的运动表示，但缺乏统一的时空分解框架，要么采用整体时间优化，要么采用耦合的分层空间组合。为此，我们提出了 WorldTree，一个统一的框架，包含时间分割树（TPT）和空间祖先链（SAC）。时间分割树通过基于继承的分割树结构实现由粗到精的优化，从而实现分层时间分解；空间祖先链递归查询祖先层级结构，提供互补的空间动态，同时对跨祖先节点的运动表示进行特殊化处理。在不同数据集上的实验结果表明，与第二好的方法相比，我们提出的方法在 NVIDIA-LS 上实现了 8.26% 的 LPIPS 提升，在 DyCheck 上实现了 9.09% 的 mLPIPS 提升。代码：https://github.com/iCVTEAM/WorldTree。

TLDR: The paper introduces WorldTree, a framework for dynamic 4D reconstruction from monocular video using Temporal Partition Trees and Spatial Ancestral Chains, achieving improved performance on benchmark datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了WorldTree，一个从单目视频进行动态4D重建的框架，它使用时间分割树和空间祖先链，并在基准数据集上取得了更好的性能。

Authors: Qisen Wang, Yifan Zhao, Jia Li

Advancing Digital Twin Generation Through a Novel Simulation Framework and Quantitative Benchmarking

Abstract (English): The generation of 3D models from real-world objects has often been accomplished through photogrammetry, i.e., by taking 2D photos from a variety of perspectives and then triangulating matched point-based features to create a textured mesh. Many design choices exist within this framework for the generation of digital twins, and differences between such approaches are largely judged qualitatively. Here, we present and test a novel pipeline for generating synthetic images from high-quality 3D models and programmatically generated camera poses. 摘要（中文）: 从真实世界物体生成3D模型通常通过摄影测量法实现，即从多个视角拍摄2D照片，然后三角化匹配的点特征以创建纹理网格。在这个框架下，存在许多数字孪生生成的设计选择，而不同方法之间的差异通常是定性判断的。在这里，我们提出并测试了一种新颖的流程，该流程从高质量3D模型和程序化生成的相机位姿中生成合成图像。这使得能够进行各种可重复、可量化的实验，从而将虚拟相机参数和虚拟对象的真实信息与这些视角和对象的重建估计进行比较。

Authors: Jacob Rubinstein, Avi Donaty, Don Engel

PathCRF: Ball-Free Soccer Event Detection via Possession Path Inference from Player Trajectories

Abstract (English): Despite recent advances in AI, event data collection in soccer still relies heavily on labor-intensive manual annotation. Although prior work has explored automatic event detection using player and ball trajectories, ball tracking also remains difficult to scale due to high infrastructural and operational costs. As a result, comprehensive data collection in soccer is largely confined to top-tier competitions, limiting the broader adoption of data-driven analysis in this domain. To address this challenge, this paper proposes PathCRF, a framework for detecting on-ball soccer events using only player tracking data. We model player trajectories as a fully connected dynamic graph and formulate event detection as the problem of selecting exactly one edge corresponding to the current possession state at each time step. To ensure logical consistency of the resulting edge sequence, we employ a Conditional Random Field (CRF) that forbids impossible transitions between consecutive edges. Both emission and transition scores dynamically computed from edge embeddings produced by a Set Attention-based backbone architecture. During inference, the most probable edge sequence is obtained via Viterbi decoding, and events such as ball controls or passes are detected whenever the selected edge changes between adjacent time steps. Experiments show that PathCRF produces accurate, logically consistent possession paths, enabling reliable downstream analyses while substantially reducing the need for manual event annotation. The source code is available at https://github.com/hyunsungkim-ds/pathcrf.git.

摘要（中文）: 尽管人工智能领域取得了最新进展，足球赛事数据的收集仍然严重依赖于劳动密集型的手工标注。虽然先前的研究已经探索了使用球员和球的轨迹进行自动事件检测，但由于高昂的基础设施和运营成本，球的跟踪仍然难以扩展。因此，足球赛事数据的全面收集主要局限于顶级联赛，限制了数据驱动分析在该领域更广泛的应用。为了解决这一挑战，本文提出PathCRF，一个仅使用球员跟踪数据来检测足球控球事件的框架。我们将球员轨迹建模为一个完全连接的动态图，并将事件检测表述为在每个时间步选择恰好一条对应于当前控球状态的边的难题。为了确保所生成边序列的逻辑一致性，我们采用条件随机场（CRF），禁止连续边之间不可能的转换。发射分数和转移分数都由基于集合注意力机制骨干架构生成的边嵌入动态计算。在推理过程中，通过维特比解码获得最可能的边序列，并且当选定的边在相邻时间步之间发生变化时，就可以检测到诸如控球或传球之类的事件。实验表明，PathCRF可以生成准确、逻辑上一致的控球路径，从而实现可靠的下游分析，同时大大减少了对人工标注的需要。源代码可在https://github.com/hyunsungkim-ds/pathcrf.git 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces PathCRF, a method for detecting soccer events using only player trajectories and Conditional Random Fields, eliminating the need for ball tracking and manual annotation.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为PathCRF的方法，该方法仅使用球员轨迹和条件随机场来检测足球事件，无需进行球跟踪和手动标注。

Authors: Hyunsung Kim, Kunhee Lee, Sangwoo Seo, Sang-Ki Ko, Jinsung Yoon, Chanyoung Park

Calibration and Evaluation of Car-Following Models for Autonomous Shuttles Using a Novel Multi-Criteria Framework

Abstract (English): Autonomous shuttles (AS) are fully autonomous transit vehicles with operating characteristics distinct from conventional autonomous vehicles (AV). Developing dedicated car-following models for AS is critical to understanding their traffic impacts; however, few studies have calibrated such models with field data. More advanced machine learning (ML) techniques have not yet been applied to AS trajectories, leaving the potential of ML for capturing AS dynamics unexplored and constraining the development of dedicated AS models. Furthermore, there is a lack of a unified framework for systematically evaluating and comparing the performance of car-following models to replicate real trajectories. Existing car-following studies often rely on disparate metrics, which limit reproducibility and performance comparability. This study addresses these gaps through two main contributions: (1) the calibration of a diverse set of car-following models using real-world AS trajectory data, including eight machine learning algorithms and two physics-based models; and (2) the introduction of a multi-criteria evaluation framework that integrates measures of prediction accuracy, trajectory stability, and statistical similarity, which provides a generalizable methodology for a systematic assessment of car-following models. Results indicated that the proposed calibrated XGBoost model achieved the best overall performance. Sequential model type, such as LSTM and CNN, captured long-term positional stability but were less responsive to short-term dynamics. LSTM and CNN captured long-term positional stability but were less responsive to short-term dynamics. Traditional models (IDM, ACC) and kernel methods showed lower accuracy and stability than most ML models tested.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶摆渡车（AS）是完全自动驾驶的交通工具，其运行特性与传统的自动驾驶汽车（AV）不同。开发专门的AS跟驰模型对于理解其交通影响至关重要；然而，很少有研究使用现场数据校准此类模型。更先进的机器学习（ML）技术尚未应用于AS轨迹，这使得ML在捕捉AS动态方面的潜力未被探索，并限制了专用AS模型的开发。此外，缺乏一个统一的框架来系统地评估和比较跟驰模型复制真实轨迹的性能。现有的跟驰研究通常依赖于不同的指标，这限制了可重复性和性能可比性。 本研究通过两个主要贡献来弥补这些差距：（1）使用真实世界的AS轨迹数据校准了一系列不同的跟驰模型，包括八种机器学习算法和两种基于物理的模型；以及（2）引入了一个多标准评估框架，该框架整合了预测精度、轨迹稳定性和统计相似性的度量标准，从而为系统评估跟驰模型提供了一种通用的方法。 结果表明，所提出的校准后的XGBoost模型实现了最佳的整体性能。诸如LSTM和CNN之类的序列模型类型能够捕捉到长期的位置稳定性，但对短期动态的响应较差。传统模型（IDM、ACC）和核方法显示出比大多数经过测试的ML模型更低的准确性和稳定性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a multi-criteria framework for evaluating car-following models for autonomous shuttles, comparing machine learning and physics-based models using real-world trajectory data and finding that XGBoost performed best.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个多标准框架，用于评估自动驾驶摆渡车的车辆跟随模型，使用真实轨迹数据比较机器学习和基于物理的模型，并发现 XGBoost 性能最佳。

Authors: Renan Favero, Lily Elefteriadou

Exploring Multiple High-Scoring Subspaces in Generative Flow Networks

Abstract (English): As a probabilistic sampling framework, Generative Flow Networks (GFlowNets) show strong potential for constructing complex combinatorial objects through the sequential composition of elementary components. However, existing GFlowNets often suffer from excessive exploration over vast state spaces, leading to over-sampling of low-reward regions and convergence to suboptimal distributions. Effectively biasing GFlowNets toward high-reward solutions remains a non-trivial challenge. In this paper, we propose CMAB-GFN, which integrates a combinatorial multi-armed bandit (CMAB) framework with GFlowNet policies. The CMAB component prunes low-quality actions, yielding compact high-scoring subspaces for exploration. Restricting GFNs to these compact high-scoring subspaces accelerates the discovery of high-value candidates, while the exploration of different subspaces ensures that diversity is not sacrificed. Experimental results on multiple tasks demonstrate that CMAB-GFN generates higher-reward candidates than existing approaches.

摘要（中文）: 作为一种概率采样框架，生成式流网络 (GFlowNets) 在通过基本组件的顺序组合构建复杂组合对象方面显示出强大的潜力。然而，现有的 GFlowNets 常常由于在广阔的状态空间中过度探索而受到影响，导致对低奖励区域的过度采样以及收敛到次优分布。有效地引导 GFlowNets 倾向于高奖励解决方案仍然是一个具有挑战性的问题。在本文中，我们提出了 CMAB-GFN，它将组合多臂老虎机 (CMAB) 框架与 GFlowNet 策略相结合。CMAB 组件剪枝低质量动作，从而产生用于探索的紧凑型高分子空间。将 GFN 限制在这些紧凑型高分子空间中加速了高价值候选者的发现，同时对不同子空间的探索确保了多样性不会被牺牲。在多个任务上的实验结果表明，CMAB-GFN 生成的候选者比现有方法具有更高的奖励。

TLDR: The paper introduces CMAB-GFN, a method integrating combinatorial multi-armed bandits with Generative Flow Networks to prune low-quality actions, accelerating the discovery of high-reward solutions in complex combinatorial spaces and maintaining diversity.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CMAB-GFN，这是一种将组合多臂老虎机与生成流网络相结合的方法，用于剪除低质量动作，加速在复杂组合空间中发现高回报解决方案，并保持多样性。

Authors: Xuan Yu, Xu Wang, Rui Zhu, Yudong Zhang, Yang Wang

Min-Sum Uniform Coverage Problem by Autonomous Mobile Robots

Abstract (English): We study the \textit{min-sum uniform coverage} problem for a swarm of $n$ mobile robots on a given finite line segment and on a circle having finite positive radius, where the circle is given as an input. The robots must coordinate their movements to reach a uniformly spaced configuration that minimizes the total distance traveled by all robots. The robots are autonomous, anonymous, identical, and homogeneous, and operate under the \textit{Look-Compute-Move} (LCM) model with \textit{non-rigid} motion controlled by a fair asynchronous scheduler. They are oblivious and silent, possessing neither persistent memory nor a means of explicit communication. In the \textbf{line-segment setting}, the \textit{min-sum uniform coverage} problem requires placing the robots at uniformly spaced points along the segment so as to minimize the total distance traveled by all robots. In the \textbf{circle setting} for this problem, the robots have to arrange themselves uniformly around the given circle to form a regular $n$-gon. There is no fixed orientation or designated starting vertex, and the goal is to minimize the total distance traveled by all the robots. We present a deterministic distributed algorithm that achieves uniform coverage in the line-segment setting with minimum total movement cost. For the circle setting, we characterize all initial configurations for which the \textit{min-sum uniform coverage} problem is deterministically unsolvable under the considered robot model. For all the other remaining configurations, we provide a deterministic distributed algorithm that achieves uniform coverage while minimizing the total distance traveled. These results characterize the deterministic solvability of min-sum coverage for oblivious robots and achieve optimal cost whenever solvable.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了一群 $n$ 个移动机器人在给定有限线段和具有有限正半径的圆上的\textit{最小和均匀覆盖}问题，其中圆作为输入给出。机器人必须协调它们的运动以达到均匀间隔的配置，从而最小化所有机器人行进的总距离。机器人是自主的、匿名的、相同的和同质的，并在一个由公平的异步调度器控制的具有\textit{非刚性}运动的\textit{观察-计算-移动} (LCM) 模型下运行。它们是无记忆和静默的，既没有持久性内存，也没有显式通信的手段。在\textbf{线段设定}中，\textit{最小和均匀覆盖}问题要求将机器人放置在线段上均匀间隔的点处，以最小化所有机器人行进的总距离。在此问题的\textbf{圆形设定}中，机器人必须围绕给定的圆均匀排列，形成一个正 $n$ 边形。没有固定的方向或指定的起始顶点，目标是最小化所有机器人行进的总距离。我们提出了一种确定性的分布式算法，该算法在线段设定中以最小的总移动成本实现均匀覆盖。对于圆形设定，我们描述了在此问题中，在所考虑的机器人模型下，\textit{最小和均匀覆盖}问题是确定性不可解的所有初始配置。对于所有剩余的其他配置，我们提供了一种确定性的分布式算法，该算法在最小化行进总距离的同时实现均匀覆盖。这些结果表征了无记忆机器人的最小和覆盖的确定性可解性，并在可解的情况下实现最优成本。

TLDR: This paper presents deterministic distributed algorithms for achieving min-sum uniform coverage with a swarm of oblivious robots on a line segment and a circle, characterizing solvability and achieving optimal cost where possible.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种确定性的分布式算法，用于在一群无记忆机器人在线段和圆上实现最小和均匀覆盖，表征了可解性，并在可能的情况下实现了最优成本。

Authors: Animesh Maiti, Abhinav Chakraborty, Bibhuti Das, Subhash Bhagat, Krishnendu Mukhopadhyaya

KAN-FIF: Spline-Parameterized Lightweight Physics-based Tropical Cyclone Estimation on Meteorological Satellite

Abstract (English): Tropical cyclones (TC) are among the most destructive natural disasters, causing catastrophic damage to coastal regions through extreme winds, heavy rainfall, and storm surges. Timely monitoring of tropical cyclones is crucial for reducing loss of life and property, yet it is hindered by the computational inefficiency and high parameter counts of existing methods on resource-constrained edge devices. Current physics-guided models suffer from linear feature interactions that fail to capture high-order polynomial relationships between TC attributes, leading to inflated model sizes and hardware incompatibility. To overcome these challenges, this study introduces the Kolmogorov-Arnold Network-based Feature Interaction Framework (KAN-FIF), a lightweight multimodal architecture that integrates MLP and CNN layers with spline-parameterized KAN layers. For Maximum Sustained Wind (MSW) prediction, experiments demonstrate that the KAN-FIF framework achieves a $94.8\%$ reduction in parameters (0.99MB vs 19MB) and $68.7\%$ faster inference per sample (2.3ms vs 7.35ms) compared to baseline model Phy-CoCo, while maintaining superior accuracy with $32.5\%$ lower MAE. The offline deployment experiment of the FY-4 series meteorological satellite processor on the Qingyun-1000 development board achieved a 14.41ms per-sample inference latency with the KAN-FIF framework, demonstrating promising feasibility for operational TC monitoring and extending deployability to edge-device AI applications. The code is released at https://github.com/Jinglin-Zhang/KAN-FIF.

摘要（中文）: 热带气旋是最具破坏力的自然灾害之一，通过极端大风、强降雨和风暴潮对沿海地区造成灾难性破坏。及时监测热带气旋对于减少生命和财产损失至关重要，但现有方法在资源受限的边缘设备上的计算效率低下和参数量巨大阻碍了这一目标的实现。目前基于物理机制的模型存在线性特征交互的问题，无法捕获热带气旋属性之间的高阶多项式关系，从而导致模型尺寸膨胀和硬件不兼容。为了克服这些挑战，本研究提出了一种基于柯尔莫哥洛夫-阿诺德网络(KAN)的特征交互框架(KAN-FIF)，这是一种轻量级的多模态架构，将MLP和CNN层与样条参数化的KAN层集成在一起。对于最大持续风速(MSW)预测，实验表明，与基线模型Phy-CoCo相比，KAN-FIF框架在保持优异精度的同时，参数量减少了94.8%（0.99MB vs 19MB），每个样本的推理速度提高了68.7%（2.3ms vs 7.35ms），平均绝对误差(MAE)降低了32.5%。在青云-1000开发板上对风云四号系列气象卫星处理器进行的离线部署实验表明，使用KAN-FIF框架的单样本推理延迟为14.41ms，证明了其在业务化热带气旋监测中的可行性，并将可部署性扩展到边缘设备AI应用。相关代码已在https://github.com/Jinglin-Zhang/KAN-FIF 上发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces KAN-FIF, a lightweight neural network architecture using spline-parameterized KAN layers for efficient and accurate tropical cyclone monitoring on edge devices, achieving significant parameter reduction and faster inference compared to existing physics-guided models.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 KAN-FIF，一种轻量级的神经网络架构，使用样条参数化的 KAN 层，用于边缘设备上高效准确的热带气旋监测，与现有的物理引导模型相比，实现了显著的参数减少和更快的推理速度。

Authors: Jiakang Shen, Qinghui Chen, Runtong Wang, Chenrui Xu, Jinglin Zhang, Cong Bai, Feng Zhang

Egocentric Gaze Estimation via Neck-Mounted Camera

Abstract (English): This paper introduces neck-mounted view gaze estimation, a new task that estimates user gaze from the neck-mounted camera perspective. Prior work on egocentric gaze estimation, which predicts device wearer's gaze location within the camera's field of view, mainly focuses on head-mounted cameras while alternative viewpoints remain underexplored. To bridge this gap, we collect the first dataset for this task, consisting of approximately 4 hours of video collected from 8 participants during everyday activities. We evaluate a transformer-based gaze estimation model, GLC, on the new dataset and propose two extensions: an auxiliary gaze out-of-bound classification task and a multi-view co-learning approach that jointly trains head-view and neck-view models using a geometry-aware auxiliary loss. Experimental results show that incorporating gaze out-of-bound classification improves performance over standard fine-tuning, while the co-learning approach does not yield gains. We further analyze these results and discuss implications for neck-mounted gaze estimation.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了颈部视角注视点估计，这是一项新的任务，旨在从颈部安装的摄像机视角估计用户注视点。以往关于以自我为中心的注视点估计的研究主要集中于头戴式摄像机，此类研究预测设备佩戴者在摄像机视野内的注视位置，而其他视角仍未得到充分探索。为了弥补这一差距，我们收集了该任务的首个数据集，其中包含 8 名参与者在日常活动中收集的约 4 小时的视频。我们在新的数据集上评估了一个基于 Transformer 的注视点估计模型，GLC，并提出了两个扩展：一个辅助的注视点超出边界分类任务和一个多视角协同学习方法，该方法使用几何感知的辅助损失联合训练头部视角和颈部视角的模型。实验结果表明，结合注视点超出边界分类可以提高优于标准微调的性能，而协同学习方法没有产生增益。我们进一步分析了这些结果并讨论了颈部视角注视点估计的意义。

TLDR: The paper introduces a new egocentric gaze estimation task using a neck-mounted camera, provides a new dataset, and evaluates a transformer-based model with two proposed extensions. The out-of-bound classification improves performance.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种使用颈部摄像头进行以自我为中心的注视估计的新任务，提供了一个新的数据集，并评估了一个基于transformer的模型以及两个扩展。 越界分类提高了性能。

Authors: Haoyu Huang, Yoichi Sato

HairWeaver: Few-Shot Photorealistic Hair Motion Synthesis with Sim-to-Real Guided Video Diffusion

Abstract (English): We present HairWeaver, a diffusion-based pipeline that animates a single human image with realistic and expressive hair dynamics. While existing methods successfully control body pose, they lack specific control over hair, and as a result, fail to capture the intricate hair motions, resulting in stiff and unrealistic animations. HairWeaver overcomes this limitation using two specialized modules: a Motion-Context-LoRA to integrate motion conditions and a Sim2Real-Domain-LoRA to preserve the subject's photoreal appearance across different data domains. These lightweight components are designed to guide a video diffusion backbone while maintaining its core generative capabilities. By training on a specialized dataset of dynamic human motion generated from a CG simulator, HairWeaver affords fine control over hair motion and ultimately learns to produce highly realistic hair that responds naturally to movement. Comprehensive evaluations demonstrate that our approach sets a new state of the art, producing lifelike human hair animations with dynamic details.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出 HairWeaver，一种基于扩散模型的流程，能够以逼真且富有表现力的头发动态来动画化单个人物图像。 虽然现有的方法成功控制了身体姿态，但它们缺乏对头发的精细控制，因此无法捕捉到复杂的头发运动，从而产生僵硬且不真实的动画。 HairWeaver 通过两个专门的模块克服了这一限制：一个用于整合运动条件的运动上下文 LoRA (Motion-Context-LoRA) 和一个用于在不同数据域中保持主体逼真外观的 Sim2Real 域 LoRA (Sim2Real-Domain-LoRA)。 这些轻量级组件旨在引导视频扩散骨干网络，同时保持其核心生成能力。 通过在从 CG 模拟器生成的动态人体运动专业数据集上进行训练，HairWeaver 能对头发运动进行精细控制，并最终学会生成对运动做出自然反应的高度逼真的头发。 全面的评估表明，我们的方法设定了新的技术水平，能够产生具有动态细节的逼真的人类头发动画。

TLDR: HairWeaver is a video diffusion pipeline that animates a single human image with realistic hair dynamics by using Motion-Context-LoRA and Sim2Real-Domain-LoRA to guide the diffusion process, trained on CG data.

简要说明: HairWeaver是一个视频扩散流程，通过使用Motion-Context-LoRA和Sim2Real-Domain-LoRA来引导扩散过程，从而赋予单个人物图像逼真的头发动态效果，并在CG数据上进行训练。

Authors: Di Chang, Ji Hou, Aljaz Bozic, Assaf Neuberger, Felix Juefei-Xu, Olivier Maury, Gene Wei-Chin Lin, Tuur Stuyck, Doug Roble, Mohammad Soleymani, Stephane Grabli

Assessing Low Back Movement with Motion Tape Sensor Data Through Deep Learning

Abstract (English): Back pain is a pervasive issue affecting a significant portion of the population, often worsened by certain movements of the lower back. Assessing these movements is important for helping clinicians prescribe appropriate physical therapy. However, it can be difficult to monitor patients' movements remotely outside the clinic. High-fidelity data from motion capture sensors can be used to classify different movements, but these sensors are costly and impractical for use in free-living environments. Motion Tape (MT), a new fabric-based wearable sensor, addresses these issues by being low cost and portable. Despite these advantages, novelty and variability in sensor stability make the MT dataset small scale and inherent to noise. In this work, we propose the Motion-Tape Augmentation Inference Model (MT-AIM), a deep learning classification pipeline trained on MT data. In order to address the challenges of limited sample size and noise present within the MT dataset, MT-AIM leverages conditional generative models to generate synthetic MT data of a desired movement, as well as predicting joint kinematics as additional features. This combination of synthetic data generation and feature augmentation enables MT-AIM to achieve state-of-the-art accuracy in classifying lower back movements, bridging the gap between physiological sensing and movement analysis.

摘要（中文）: 腰背疼痛是一个普遍存在的问题，影响着相当一部分人群，某些腰部动作常会加剧疼痛。评估这些动作对于帮助临床医生开出合适的物理治疗方案至关重要。然而，在诊所以外远程监测患者的动作可能比较困难。来自动作捕捉传感器的高保真数据可以用于对不同的动作进行分类，但这些传感器成本高昂且不适合在自由生活环境中使用。运动胶带（MT）是一种新型的基于织物的可穿戴传感器，它通过低成本和便携性解决了这些问题。尽管有这些优点，但传感器的稳定性的新颖性和可变性导致MT数据集规模较小且固有噪声。在这项工作中，我们提出了运动胶带增强推理模型（MT-AIM），这是一个基于MT数据训练的深度学习分类管道。为了应对MT数据集中存在的样本量有限和噪声的挑战，MT-AIM利用条件生成模型来生成所需动作的合成MT数据，并预测关节运动学作为附加特征。合成数据生成和特征增强的结合使MT-AIM能够在腰部动作分类中实现最先进的准确性，从而弥合了生理传感和运动分析之间的差距。

TLDR: This paper introduces MT-AIM, a deep learning pipeline that uses conditional generative models to augment noisy data from a new wearable motion sensor (Motion Tape) for accurate classification of lower back movements.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种深度学习管道MT-AIM，它使用条件生成模型来增强来自新型可穿戴运动传感器（Motion Tape）的噪声数据，从而准确分类下背部运动。

Authors: Jared Levy, Aarti Lalwani, Elijah Wyckoff, Kenneth J. Loh, Sara P. Gombatto, Rose Yu, Emilia Farcas

Data-Driven Trajectory Imputation for Vessel Mobility Analysis

Abstract (English): Modeling vessel activity at sea is critical for a wide range of applications, including route planning, transportation logistics, maritime safety, and environmental monitoring. Over the past two decades, the Automatic Identification System (AIS) has enabled real-time monitoring of hundreds of thousands of vessels, generating huge amounts of data daily. One major challenge in using AIS data is the presence of large gaps in vessel trajectories, often caused by coverage limitations or intentional transmission interruptions. These gaps can significantly degrade data quality, resulting in inaccurate or incomplete analysis. State-of-the-art imputation approaches have mainly been devised to tackle gaps in vehicle trajectories, even when the underlying road network is not considered. But the motion patterns of sailing vessels differ substantially, e.g., smooth turns, maneuvering near ports, or navigating in adverse weather conditions. In this application paper, we propose HABIT, a lightweight, configurable H3 Aggregation-Based Imputation framework for vessel Trajectories. This data-driven framework provides a valuable means to impute missing trajectory segments by extracting, analyzing, and indexing motion patterns from historical AIS data. Our empirical study over AIS data across various timeframes, densities, and vessel types reveals that HABIT produces maritime trajectory imputations performing comparably to baseline methods in terms of accuracy, while performing better in terms of latency while accounting for vessel characteristics and their motion patterns.

摘要（中文）: 对海上船舶活动进行建模对于众多应用至关重要，包括航线规划、运输物流、海事安全和环境监测。过去二十年中，船舶自动识别系统 (AIS) 实现了对数十万艘船舶的实时监控，每天生成海量数据。 使用 AIS 数据的主要挑战之一是船舶轨迹中存在大量缺口，这通常由覆盖范围限制或有意传输中断引起。这些缺口会显著降低数据质量，导致不准确或不完整的分析。目前最先进的插补方法主要用于解决车辆轨迹中的缺口，即使不考虑底层路网。但航行船舶的运动模式差异显著，例如，平稳转向、港口附近的操控或在恶劣天气条件下的航行。 在这篇应用论文中，我们提出了 HABIT，一个轻量级、可配置的基于 H3 聚合的船舶轨迹插补框架。这种数据驱动框架通过提取、分析和索引历史 AIS 数据中的运动模式，为填补缺失轨迹段提供了有效手段。 我们对不同时间范围、密度和船舶类型的 AIS 数据进行的实证研究表明，HABIT 在准确性方面产生的海洋轨迹插补与基线方法相比具有可比性，但在考虑船舶特性及其运动模式的同时，在延迟方面表现更好。

TLDR: The paper introduces HABIT, a data-driven framework for imputing missing segments in vessel trajectories using historical AIS data, achieving comparable accuracy to baselines with improved latency and consideration for vessel characteristics.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为HABIT的数据驱动框架，用于使用历史AIS数据填补船舶轨迹中的缺失片段，在准确性方面与基线方法相当，同时提高了延迟，并考虑了船舶特征。

Authors: Giannis Spiliopoulos, Alexandros Troupiotis-Kapeliaris, Kostas Patroumpas, Nikolaos Liapis, Dimitrios Skoutas, Dimitris Zissis, Nikos Bikakis

Explainable Machine-Learning based Detection of Knee Injuries in Runners

Abstract (English): Running is a widely practiced activity but shows a high incidence of knee injuries, especially Patellofemoral Pain Syndrome (PFPS) and Iliotibial Band Syndrome (ITBS). Identifying gait patterns linked to these injuries can improve clinical decision-making, which requires precise systems capable of capturing and analyzing temporal kinematic data. This study uses optical motion capture systems to enhance detection of injury-related running patterns. We analyze a public dataset of 839 treadmill recordings from healthy and injured runners to evaluate how effectively these systems capture dynamic parameters relevant to injury classification. The focus is on the stance phase, using joint and segment angle time series and discrete point values. Three classification tasks are addressed: healthy vs. injured, healthy vs. PFPS, and healthy vs. ITBS. We examine different feature spaces, from traditional point-based metrics to full stance-phase time series and hybrid representations. Multiple models are tested, including classical algorithms (K-Nearest Neighbors, Gaussian Processes, Decision Trees) and deep learning architectures (CNNs, LSTMs). Performance is evaluated with accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score. Explainability tools such as Shapley values, saliency maps, and Grad-CAM are used to interpret model behavior. Results show that combining time series with point values substantially improves detection. Deep learning models outperform classical ones, with CNNs achieving the highest accuracy: 77.9% for PFPS, 73.8% for ITBS, and 71.43% for the combined injury class. These findings highlight the potential of motion capture systems coupled with advanced machine learning to identify knee injury-related running patterns.

摘要（中文）: 跑步是一项广泛进行的活动，但膝关节损伤的发生率很高，特别是髌股关节疼痛综合征 (PFPS) 和髂胫束综合征 (ITBS)。 识别与这些损伤相关的步态模式可以改善临床决策，这需要能够捕获和分析时间运动学数据的精确系统。 本研究利用光学运动捕捉系统来增强对与损伤相关的跑步模式的检测。我们分析了一个包含来自健康和受伤跑者的839个跑步机记录的公共数据集，以评估这些系统捕捉与损伤分类相关的动态参数的有效性。重点关注站立相，使用关节和节段角度时间序列以及离散点值。 研究解决了三个分类任务：健康 vs. 受伤、健康 vs. PFPS 以及健康 vs. ITBS。我们考察了不同的特征空间，从传统的基于点的指标到完整的站立相时间序列以及混合表示。测试了多种模型，包括经典算法（K近邻、高斯过程、决策树）和深度学习架构（CNN、LSTM）。 使用准确率、精确率、召回率和 F1 分数评估性能。 使用 Shapley 值、显著性图和 Grad-CAM 等可解释性工具来解释模型行为。结果表明，将时间序列与点值相结合可显着提高检测率。深度学习模型优于经典模型，其中 CNN 实现了最高的准确率：PFPS 为 77.9%，ITBS 为 73.8%，综合损伤类别为 71.43%。 这些发现强调了运动捕捉系统与先进机器学习相结合，以识别与膝关节损伤相关的跑步模式的潜力。

TLDR: This paper uses machine learning and explainability techniques to detect knee injuries (PFPS and ITBS) in runners using motion capture data, achieving up to 77.9% accuracy with CNNs.

简要说明: 本文使用机器学习和可解释性技术，通过运动捕捉数据检测跑步者膝盖损伤（髌股关节疼痛综合征和髂胫束综合征），CNNs 实现了高达 77.9% 的准确率。
